## рЯЖХ ORDER-AWARE COVERAGE (FAST-FOLLOW #1 to the burn engine) вАФ PM RULINGS 2026-06-11 (pre-build; render-only, NO mig)
Kouros flagged a real inconsistency: the seasonal headline `semaines_stock` is pure `physique√Јburn` and IGNORES the committed open-order book, while `live_futur` (=physiqueвИТopen_total) already encodes it. PROOF SKU **ALTF**: physique=40, rythme_base(L)=2.4/wk вЖТ semaines=14.4, BUT 45 units on the open book (overdue/near 30+6+6 + a 3 due 07-03) вЖТ live_futur=вИТ5 (survendu). 14.4 is arithmetically fine but operationally blind. **DECISION (Kouros): order-aware coverage вАФ the forward sim subtracts committed open orders at their due dates FIRST, then burns the rest at the seasonal rate.** Reconciles `semaines_stock` with `live_futur`. RENDER-TIME ONLY (orders already queried Step 7) вАФ NO migration.
- **RULING Q1 вАФ RECONCILIATION = `max()`, RULED.** Per forward week: `demand[week] = max(L√ЧS[week], open_orders[week])`. Adding double-counts (history `L√ЧS` is already mostly B2B orders; the open book is the *realization* of that same demand). `max()` = take the better-informed estimate per week: a big committed order dominates its week; an order-free week still burns the seasonal baseline. **REJECTED "orders-replace-forecast-for-ordered-weeks, baseline-for-the-rest"** вАФ a small order in a high-baseline peak week would UNDER-burn (false runway = the dangerous direction). Overdue + current-ISO-week orders FOLD into forward-week-1 (mirrors live_futur treating the whole open book as immediately-committed). **GUARD: the fractional-stockout denominator (`($h-1)+$stock/$forecast`) must use the reconciled `demand[week]`, not raw L√ЧS вАФ apply `max()` INSIDE the loop before the `$stock<=$forecast` test.**
- **RULING Q2 вАФ SINGLE BURN PATH = CONFIRMED, with one HARD invariant.** Order-aware logic lives INSIDE `sb_forward_weeks()` (the lone sim consumer) вАФ it gains ONE param `array $openByWeek` passed in; the runway derivation stays single. The bucketed open-orders query (Step 8) **MUST mirror the live_futur query (Step 7, fg-stock.php:558-567) EXACTLY**: same `FROM ord_order_lines l JOIN ord_orders o ON o.id=l.order_id_fk`, same `WHERE o.status NOT IN ('shipped','cancelled')`, **NO upper date bound** (live_futur subtracts the ENTIRE open book). **HARD INVARIANT / build-time assertion: ќ£(openByWeek across all buckets per SKU) == that SKU's `open_total_qty` from Step 7.** Ideally derive both from ONE fetch so they can't drift. **AXIS: bucket by weeks-from-today (`FLOOR(DATEDIFF(requested_date,today)/7)` clamped вЙ•0 for overdue/current), NOT YEARWEEK-of-year** вАФ the sim loops by horizon offset `$h`, so the PHP bucket the sim consumes must be the `$h` axis (SQL may still compute YEARWEEK, convert to offset before feeding the sim).
- **RULING Q3 вАФ MEANING SHIFT = SAFE, no downstream breaks (every consumer traced).** `semaines_stock` shifts from 'burn-runway on physical stock' вЖТ 'runway accounting for committed orders + burn'. All consumers take it as opaque `float|null`; a smaller number simply lands a lower (more urgent) health tier = INTENDED. 6-tier `exp_classify_*` (expeditions.php:2577-2624, WEEKS_CRITICAL=1/LOW=3/HIGH=10), `flag_low_stock` (fg-stock.php:677 `<2.0 && physique>0`), `exp_fmt_semaines`, gauge bars вАФ ALL unchanged. **рЯФі THE ONE CARE POINT: tier 6 `sans_rotation` = `physique>0 && semaines_stock===null` means 'no burn data / EOL', NOT 'order-depleted'. An order-aware stockout in week 1 must return a small POSITIVE float (or 0), NEVER null. ALTF вЖТ ~0 weeks (critique), NOT sans_rotation. Keep null reserved strictly for no-level/EOL (sb_forward_weeks already returns positive on stockout вАФ preserve).** Divergence with live_futur is REDUCED not raised (that's the deliverable): post-change both encode order-awareness вЖТ can no longer contradict (one survendu / other 14wk). Invariant: live_futur<0 вЗТ semainesвЙ§~0-1wk (week-1 bucket carries all overdue/current orders > physique). Bands/legend/`sans rotation` logic UNCHANGED вАФ only the number. COPY tweak (ui, not logic): legend/drill may note "couverture (stock вИТ commandes engag√©es)" so operator reads it as order-aware.
- **RULING Q4 вАФ DRILLDOWN = EXTEND the existing `exp-stock-drill` with a THIRD face "Couverture". NOT a modal, NOT the exp-hist client panel.** The `?view=stock` per-SKU drill is ALREADY a `role=tablist` segmented toggle (commit `711905c` 2026-06-10): Face "Stock" + Face "Activit√©", delegated `button[data-evt-tab]` scoped `closest('.exp-stock-drill')` + `resetDrillFace()` on collapse. **Add a 3rd tab/face.** Modals are reserved for the Commandes view (`exp-stock-detail-modal`, opened from expeditions.js) вАФ a modal here forks the idiom (UI-level divergence smell). The `exp-hist-*` panel is per-CLIENT (wrong grain). The "Couverture" face carries Kouros's breakdown: physique+flows, open-order book by date (reuse the already-loaded data, no new query), live_futur, rythme de base L + lumpiness note (Q5), the family seasonal curve, and the **week-by-week projection table** (demand=max(L√ЧS,orders) ¬Ј running stock ¬Ј week-hits-0 ¬Ј status) вАФ the high-value artifact making `max()` legible. Feed via the established `window.EXP_*` page-wide injection (sim emits an optional per-week trace), NO AJAX/endpoint (mirrors "Activit√© r√©cente" + the risk modal). A11y: real `<button role=tab>`/`role=tabpanel`, `resetDrillFace()` resets across all 3 faces on every collapse path, arrow-nav extends to 3.
- **RULING Q5 вАФ CROSTON'S STAYS FAST-FOLLOW (confirmed). SHOW lumpiness, don't change level math.** Kouros chose 'Order-aware' not 'Both' вЖТ sporadique/Croston's (ADI>1.32) stays deferred. The "Couverture" face SHOWS `nonzero_weeks/53` + recent-spike note as DIAGNOSTIC context (e.g. "17/53 sem. avec ventes ¬Ј pic r√©cent"), NOT a recomputed L. **Order-awareness is the load-bearing fix for ALTF, not Croston's** вАФ with the 45 committed units folded in, ALTF reads ~0wk regardless of whether L=2.4 or Croston's-corrected; the lumpy L misreading the spike is 2nd-order. Folding Croston's in now = two level-math paths in one build = scope-creep against single-burn-path discipline. Keep it a clean separate fast-follow.
- **VERDICT + SEQUENCING:** architecturally sound; render-time-only, NO migration (orders already queried). Single-path integrity hinges on ONE query matching live_futur exactly + the ќ£(buckets)==open_total_qty assertion. Safe in one arc. No `ref_pages` change вЖТ NO tour-steward dispatch.
- **EQUIP: sql + coder + ui + webapp-testing.** sql = bucketed open-orders query (mirror Step 7 filter/join exactly) + ќ£-reconciliation EXPLAIN/dry-run; coder = `sb_forward_weeks()` order-aware param + Step 8 wiring + per-week trace emission; ui = the 3rd "Couverture" drill face (mirror `711905c` tablist idiom, inline NOT modal) + projection table + lumpiness note; webapp-testing = read-only `?view=stock` prod smoke (ALTF reads survendu/~0, 3rd face opens, projection renders, no 500).

## вЬЕ ORDER-AWARE COVERAGE (FAST-FOLLOW #1) вАФ SHIPPED + LIVE on prod 2026-06-11
**Built, deployed, verified-live on `?view=stock`. Implements EVERY ruling Q1-Q5 above вАФ no architecture deviation. Render-only, NO migration (orders already queried Step 7), HEAD unchanged.**
- **FUNCTION REFACTOR (note for future refs):** `sb_forward_weeks()` вЖТ **`sb_forward_sim()`** returning `{weeks, trace}` (was scalar weeks). **Back-compat wrapper kept** under the old name. So the lone sim consumer is now `sb_forward_sim` in `app/seasonal-burn.php`; the per-week `trace` is what feeds the Couverture projection table.
- **Q1 max() вАФ IMPLEMENTED:** per forward week `demand = max(L√Чidx, open_orders[h])`; overdue + current-ISO-week orders fold into `h=1` (mirrors live_futur's whole-book-immediate treatment). Order-depleted stockout returns **~0, never null** (Q3 care-point honored вАФ EOL stays the ONLY null).
- **Q2 single path + HARD INVARIANT вАФ PASSES:** order-awareness lives inside the one sim; bucketed open-orders query **mirrors the Step-7 `live_futur` filter EXACTLY**; bucketed by **weeks-from-today offset** (`h=1` for overdue/current), not yearweek-of-year. **Build-assert `ќ£(openByWeek) == open_total_qty` PASSES 32/32 SKUs, no warnings.**
- **Q3 meaning-shift вАФ clean:** normal SKUs (no open orders) byte-unchanged вАФ `max()` is a no-op without orders, so all downstream tiers/gauges/`flag_low_stock`/`sans_rotation` untouched. 54/54 rows carry `couverture`.
- **Q4 3rd "Couverture" face вАФ SHIPPED on the existing `exp-stock-drill` tablist** (server-rendered inline, NO modal/AJAX вАФ Q4 honored); `fg_stock_compute` emits a per-SKU `couverture` drill payload (physique+flows, open_book, live_futur, rythme_base, lumpiness, recent_spike, seasonal now/peak, projection trace, status). Week-by-week projection table with **stockout-row highlight** (colour+border+glyph). **Fixed a pre-existing tab-switcher JS bug** (hardcoded ternary mis-routed any 3rd tab вЖТ generic regex) вАФ was latent before this build added the 3rd face.
- **Q5 Croston's вАФ stays fast-follow:** lumpiness shown as DIAGNOSTIC only, level math unchanged. Confirmed.
- **LIVE VERIFICATION:** **ALTF 14.4 вЖТ 1.86 wk** (trace shows the 42u 20/06 order landing at h2 вЖТ stock вИТ5.76 survendu вАФ the exact reconciliation with live_futur this build exists to deliver); normal SKUs byte-identical (max() no-op); 54/54 rows carry couverture; 0 errors / 0 assertion-warnings; `php -l` clean on all touched files.
- **FILES DEPLOYED, UNCOMMITTED:** `app/seasonal-burn.php`, `app/fg-stock.php` (cleanly this build's). `public/modules/expeditions.php`, `public/css/expeditions.css`, `public/js/expeditions-stock.js` **ENTANGLED with a parallel session's uncommitted edits** in the same 3 files (same shared-clone entanglement as the morning burn-engine build) вАФ **commit by PATHSPEC, do NOT sweep the parallel hunks.** `seasonal-burn.php` + `fg-stock.php` commit cleanly on their own.

## рЯЖХ SEMAINES-RESTANTES / BURN-RATE вАФ SCOPE UPGRADED to FORWARD SEASONAL ENGINE (S&OP expert ruling) вАФ PM ARCHITECTURE RULING 2026-06-11 (вЬЕ NOW BUILT вАФ see SHIPPED block above)
Kouros uploaded weekly sales per SKU back to 2021 вЖТ wants real "semaines restantes de stock" on `?view=stock`. **The flat trailing-24mo-mean swap is SUPERSEDED.** Kouros consulted an industry S&OP/demand-planning expert; the locked model is a **forward, seasonal, family-pooled depletion engine**: family multiplicative seasonal index `S[family][1..52]`, per-SKU deseasonalized EW level `L[sku]` (ќї=0.95, half-life ~13wk), forward week-by-week depletion sim charging `L√ЧS[isoweek]`, status chip (normal/provisoire/sporadique-Croston/EOL), display triad. Full locked model in the consult message of record.
- **KEY FINDING (still holds) вАФ this is a VELOCITY-SOURCE SWAP at the seam, not a new surface.** `semaines_stock` ALREADY EXISTS in `app/fg-stock.php` (Step 8, ~L586), wired into `?view=stock`: 6-tier health (`WEEKS_CRITICAL=1`/`WEEKS_LOW=3`/`WEEKS_HIGH=10`, `exp_classify_*` ~L2447-2494), `exp_fmt_semaines()` "вИЮ" formatter ~L3852, progress bars ~L4278, `flag_low_stock`. Today velocity = trailing-56-day flat mean off `inv_sales_bc`+`inv_sales_order_lines`. The new engine REPLACES the Step-8 numerator/window with `L√ЧS` forward sim; `physique` numerator + all downstream classification/render UNCHANGED (thresholds may need re-tuning to forward semantics вАФ fast-follow).
- **DATA SOURCE = `inv_sales_ledger`** (live-verified 2026-06-11): `posting_date` DATE (idx `idx_sl_posting`), `sku_id_fk` INT UNSIGNED (idx `idx_sl_sku`), `qty_signed`/`qty_invoiced` DECIMAL(14,4) SKU units, `hl_resolved`, `doc_type` ENUM(shipment/invoice/credit/return_receipt). **2021-01-05вЖТ2026-06-09, 44,164 rows, 133 SKUs.** вЪ†пЄП **25% NULL `sku_id_fk`** (unresolved sku_code_raw) вАФ coverage-gap surface, NEVER drop. вЪ†пЄП **NO composite (sku_id_fk, posting_date) index вАФ only two single-col idxs; mig must add the covering composite** for the per-SKU 52wk pull + the cron's full decomposition.
- **рЯФі FAMILY POOLING DATA TRUTH (live-verified вАФ the expert model assumed `recipe_id_fk`; THE DB DOES NOT HAVE IT):** `inv_sales_ledger` has **NO `recipe_id_fk`** (only `sku_id_fk`). `ref_skus` has **NO `recipe_id_fk` either вАФ the family key is `ref_skus.recipe_id` (INT UNSIGNED, NULLable)**. So **family = `ref_skus.recipe_id`, reached by JOIN `inv_sales_ledger.sku_id_fk вЖТ ref_skus.id вЖТ recipe_id`** (NOT a direct column, NOT a string). **25 distinct recipe families** in the resolved ledger. **NULL-`recipe_id` rows: 6/182 active SKUs + 146 ledger rows** вЖТ these CANNOT pool to a family вЖТ **fall back to the GLOBAL brewery seasonal curve** (same path as <2yr-history families). The 25% NULL-`sku_id_fk` rows can't even resolve a SKU вЖТ excluded from both S and L (coverage gap, surfaced not dropped).
- **physique = `fg_stock_compute()`** вАФ already the numerator (`$physique`). No change.

### A. CRON + CACHE TABLE вАФ BLESSED (revising the earlier "no cron / materialize only if slow")
The seasonal index `S` genuinely needs precompute: 52√Чfamily ratio-to-centered-MA decomposition over 44k rows, STABLE week-to-week, NOT render-cheap. **BLESS a new cache table + weekly cron. This stays SINGLE-HOMED = ONE burn path:** `S` is materialized by the cron, `L` is computed at render, the forward sim (render) consumes both вАФ there is exactly one velocity derivation, no parallel store. Divergence-clean because S is a *materialized projection* of `inv_sales_ledger` (the SoT), recomputed wholesale each cron run (idempotent overwrite вАФ no incremental drift), never hand-edited, never a second authority. This is the SAME materialization pattern already blessed for the daily-recap perf index вАФ heavy stable analytic precomputed, render reads cache.
- **Table name (house convention `kpi_` prefix for materialized analytic caches): `kpi_sku_seasonal_index`.** Grain = ONE row per (family_recipe_id, iso_week 1..52) carrying the multiplicative index + a `is_global_fallback` flag for the brewery-wide curve (store the global curve as its own pseudo-family, e.g. `recipe_id=NULL`/sentinel row-set, so fallback is a lookup not a branch). Columns (sql agent finalizes): `recipe_id` (NULL=global curve), `iso_week` TINYINT, `seasonal_index` DECIMAL, `sample_years` / `n_obs` (provenance for the <2yr fallback decision), `computed_at`, plus a small `kpi_seasonal_index_meta` row OR a `computed_at` MAX read for freshness-chip. `schema_meta` row required (new table).
- **Cron:** weekly (S is stable; daily is wasteful). Wire as a maltyweb cron / scheduled PHP CLI, NOT a maltytask Node script (strangler: new compute homes in maltyweb+MySQL). Recompute wholesale, INSERT-fresh into a temp/swap or TRUNCATE+repopulate in one txn (idempotent). Emit a freshness timestamp so the render can show "indice saisonnier au {date}" and degrade gracefully (if cache empty/stale вЖТ fall back to the current flat-mean so the page NEVER hard-fails on a cold cache).
- **L stays at RENDER** (per the model): one indexed aggregate on `inv_sales_ledger(sku_id_fk, posting_date)` for the trailing 52 weeks + EW-mean in PHP. Cheap with the new composite index. This is the part that legitimately belongs in `fg_stock_compute()` Step 8.

### B. DERIVATION-TREE PLACEMENT
- **S (cached family seasonal shape)** = a NEW materialized leaf hanging off `inv_sales_ledger` (SoT) via the `sku_id_fkвЖТref_skus.recipe_id` family rollup. It is a projection, not a new fact. Upstream: `inv_sales_ledger` + `ref_skus.recipe_id`. Downstream: the forward sim only. It is NOT in the Le Zeppelin commissioning chain and NOT COGS/beer-tax-bearing (it's a demand-shape analytic, unit-counts only) вАФ so it does not touch the SOT chain. Single canonical owner = the cron.
- **L (per-SKU level)** = render-time scalar, lives in `fg_stock_compute()` Step 8, owned by that function. Upstream: `inv_sales_ledger` (sku-grain) + `S` (to deseasonalize). Downstream: the sim.
- **Forward sim + semaines_restantes** = render-time, `fg_stock_compute()` Step 8, owned there. Upstream: `physique` (already computed) + `L` + `S`. Downstream: existing health-tier classification + chip + progress bars (unchanged seam).
- **Pooling collision check (resolved):** family=`ref_skus.recipe_id` does NOT collide with anything вАФ it's the existing recipe-family key already used across the BOM/SKU tree. The ONLY friction is the NULLs (6 active SKUs + 146 ledger rows + the 25% unresolved-SKU rows) вЖТ all route to the global-curve fallback / coverage-gap surface; none silently corrupt a family aggregate.

### C. PHASING вАФ AGREED (with one addition)
- **MVP** (delivers the CORRECT forward seasonal number): family seasonal index `kpi_sku_seasonal_index` + weekly cron + render-time `L` (EW ќї=0.95, weeks-since-first-sale divisor for new SKUs) + forward depletion sim + net-of-returns (qty_out=вИТќ£signed_qty floored вЙ•0/week) + EOL "sans rotation" label + display triad (primary semaines_restantes + secondary "rythme de base" L + status chip with normal/provisoire). **Cold-cache graceful fallback to current flat-mean is part of MVP** (so the page can't 500 on an un-run cron). This is your MVP list вАФ AGREED.
- **Fast-follow:** Croston's level for sporadique SKUs (ADI>1.32) + lead-time-relative bands (needs per-family `L_repl` data **Kouros must provide** вАФ until then bands stay on the current absolute `WEEKS_*` constants) + overstock ceiling + threshold re-tune to forward semantics. **ADD to fast-follow:** the `kpi_sku_seasonal_index` **freshness-chip on the page** (same maltyweb-prefers-live discipline that's still open on the COP tiles вАФ surface "indice au {date}", don't let a silently-stale cron pass as fresh). AGREED.

### D. MIGRATION / EQUIP / SEQUENCING / FLAGS
- **Migration number: `325` is the next free slot** (live-verified 2026-06-11: no `325_*` file local OR on VPS, absent from `schema_migrations`; 326/327 already applied вАФ there is a GAP at 325). 328 also free if a second mig is needed. **RE-RUN `migrate.php --status` + `ls db/migrations` at build-start вАФ parallel sessions live; the gap could be claimed.** One mig suffices: `325_kpi_sku_seasonal_index.sql` = CREATE TABLE `kpi_sku_seasonal_index` (+`schema_meta` row) + the composite index `ADD INDEX idx_sl_sku_posting (sku_id_fk, posting_date)` on `inv_sales_ledger` (INSTANT/INPLACE) + the `system_settings` param INSERTs (section e.g. `prevision_stock`). MySQL-8 syntax (no IF NOT EXISTS on ALTER, no bare SELECT).
- **PARAMS вЖТ `system_settings`** (the canonical central params table, NOT hardcoded): ќї, season=52, horizon=104, clamp[0.2,4.0], ADI cutoff 1.32, EOL K=26wk, provisional thresholds (13wk/6 non-zero/full-summer), smoothing window=3, half-life. Shape fits: `section`/`key_name`/`value_num DECIMAL(10,4)`/`default_num`/`unit_fr`. Per-family `L_repl` lead-times = a SEPARATE keyed set Kouros provides (fast-follow) вАФ likely `commissioning_settings` or a small `ref_*` per-family table, NOT `system_settings` scalars (it's per-family). NB `value_num` is DECIMAL(10,4) вАФ fine for ќї=0.95 and clamps.
- **EQUIP: sql + coder + ui + webapp-testing.** sql owns mig 325 + the cron query + the composite-index plan + EXPLAIN on the 52wk render pull. coder owns the cron CLI + `fg_stock_compute()` Step-8 rewrite + cold-cache fallback. ui owns the display triad + chip + freshness label. webapp-testing = read-only `?view=stock` prod smoke (semaines renders, chip states, no 500 on cold cache).
- **DIVERGENCE FLAGS:** (i) **family JOIN, never string/name** вАФ pool on `ref_skus.recipe_id` via FK JOIN, NEVER on beer-name (the match-on-recipe_id-not-beer-name rule). (ii) **single burn path** вАФ S=cron-materialized, L=render; the sim must be the ONLY consumer; do NOT let the old flat-mean and the new engine BOTH feed `semaines_stock` except as the explicit cold-cache fallback. (iii) **NULL families вЖТ global curve, surfaced** вАФ never silently drop the 6 NULL-recipe SKUs / 146 ledger rows / 25% unresolved-SKU rows; they go to the global fallback + a coverage-gap count, refuse-don't-NULL discipline. (iv) **not COGS/beer-tax** вАФ unit-counts only; the cron must NOT touch `inv_consumption`/`ref_sku_bom`/CHF; it's a demand-shape analytic, outside the SOT chain. (v) **idempotent cron** вАФ wholesale recompute/overwrite, no incremental accumulation that could drift S from the ledger. (vi) **cold-cache must degrade** вАФ page renders (flat-mean fallback) when the cron hasn't run, never 500.

### D2. BURN-QUANTITY SEMANTICS вАФ PM RULING 2026-06-11 (recon-driven; resolves 3 quantity-correctness forks the S&OP expert could not, having no BC-export visibility)
Live recon (2026-06-11): `inv_sales_ledger` 44,164 rows 2021-01-05вЖТ2026-06-09, 133 resolved SKUs, 25% NULL `sku_id_fk`. doc_type qty_signed sums: **shipment вИТ1,080,057 (n=31257); invoice вИТ753,202 (n=6309, SAME sign as shipment); credit +526,362 (n=6580, dominated by ¬±58,206 correction PAIRS w/ invoice); return_receipt +98 (n=18).** Columns: posting_date, doc_type ENUM(shipment/invoice/credit/return_receipt), sku_id_fk, qty_signed DEC(14,4), customer_id_fk, sales_amount_chf, hl_resolved. Composite (sku_id_fk,posting_date) idx CONFIRMED MISSING (two single-col idxs only) вЖТ mig 325 must add it.
- **рЯФі RULING 1 вАФ SHIPMENT-ONLY: SUPERSEDED FOR BURN 2026-06-11 (escalation-driven reversal; the verify-gate fired exactly as designed).** The original ruling (shipment-only, on a mirror-double-count hypothesis) was REVERSED when its own VERIFY-BEFORE-CODE clause (b) surfaced invoice-only goods-out. **Burn = вИТSUM(qty_signed) across ALL doc_types** (shipment+invoice outbound вИТ ; credit+return_receipt back-in + ; net naturally via qty_signed sign). EVIDENCE (live re-verified 2026-06-11, sale_class√Чdoc_type net вИТSUM): **eshop invoice 77,537 vs shipment 4,722 (94% of eshop goods-out is INVOICE-documented); taproom invoice 11,451, shipment 0 (100% invoice, ZERO shipment) вЖТ shipment-only DROPS taproom entirely + 94% of eshop.** Mirror hypothesis FALSIFIED: (i) `bc_source_no` is CUSTOMER-grained (~8 docs/source, 1064 distinct vs 8265 shipment docs) вАФ the "252 shared source_no" = 252 customers using both flows, NOT per-order mirrors; (ii) each (doc_type, bc_line_seq) is a DISTINCT BC Item-Ledger movement вАФ credits visibly net against shipments same-week, no shipment+invoice pair narrates one physical line; (iii) eshop literally migrated doc_type ERA (shipment-posting 2021 вЖТ invoice-posting later, same goods). The вИТ/вИТ sign agreement encodes DIRECTION (both outbound), not duplication. **b2b CONSISTENCY (make explicit so no one re-restricts b2b later): b2b also posts invoice +664,143 alongside shipment +1,072,632 вАФ same doc_type-era migration, b2b-wide. The all-doc-type rule applies to b2b too; do NOT special-case b2b back to shipment-only.** SAFE DIRECTION: shipment-only under-counts burn on eshop/taproom-heavy SKUs вЖТ over-states weeks-remaining вЖТ false runway on the fastest-growing channels (the dangerous direction Kouros flagged). All-doc-type = honest/slightly-conservative runway. **Shipment-only REMAINS correct as the B2B-DISPLAY lens (mig-326 `v_sales_ledger_order_lines`, Commandes surface) вАФ a legitimately different question (one-shipment-per-order-line for display); the two coexist by design. Do NOT point burn at that view.**
- **RULING 2 вАФ channel scope = OPTION (a): ledger, ALL physical-stock sale_classes (incl. taproom + eshop where present), accept pre-2024 eshop-history gap as a NAMED FAST-FOLLOW (not MVP blocker).** [NB 2026-06-11: "shipment-only" qualifier here is OBSOLETE вАФ RULING 1 reversed to all-doc-type; channel scope itself stands, now even more so since taproom/eshop are invoice-documented.] Rejected (b) eshop-splice from inv_sales_orders = a 2nd burn path across two stores/grains/temporal-seam вЖТ violates single-burn-path flag (ii). Rejected (c) strict-canonical B2B-only = OVER-states weeks-remaining on taproom/eshop-heavy SKUs (the dangerous direction: false runway on core beers). Burn universe must MATCH the `physique` numerator's depletion universe (b2b+taproom+eshop). Family-pooled S already absorbs eshop's seasonal shape wherever eshop hits the ledger; eshop-only L precision = fast-follow. VERIFY-BEFORE-CODE: `SELECT c.sale_class,l.doc_type,COUNT(*),ROUND(-SUM(l.qty_signed)),MIN/MAX(posting_date) FROM inv_sales_ledger l JOIN ref_customers c ON c.id=l.customer_id_fk GROUP BY 1,2` вЖТ proves which sale_classes/eshop are in the ledger + date-span вЖТ decides if eshop-splice fast-follow is even needed.
- **RULING 3 вАФ sale_class universe = DENY-LIST `customs_artifact` ONLY (REFINED 2026-06-11 to what's actually in the ledger).** Filter = `sale_class IS NULL OR sale_class NOT IN ('customs_artifact')`. Live ledger sale_classes present: b2b, eshop, taproom, event, giveaway, staff, customs_artifact, + 1 NULL-customer shipment row. INCLUDE everything physical: b2b/taproom/eshop + giveaway/staff/event (each unit physically left FG stock = real depletion) + the NULL-customer row (+228, physical goods-out; NULL = coverage-gap to surface, refuse-don't-drop). EXCLUDE only customs_artifact (fiscal artifact; nets to 0 anyway, but exclude explicitly so a future non-zero customs row can't leak). **`transfer`/`sample` are NOT present in `inv_sales_ledger`** (they live elsewhere, operator-confirmed) вЖТ dropped from the deny-list to keep it honest to the table; if a transfer/sample row EVER appears in this ledger that's a schema surprise вЖТ ESCALATE, do NOT pre-emptively sweep it. вЪ†пЄП sales-side `sale_class='giveaway'` is WHOLLY DISTINCT from `inv_side_stock_ledger movement_type='giveaway'` (mig 303) вАФ burn reads the SALES ledger ONLY.
- **рЯФі NET DERIVATION (one line, CORRECTED 2026-06-11):** Burn = **вИТSUM(qty_signed) over inv_sales_ledger WHERE sku_id_fk IS NOT NULL AND (sale_class IS NULL OR sale_class NOT IN ('customs_artifact'))** вАФ **ALL doc_types** (shipment+invoice+credit+return_receipt net via sign) вАФ floored вЙ•0/week, family-pooled sku_id_fkвЖТref_skus.idвЖТrecipe_id (S) / sku-grain (L). **DELIBERATE DIVERGENCE from `v_sales_ledger_order_lines`: that view is the B2B shipment-only DISPLAY lens; burn is all-doc-type all-physical-channel. DO NOT reuse the B2B view as the burn source вАФ burn needs its own SELECT over the base table. Comment this in cron+Step-8 so a future reader doesn't "fix" the discrepancy by pointing burn at the view.** (Prior shipment-only NET DERIVATION superseded вАФ see RULING 1.)
- **VERIFY-GATES вАФ RESOLVED 2026-06-11 (the gate worked: R1(b) surfaced invoice-only goods-out вЖТ escalated вЖТ RULING 1 reversed).** R1 mirror-check: mirror hypothesis FALSIFIED (bc_source_no customer-grained, not order-mirror; doc_types are distinct Item-Ledger movements). R2 channel-presence: b2b/eshop/taproom/event/giveaway/staff + 1 NULL present; transfer/sample absent. R3 ENUM: deny-list narrowed to customs_artifact only. All three CLOSED вАФ no remaining pre-code blocker on the burn-source leg. **EQUIP for the verify+burn-source leg: sql + coder** (ui+webapp-testing stay equipped for the render/smoke legs of the broader build).

## рЯФС D2 ECHO-FIELD RULING вАФ credit-memo write-back (PM ruling 2026-06-15, BC-probe-backed)
**Context:** D2 (credit-memo write spine, disarmed, nothing committed) surfaced a surface-split conflict. The avoir (credit memo) entity is NOT on the OData v4 web-service surface D1 uses (`/ODataV4/.../SalesCreditMemo*` вЖТ 404). It lives ONLY on **BC API v2.0** (`/api/v2.0/companies(<uuid>)/salesCreditMemos`), where `Your_Reference` does NOT exist вАФ the only filterable echo field is **`externalDocumentNumber`** (= `External_Document_No`), the field RESERVED in the D1 ruling for SalesOrders.

**LIVE BC PROBE (2026-06-15, read-only, NEBULEUSE company id `e2b691c6-8393-ed11-bff5-002248f307ee`):** 3,800 credit memos total; **155 (4%) have `externalDocumentNumber` populated**; sample values = free-text human refs (`RETOUR DOWTOWN LAUSANNE`, `COMMANDE 127596`, `CMD: N¬∞ 4031¬І`, `ERREUR QUANTITE`, bare invoice numbers). **ZERO start with `mt:`** вЖТ namespace collision-free. `$filter=externalDocumentNumber eq 'mt:cm:<n>'` confirmed OData-filterable вЖТ GET-before-create idempotency works.

**RULING (option 3 + 2a hybrid):**
1. `externalDocumentNumber='mt:cm:<order_id>'` is **ACCEPTABLE as the echo for CREDIT MEMOS** (NOT for sales orders вАФ the D1 reservation stands unchanged on the OData SalesOrder surface). Three reasons: (a) the D1 reservation was framed around `External_Document_No` as KOUROS'S split-order key вАФ that key lives on the SALES ORDER flow, not on credit memos; on the CM entity the field is a free-text human ref, sparsely used (4%), and our namespaced `mt:cm:` prefix is provably disjoint from every existing value AND from the order namespace `mt:` (bc_echo.py enforces the disjointness in code: `bc_echo_parse` returns None for `mt:cm:вА¶`, `bc_cm_echo_parse` returns None for `mt:вА¶`). (b) it is the ONLY filterable echo field on the v2.0 CM entity, so GET-before-create idempotency has no alternative anchor on the BC side. (c) namespacing makes accidental collision with a human-typed order ref structurally impossible.
2. **BUT the echo field is the SECONDARY idempotency guard, not the primary.** Primary = the `ord_bc_credit_memos` tracking table (mig 366): a local row keyed on the source order means "we already issued an avoir for this." The BC-side GET-before-create on `externalDocumentNumber eq 'mt:cm:<id>'` is the cross-process safety net (catches a tracking-table/BC divergence вАФ e.g. tracking write failed after BC create). Both must agree before a CREATE; either one matching = skip-and-rekey, never double-issue. (This is option-2a's tracking-table idempotency layered UNDER option-3's namespaced echo вАФ belt and suspenders, because a credit memo is financially irreversible.)
3. **SURFACE-SPLIT IS FINE вАФ no reader/echo-loop problem.** The reader (`ingest_bc_sales_orders.py`) pulls ORDERS only and never pulls credit memos back; nothing in maltytask consumes the avoir on a later pull. So the CM "echo" exists SOLELY for GET-before-create idempotency, NOT a read-loop вАФ which is exactly why the field choice is low-stakes (no downstream parser keys on it). The re-invoice (document #2) continues through D1's OData SalesOrder path with `Your_Reference='mt:<id>'`; the avoir (document #1) goes through API v2.0 with `externalDocumentNumber='mt:cm:<id>'`. Two surfaces, two disjoint namespaces, one tracking table вАФ coherent. The ONLY thing that must hold: `bc_cm_echo_parse` must never be fed to the order reader and vice-versa (already structurally guaranteed by bc_echo.py).

**CONFIRMED UNCHANGED from prior D2 scope:** CREATE-only, NEVER POST/post (avoir + re-invoice stay in draft/unposted). Disarm = dry-run default + two-flag live (`--apply` AND `--i-have-kouros-go`) + NO cron. The COGS verification Opus owes BEFORE any write (the DGDF-wrong-vs-DGDB-right line depletes correctly) is STILL REQUIRED вАФ run it as the rolled-back-txn probe, same discipline as D1's id=365 no-double-deplete check. Live proof = ONE synthetic fixture (createвЖТverifyвЖТdelete), NEVER the real already-invoiced Pepitium doc.

**mig 366 NUMBER вАФ CONFIRMED CLEAN.** VPS `migrate.php --status` MIG HEAD = 364, 0 pending (verified 2026-06-15). 365 and 366 are both free; the duplicate-361 mess (`361_ord` benign collision) is well below and does not touch 366. вЪ†пЄП STANDING PRE-FLIGHT: re-run `migrate.php --status` AND `ls db/migrations | grep 36` immediately before applying вАФ parallel sessions can land a number between now and apply-time (the 278 duplicate is the proof case).

## вЬЕ D2 AS-BUILT вАФ credit-memo write-back SHIPPED + LIVE-PROVEN + DISARMED + COMMITTED (`de7b610`, ON origin/main, 2026-06-15). **PHASE 2 (D = D1 + D2) NOW COMPLETE.**
The ECHO-FIELD ruling above was implemented exactly as ruled (option 3 + 2a hybrid; two surfaces, two disjoint namespaces, one tracking table). As-built:
- **Writer `scripts/python/push_bc_credit_memos.py`** (SIBLING вАФ imports D1's `push_bc_sales_orders.py`, did NOT modify it): drains `divergence_status='correction_compta_requise'`; creates the avoir via **BC API v2.0 `salesCreditMemos` + `salesCreditMemoLines`** (credit memos are NOT on the OData v4 surface D1 uses вАФ 404 confirmed; v2.0 is the ONLY write surface). Admin ops: `--delete-bc-cm` (v2.0 DELETE by UUID + If-Match) + `--make-test-correction`/`--cleanup-test-correction`.
- **`bc_echo.py` EXTENDED (not forked):** credit-memo namespace `bc_cm_echo_format`/`bc_cm_echo_parse` вЖТ `mt:cm:<id>`, provably disjoint from order `mt:<id>` (each parser returns None for the other's prefix вАФ disjointness enforced in code).
- **mig 366** (applied + on origin, number clean вАФ no collision): `ord_bc_credit_memos` tracking table (FKвЖТ`ord_orders.id` BIGINT UNSIGNED, ON DELETE RESTRICT, UNIQUE on `order_id_fk` + `echo_ref`) + new terminal `divergence_status` ENUM value `correction_compta_emise`.
- **ECHO-FIELD as-built:** avoir uses **`externalDocumentNumber='mt:cm:<id>'`** (PM-ruled OK for CMs вАФ live probe 3800 CMs, 4% populate it, ZERO with `mt:` prefix; the `External_Document_No` reservation applies ONLY to the sales-order surface). Two surfaces / two disjoint namespaces / one tracking table.
- **LIVE SUPERVISED ROUND-TRIP** (Kouros-authorized, executed by Opus, 2026-06-15): synthetic correction fixture (order 161, line corrected to DGDB, `ord_order_bc_lines` wrong=DGDF) вЖТ live `--apply` вЖТ **avoir AVVEN-005495** created (API v2.0, line DGDF, echo `mt:cm:161`) + tracking row + divergence flip вЖТ **re-invoice ORD210080** created via D1 path (line DGDB) вЖТ idempotency re-run = 0 corrections (terminal flip prevents re-drain) вЖТ deleted BOTH BC docs (avoir via `--delete-bc-cm`, re-invoice via D1 `--delete-bc`) вЖТ cleaned local (back to 138, 0 tracking/divergence residue). **API v2.0 `salesCreditMemos` POST works under D365 BUS FULL ACCESS вАФ NO new permission gap.**

A line corrected to DGDB depletes DGDB by exactly the qty, DGDF unmoved; the wrong DGDF line hits DGDF only; NO double-count. The avoir reconciles BC to a correct operational state.
- **рЯФі STANDING FLAGS (carry forward):** D2, like D1, is **proven plumbing with NO live producer** вАФ zero `correction_compta_requise` rows in prod; the real Pepitium doc is already invoiced вЖТ handled by manual BC credit-note (Kouros). The **OPEN-SCOPING flag still stands: no maltytask-native order/correction PRODUCER in v1.**

## рЯЖХ PER-ORDER DEPARTURE-SITE вАФ TWO-TIER "learn-default + per-order exception" MODEL (P1 chip+override SHIPPED 2026-06-16; P2 learning-write PM-SCOPED, NOT built)

> вЪ†пЄП **STATUS RECONCILED 2026-06-16 (was stale below "NOT built"):** P1 (board chip рЯУНauto/вЬОoverride + inline `<select>` + endpoint `public/api/expeditions-set-site.php` + JS `expeditions-set-site.js`) IS **SHIPPED** (repo files dated 06-16; chip render `expeditions.php` L4205-4225, resolver call L4103, board query carries `fulfilment_site_id_fk`+`customer_default_site_id` L1838-1840, fg_stock_compute consumes resolver Step 4 L451 + snapshot L1210). Endpoint writes ONLY `ord_orders.fulfilment_site_id_fk` + log_revision. The ¬ІBUILD SCOPE / DIVERGENCE FLAGS / EQUIP blocks BELOW describe P1 as-shipped (kept as the build record).

### THE REFINED TWO-TIER MODEL (Kouros verbatim intent, 2026-06-16) вАФ P2 build target
**Tier 1 = customer's VALIDATED ship-from = `ref_customers.default_delivery_site_id_fk`** (the durable client-fiche fact; vast majority = Zeubi/warehouse id2, correct). **Tier 2 = per-order one-off = `ord_orders.fulfilment_site_id_fk`** (exception for THIS order only, must NOT touch the customer default). **"maltytask n'invente pas":** a customer with NO validated default must be FLAGGED вЪ† √† renseigner, not shown an invented site. The logistics operator's FIRST site-input on an order **auto-establishes the customer default** (learning write); subsequent orders pre-fill from it; per-order override is the exception layer on top; permanent change = edit the client fiche.

**LIVE DATA (probed 2026-06-16):** ord_orders site-overrides: import=71 (all site2/Zeubi, **62 of those customers have NO default**, 0 override==default), web=0, bc=0. Only **15 of 2665** active customers carry a `default_delivery_site_id_fk`. Sites holds_fg_stock: 1 Zgeg(production) / 2 Zeubi(warehouse) / 3 Taproom(pos) / 4 Nausikraft(consignment). `ref_customers` governance = **only `needs_review` tinyint** вАФ NO draft/lock/verify gate on the master вЖТ cross-table write from the order endpoint to `default_delivery_site_id_fk` collides with NO ownership rule.

**A. RESOLVER 3rd UI STATE вАФ NO depletion change.** `fg_stock_compute()` Step 4 (L451) + snapshot (L1210) call `resolve_fulfilment_site()` per order, which ALWAYS returns a non-zero site (warehouse fallback at the bottom) вЖТ stock math never breaks even with no customer default. The вЪ† "√† renseigner" state is **pure UI**, derived from `customer_default_site_id IS NULL AND fulfilment_site_id_fk IS NULL AND order_type='customer'` (not eshop/taproom which have hard channel defaults). Warehouse STAYS the compute fallback; the flag is display-only, zero depletion impact. Eshop stays hard-wired warehouse (unchanged).

**B. THE LEARNING WRITE (core new behavior) вАФ endpoint branch logic.** On operator pick via the inline control, the endpoint decides which column:
  - customer default IS NULL вЖТ write pick to **`ref_customers.default_delivery_site_id_fk`** (establish validated site; order then resolves via customer default; per-order override stays NULL).
  - customer HAS default AND pick вЙ† default вЖТ write **`ord_orders.fulfilment_site_id_fk`** (per-order exception).
  - customer HAS default AND pick == default вЖТ clear any per-order override (no-op exception, set fulfilment_site_id_fk=NULL).
  - explicit "clear override" вЖТ set `ord_orders.fulfilment_site_id_fk=NULL` (back to auto).
  **Both writes log_revision (two audit targets: ref_customers AND ord_orders).** RECOMMENDED UX = **EXPLICIT intent, not pure inference** when establishing a default: when customer-default IS NULL, the control offers two confirmable actions вАФ "d√©finir comme d√©faut du client" (writes ref_customers, the expected path) vs "juste pour cette commande" (writes the per-order override even with no default). Inferring purely from default-presence is too magic for a COGS-adjacent location fact and gives the operator no escape hatch for a genuine one-off on a defaultless customer. When customer HAS a default, the control is the plain override (single action) + a clear-to-auto. Endpoint response must carry which table was written + the new resolved name + the new UI state so the chip re-renders рЯУН/вЬО/вЪ† correctly.

**C. PERMANENT-CHANGE PATH вАФ ALREADY SHIPPED.** No "Carnet clients" module exists; customer-master `default_delivery_site_id_fk` editing already lives at **`reglages-generaux.php?sec=delivery_sites`** (admin assign/remove, holds_fg_stock whitelist validation + log_revision, L890-957). This IS Kouros's "changement permanent" path вАФ verified. P2 may add a convenience "Lieu de d√©part par d√©faut" dropdown to a per-customer fiche later, but the canonical write surface exists; do NOT build a parallel one.

**D. P2 BUILD PLAN (minimal diff atop shipped P1):** (1) endpoint `expeditions-set-site.php` вАФ add branch logic (read customer default in the already-present order-fetch JOIN; route write to ref_customers vs ord_orders per B; second log_revision target); add an `intent` param ('default'|'order') for the explicit-UX when default IS NULL. (2) board chip вАФ add the вЪ† "√† renseigner" 3rd state (derive from the columns already in the board query L1838-1840; pure render). (3) JS вАФ when chip is вЪ†/defaultless, present the two-action choice; otherwise plain override+clear; consume the endpoint's table-written + state fields. **MIGRATION: NONE** (both columns exist). RULE 3: no ref_pages change вЖТ no tour card. RULE 1: nothing scrapped (additive on P1). **EQUIP: sql + coder + ui + webapp-testing.** SMOKE: new-customer first-input writes the default (ref_customers row updated + order resolves рЯУН via default, override stays NULL); 2nd order on that customer pre-fills рЯУН auto; per-order override on a defaulted customer writes ord_orders ONLY (customer default untouched); clear-to-auto re-resolves; fiche edit at reglages changes the default. Both audit targets verified in audit_row_revisions.

**E. LEGACY 71 IMPORT-OVERRIDES вАФ PM RECOMMENDATION = OPTIONAL dry-run migration, needs Kouros's OK (do NOT auto-run).** Under the two-tier model these 71 (all site2/Zeubi, source='import', from the retired WeeklyOrders importer) sit in the EXCEPTION column but are really "normal Zeubi" вЖТ they render вЬО (manual) when they should read рЯУН (auto). Clean fix: for rows where `fulfilment_site_id_fk == would-be channel-default(warehouse=2) AND customer.default_delivery_site_id_fk IS NULL`, **move overrideвЖТcustomer-default (set ref_customers.default=2) then clear ord_orders.fulfilment_site_id_fk=NULL** вЖТ they read рЯУН and the customer gains its validated default (which is correct вАФ these clients DO ship from Zeubi). 62/71 qualify (no customer default). рЯФі **FG-ATTRIBUTION CAVEAT: clearing the override on a SHIPPED/historical order changes nothing in fg_stock attribution** because the resolver returns the SAME site (override 2 вЖТ now customer-default 2 вЖТ identical resolved id); ќ£-by-site unchanged. Safe. The 9 non-qualifying rows (customer already has a default, or defaultвЙ†2) stay as-is. **Kouros's stance = leave them; PM concurs leaving is acceptable** (majority Zeubi is correct, just mislabeled вЬО). Offer the dry-run migration as a cosmetic+data-hygiene nicety only if the вЬО/рЯУН mislabel bothers the operator. Dry-run first, count qualifying rows, Opus-verify resolver returns identical site pre/post before any apply.

**Ask (Kouros, original P1):** orders enter via BCвЖТord_orders cron (source='bc'), NOT the maltytask saisie form. On maltytask he wants (a) the resolved departure site VISIBLE per order on the Commandes board, and (b) an inline override (e.g. MKK normally Nausi вЖТ this time Crissier) usable directly on BC-sourced rows. вФАвФА P1 below as-shipped.
- **WHERE IT SITS:** override field `ord_orders.fulfilment_site_id_fk` (already exists, mig 290-era) вЖТ `resolve_fulfilment_site()` (`app/fulfilment-site.php`, THE single authority: override > `_customer_default_site_id`/`customer_id_fk`вЖТ`ref_customers.default_delivery_site_id_fk` > channel-default warehouse/pos). Whitelist = `ref_sites WHERE holds_fg_stock=1 AND is_active=1` (the 4 sites). Downstream of the field: `fg_stock_location_snapshot()` site attribution. THIS IS THE SOT CHAIN вАФ feature reuses it end-to-end, adds NO parallel store.
- **CURRENT DISPLAY STATE (code-verified 2026-06-16):** resolved site is **NOT** on the Commandes board. Board query (`expeditions.php` ~L1826) selects NO `fulfilment_site_id_fk` / `customer_id_fk` / customer-default-site, never calls the resolver; B2B row renderer (~L4122) renders chips for overdue/stock-risk/backorder/divergence/BC-shipped/lead-time but NO ship-from chip. The field is editable ONLY inside the edit form (`expeditions.php` ~L4718): `<select name="fulfilment_site_id_fk">` "Automatique" + `$fgStockSites` whitelist, pre-selected from `$editOrder['fulfilment_site_id_fk']`. POST whitelist-enforced (L394/422/483: invalid id вЖТ NULL).
- **рЯЯҐ CRON-CLOBBER VERDICT вАФ SAFE, NO GUARD NEEDED (code-verified).** `scripts/python/ingest_bc_sales_orders.py::upsert_order()` UPDATE (status IN entered/confirmed) writes ONLY `requested_date, order_created_date, updated_at`; INSERT writes `(order_type, customer_id_fk, requested_date, order_created_date, status, source, source_ref, created_by_user_id, comment)`. The bulk delivery-date one-shot (~L1620) writes ONLY `requested_date, order_created_date, updated_at WHERE id=? AND source='bc'`. **`fulfilment_site_id_fk` is in NO BC write path** вЖТ a manually-set override SURVIVES every `*/15` re-pull. (Verdict is structural; a build agent must re-grep both writers' column lists pre-ship to confirm no new column was added вАФ but as of 2026-06-16 it is clean.)
- **BUILD SCOPE (minimal, clean вАФ field + whitelist + resolver already exist):**
  - **(a) Board ship-from chip:** add to the board query (~L1826) `o.fulfilment_site_id_fk, o.internal_channel, c.default_delivery_site_id_fk AS customer_default_site_id` (customer already LEFT-JOINed); per row call `resolve_fulfilment_site($pdo, [...])` with those + `customer_id_fk` to get the resolved id, map idвЖТname from the already-loaded `$fgStockSites`. Render a chip showing the site name; **mark explicit-override vs auto-resolved** = `fulfilment_site_id_fk IS NOT NULL` (a вЬО/рЯУН glyph + title="site choisi manuellement" vs plain chip "exp√©di√© depuis {site}"). Reuse the resolver вАФ do NOT inline a channelвЖТsite map (divergence anti-pattern, called out in the resolver's own docblock).
  - **(b) Inline override control:** new JSON endpoint `public/api/expeditions-set-site.php` вАФ **direct clone of `public/api/expeditions-line-status.php`** (the proven sibling pattern): POST `{csrf, order_id, fulfilment_site_id_fk}`; guards = `require_login` + `require_page_access('expeditions')` + `can_write_expeditions($me)` 403 + `csrf_verify` (fresh-token echo); validate `order_id>0` + site_id вИИ holds_fg_stock whitelist OR =0/'' (= clear override вЖТ "Automatique", writes NULL); ONE txn: `UPDATE ord_orders SET fulfilment_site_id_fk=? WHERE id=?` + `log_revision`; respond `{ok, order_id, fulfilment_site_id_fk, resolved_site_name, is_override, csrf}` (recompute resolved name server-side so the chip re-renders correctly even when cleared-to-auto). ## вЬЕ HISTORICAL-COMMANDES DATA LANE вАФ SHIPPED + LIVE on prod 2026-06-11 (mig 326; 3 read-only VIEWs over `inv_sales_ledger`)

- **3 read-only VIEWs over `inv_sales_ledger`:**
  - `v_sales_ledger_orders` вАФ **7,497 historical orders.** `synthetic_order_id = CONCAT('BC:', bc_document_no)`, + `posting_date`, `customer`, `line_count`, `total_units`, `total_hl`. **MAX(posting_date) = 2026-06-05** (cutover cap holds вАФ no forward leakage).

- **рЯФС GRAIN REFINEMENT to the earlier PM read-contract (durable вАФ supersedes the allnet-display assumption):** order CARDS are built from **shipment documents** (`doc_type='shipment'`), NOT the allnet-netted figure. Rationale: a commande = a delivery; credits/invoices are separate correction *documents* that cannot net *within* a document-grouped order and would clutter a browse view. **`allnet` stays the AUDIT-total basis** (the reconciliation report); **shipment-doc grain is the DISPLAY basis** for browsing past commandes. Both coexist cleanly вАФ display вЙ† audit, by design.
- **Basis (confirmed):** resolved-FG only; **B2B-scope** = `ref_customers.sale_class NOT IN ('eshop','taproom','customs_artifact','transfer','sample')` вАФ eshop/taproom stay owned by their existing auto-rows (no double-count, R1 XOR preserved). **Cutover = 2026-06-08** (earliest forward `ord_orders.requested_date`; forward вЙ• cutover, historical < cutover вЖТ clean partition with the forward `ord_*` lane).
- **Division held (lane discipline):** the data lane (I) shipped the VIEWs + read-contract with **ZERO `expeditions.php` edits** вАФ no collision with the parallel expeditions overhaul. The **expeditions UI chat** wires the Commandes gather to read these views per `docs/historical-commandes-read-contract.md` (their lane, when their overhaul lands).

### ASK 1 вАФ Tap-machine (T7) PICKUP orders must surface on the Commandes board вЬЕ SHIPPED
**AS BUILT (render-only, this session's expeditions.php change set):** eshop line render now reads `inv_sales_order_lines.title` (pill fallback `sku_code ?? title ?? '?'`) with a "mat√©riel" badge when `sku_id_fk IS NULL` вАФ 65√Ч "Tireuse Portable" + 65√Ч "Caution" now show readably instead of `?√Ч1`. NO schema, NO ingest change, NO stock effect; T7 stays OUT of `ref_skus`. Playwright-smoke-verified. Pre-build probe below for provenance.
**LIVE-VERIFIED render behaviour (expeditions.php Commandes / `exp_render_eshop_row`):**
- Eshop order HEADER comes from `inv_sales_orders` (Query 3a, L1715) with **NO SKU-existence filter** вЖТ an order whose lines don't resolve to a SKU **IS shown** (header, customer, рЯПђ/рЯЪЪ/вЪ† badge, Shopify tag). The order is NOT dropped.
- Lines (Query 3b, L1733) = `inv_sales_order_lines isol LEFT JOIN ref_skus s` вЖТ NULL `sku_id_fk` keeps the row; render pill = **`isol.sku_code` (raw), falling back to `'?'`** when `sku_code` itself is NULL; family colour = `exp_format_family('')` (NULL `s.format`). **The line is shown but uninformative.**
- рЯФС **ROOT GAP (the load-bearing finding):** the ingest (`scripts/ingest-shopify-orders.ts` L317) maps **Shopify's SKU field вЖТ `sku_code`** and the **line TITLE вЖТ a SEPARATE `title` column** (L327). Tap-machine lines have a BLANK Shopify SKU вЖТ `sku_code=NULL` вЖТ render as bare **`?√Ч1`**, EVEN THOUGH the descriptive `title` ("Tireuse Portable", "Caution") IS persisted in `inv_sales_order_lines.title` вАФ **the render NEVER reads `title`.** Live: 65√Ч "Tireuse Portable" + 65√Ч "Caution" + Gobelets/Pack-de-No√Ђl/Beer-des-Rosses/Carte-cadeau all sit in `title` with `sku_code=NULL` (263 NULL-sku lines / 2646 qty total). **NO order carries a "Tireuse"/"TAP"/"T7" sku_code** вАФ they are ALL title-only.
- **DERIVATION-CORRECT FIX (no phantom SKU, no stock touch):** render pill fallback chain = `sku_code ?? title ?? '?'`; when `sku_id_fk IS NULL` add a **"non-stock / mat√©riel" badge** on the pill (greyed, distinct from beer families). T7 stays OUT of `ref_skus` (correct вАФ it's non-stock equipment), so it never enters `fg_stock_compute()` and never depletes. This is RENDER-ONLY (expeditions.php + .css), NO mig, NO ingest change (title already captured). The Phase-3c `ref_skus.is_non_stock` flag (mig 323) is INERT here вАФ it only matters for SKUs that EXIST in ref_skus; T7 isn't one, so the discriminator is simply "`sku_id_fk IS NULL` вЖТ non-stock line". Reuse that predicate, don't invent a parallel flag.
- **Re "вСҐ tap machine soon integrated as Shopify sales":** that note is the SALES/COGS lane (does a tap-machine sale post revenue / become a sellable line), NOT FG-stock. It does NOT change the fulfilment surface: even if T7 becomes a revenue line later, it stays NON-STOCK equipment (no liquid/packaging BOM, no FG depletion). Fulfilment-only display is the right scope now; a sellable-T7 path is a separate later question (would touch `inv_sales_ledger` sale_class + possibly a non-FG `ref_*` equipment catalog, NOT `ref_skus` inventory). Surface for fulfilment now; do NOT pre-build a sellable path.
- **VERDICT: BUILD (no Kouros decision needed) вАФ render-only, SOT-safe, no phantom SKU, no depletion.** Only judgement call = the badge label ("mat√©riel" vs "non-stock" vs "retrait mat√©riel") вАФ a copy choice, fine to pick + show Kouros. **EQUIP: ui + coder + webapp-testing** (sql NOT needed вАФ zero schema/query change; the `title` column is already selected if we add it to Query 3b, which is a one-column add, still no schema). NB: add `isol.title` to the Query-3b SELECT (it's not currently selected) вАФ that's the only backend touch.

### ASK 2 вАФ "Several times a day" Exp√©ditions refresh from Shopify вЬЕ SHIPPED (VPS-REHOMED)
**AS BUILT (Option-2 ruling executed вАФ see ¬ІSHOPIFY-INGEST VPS REHOME below):** `/opt/maltytask-pipeline` synced to current HEAD via `bin/deploy.sh --apply-pipeline` (the 05-22 stale copy GONE вАФ ingest now md5-matches local, has shipping_lines/fulfilment_mode capture; npm ci ran); `secrets/shopify.env` on VPS at `/opt/maltytask-pipeline/secrets/shopify.env` (mode 640, maltytask:www-data); new cron `db/cron/maltytask-shopify-ingest.cron` (maltyweb repo = source-of-truth) вЖТ `/etc/cron.d/maltytask-shopify-ingest`, `*/15`, maltytask user, nvm idiom (mirrors document-ingest), DB via db.env (127.0.0.1:3306, NO tunnel). **Commit `5ade521`.** Validated: VPS dry-run + a real run freshened the 2-day-stale board (latest import seconds-old, 3164 eshop orders); **cron CONFIRMED firing autonomously** (11:00 UTC tick wrote the log, idempotent no-op, no new orders in window). **The fragile local-WSL `*/15` tunnel crontab is RETIRED вАФ VPS cron is the sole runner, independent of the operator's machine.** Freshness chip ("Dernier import Shopify", amber > 90 min) shipped on the board EITHER-WAY (the staleness sentinel that justified the rehome). Pre-build probe below for provenance.

**LIVE-VERIFIED cadence/host (pre-build probe вАФ now superseded by the VPS rehome above):** ingest is a **`*/15` USER-CRONTAB job on the LOCAL WSL box** (`crontab -l`: `flock -n /tmp/shopify-ingest.lock npx tsx scripts/ingest-shopify-orders.ts --since $(date -d "2 days ago")`), writing to MySQL **over a manually-established SSH tunnel on 13306** (`ssh -f -N -L 13306:... maltyweb`, ServerAliveInterval=30). BOTH cron AND tunnel are local-box-resident = the exact fragility recorded (memory was right). It already runs every 15 min, so "several times a day" is ALREADY met IF the box+tunnel are up.
- **The real thing to fix is NOT frequency вАФ it's the host/transport fragility.** Bumping frequency on a local-box/tunnel cron buys nothing; the failure mode is "WSL asleep / tunnel dropped вЖТ board silently stale," not "not frequent enough." **DERIVATION-CORRECT TARGET: move the ingest to the VPS** (where MySQL is local, no tunnel) as a real `/etc/cron.d/maltytask-shopify-ingest` entry вАФ same strangler discipline as the recipe-profile + seasonal-index crons (compute homes on the VPS). Cadence on the VPS: every 15вАУ30 min is fine ("several times a day" satisfied with margin). Secrets: `secrets/shopify.env` must land on the VPS (not committed). Runtime: `npx tsx` exists where the maltytask repo is вАФ confirm the repo (or just the script + lib) is deployable to the VPS, or wrap as a maltyweb PHP CLI that shells the existing TS (prefer keeping the TS, just rehome the cron).
- **Idempotency: SAFE to run more often.** Line-level `row_hash = sha256("shopify|order|line|sku|qty")` UNIQUE + `INSERT IGNORE` (L321/L503-553); header upsert keyed on `(source, external_order_id)` with a real UPDATE branch (L447-472). The earlier line-idempotency bug (recorded in ¬І0a11 Phase 0) is FIXED. Re-running over an overlapping `--since` window = no-op on unchanged rows, UPDATE on changed status. No double-ingest concern.
- **VERDICT: small Kouros decision, then BUILD.** The build (rehome cron to VPS) is sound + low-risk, but it needs (a) Kouros OK to install a VPS cron + put `shopify.env` on the VPS, and (b) confirming the maltytask repo/script is present/deployable on the VPS (today the ingest only runs from the local clone). If Kouros would rather NOT put the Node toolchain on the VPS, fallback = harden the local path (autossh + a cron-health/freshness chip on the board surfacing "dernier import Shopify: {time}" so staleness is VISIBLE вАФ same maltyweb-prefers-live discipline as the COP/seasonal freshness-chip debt). **PM rec: VPS-rehome is the clean target; the freshness-chip is worth doing EITHER WAY** (so a stalled ingest can't masquerade as "no new orders"). **EQUIP: coder + sql** (cron/CLI + host migration) **+ ui + webapp-testing** if the freshness-chip is included.

Model P in force (global-pool depletion, no per-order/per-production location tag).

**THE LOAD-BEARING CALLS (canonical):**
1. **Per-location CARD = that location's latest-count-DATE snapshot only.** loc1 Production card shows the **4 June SKUs, NOT the 37 April-only leftovers** (pre-split bootstrap; a fresh full physical is a complete statement of what's standing there). Card query: per (sku, location) take rows where `counted_at = MAX(counted_at) for that location`. **Do NOT delete/tombstone the 37 April rows** вАФ card *visibility* вЙ† anchor *membership* (see #3).
2. **Cards STATIC (frozen Monday snapshot) / TOTAL LIVE.** `TOTAL physique = ќ£_loc(latest-count qty) + global production since anchor вИТ global shipments/eshop/taproom since anchor`. The ќ£-anchor term and the flow window MUST be the same count rows. The 2 derived lines (вИТsemaine-open, вИТall-open) come off the live TOTAL only. Orders are global (no location tag) вЖТ subtract from TOTAL, never from a card.
3. **рЯФі R4 RESOLVED вАФ anchor is PER (sku) = SKU's latest count across all locations, NOT one global `MAX(month_closed)`.** The current `fg_stock_compute()` does global `MAX(month_closed)` вЖТ picks `2026-06` вЖТ **silently ZEROES the 37 loc1 April-only SKUs** (no June row вЖТ anchor 0). THAT is the concrete R4 bug. Correct model: `anchor_qty(sku) = ќ£_loc(qty at that loc's latest count of that sku)`; `flow_window_start(sku) = MAX(counted_at) over the rows feeding that anchor`. SKUs only in April bootstrap anchor on April + deplete by prod/ship since April (NOT zeroed); SKUs counted 06-08 anchor on June. Staggered counts (Taproom 06-09) advance per-SKU automatically. **This per-SKU anchor fix is a CORRECTNESS fix to fg_stock_compute() independent of the board вАФ do it regardless.** "Stop showing April on the Production card" вЙ† "stop summing April into the anchor".
4. **Taproom empty вЖТ graceful-zero** ("pas encore compt√©", contributes 0, NEVER blocks). Its SKUs anchor on whatever other location last counted them (or April) until 06-09.

**ARCHITECTURE (B): two functions, clean split.** Keep `fg_stock_compute()` GLOBAL for TOTAL + derived lines + per-SKU live table (**but fix to per-SKU anchor model #3**). ADD pure-read `fg_stock_location_snapshot(PDO)` keyed `[loc][sku]=>latest-count qty` for cards (NO flow math). Both read same `is_active=1` rows. **Verification gate: after a no-flow Monday count, `ќ£ cards == TOTAL physique`** (proves anchor model); and the 37 April-only loc1 SKUs appear in TOTAL but NOT on the Production card.

**SOT/derivation hazards preserved:** R1 (both functions READ-only, no 2nd FG-depletion path; Stage-2 tracker writes inv_consumption = different fact); R2 (cage -X vs box -B вАФ card model is safer, just confirm eshop cage-first netting when -X anchors land); R3 (verify production leg excludes is_tombstoned/is_white_label AND contract recipes вАФ Bamberg/Jasper +5 contract SKUs must NOT leak into Neb total, check `ref_recipes.classification`); **C5 вАФ carry `display_family` into the board grouping** (mig 287 added it; fg-stock grouping deliberately NOT yet changed вАФ Task #10 IS the place to split multipacks PD8/Xmas/Louis/Chef under their own header, LEFT JOIN ref_packaging_formats, group `COALESCE(display_family, format)`).

### вЬЕ PF-STOCK BUILD вАФ FULL-BOX FLOORING + PER-LOCATION PRODUCTION ATTRIBUTION SHIPPED 2026-06-09 (committed `d71d890`, pushed, live; NO migration вАФ data + PHP: `app/fg-stock.php` + `public/modules/expeditions.php`; EQUIP coder+sql+ui +webapp-testing)
**Built per the design we consulted; supersedes the `566b9d3` production-leg fix with the operator's full-box PF rule + per-location production crediting. No mig (data + PHP).**

1. **FULL-BOX FLOORING (operator PF rule).** production = `SUM(FLOOR(prod_total_units / units_per_pack))` вАФ floored **PER EVENT then summed** (NOT sum-then-floor). **Operator rule: PF = full boxes only; loose units from a partial run are NOT PF** вАФ they are the future "mini side-stock" (item E below). DIV4 9901 вЖТ **412 boxes** (was 412.54). kegs/cuv `units_per_pack=1` вЖТ floor is a no-op. `prod_qty` + `physique` are now INTEGERS.
2. **PER-LOCATION PRODUCTION ATTRIBUTION.** `fg_stock_location_snapshot()` now credits floored production-since-prod-site-count to the **production-site card** (DB-derived `site_type='production'`, gated by `$isProdSite`). Renens DIV4: 37 count вЖТ **449** (37 + 412). Other sites are anchor-only. **New invariant: ќ£(locations) == physique when sales=0** (verified 449+39+23 = 511).
3. **SINGLE-SOURCED (drift-proof вАФ the Q2 requirement).** New private helper **`fg_prod_since_anchor(PDO, $globalAnchor)`** returns `{prod_site_ids, by_sku:{prod_qty:int, prod_events:int}}`; **BOTH `fg_stock_compute()` AND the snapshot call it**, so the SKU-total card and the per-location card cannot drift.
4. **INTEGER DISPLAY (Q5 #4).** unit/box columns render 0-decimals; **HL stays decimal**.
5. **STOCK ORDER.** `$stockFamilyOrder` now **Keg вЖТ Bot вЖТ Can вЖТ Can33 вЖТ multipack вЖТ Cuve**; single-unit SKUs (`sku_code` suffix `/(BU|CU)$/`, taproom-only) bucketed into **"√А l'unit√© (taproom)" rendered LAST**. Applied to total table, filter chips, AND per-location snapshot grouping.

**Q1 verdict held: NO new setting, NO `receives_packaging` column вАФ `site_type='production'` remains the single SoT.**

**STILL OPEN вАФ item B (DEFERRED, likely next pending operator confirm):** expose `ref_sites.site_type` + `holds_fg_stock` editing in the Donn√©es g√©n√©rales sites admin (`reglages-generaux.php` `edit_site` handler currently does NOT expose `site_type`), with helper line "le conditionnement alimente le stock PF des sites de type Production" вАФ so the operator can SEE/SET it.

**вЬЕ ITEM 2 / item E вАФ MINI SIDE-STOCK / GIVEAWAYS TRACKER вАФ SHIPPED + PUSHED 2026-06-10 (maltyweb `1c95e23` on origin/main; mig 303; UNIT-COUNTS ONLY, NEVER COGS).** Packaging loose-unit remainder = `bd_packaging_v2.prod_total_units MOD ref_skus.units_per_pack`. Lives between `bd_packaging_v2` and beer-tax. As-built:
- **mig 303 `inv_side_stock_ledger`** вАФ append-only, tombstone-only, `table_class='source'`, `corrections_policy='allowed'`. Per-SKU keyed (`sku_id_fk` INT UNSIGNED FKвЖТ`ref_skus` RESTRICT). `movement_type` ENUM(`accrual`+ / `complete_box`вИТ / `giveaway`вИТ / `year_end_offered`вИТ / `adjustment`¬±) with enforced `chk_ssl_sign`. `bd_packaging_id_fk` BIGINT UNSIGNED FKвЖТ`bd_packaging_v2` SET NULL. `fiscal_year` CHAR(4). `submitted_by_user_fk` FKвЖТ`users` SET NULL.
- **DEVIATION (recorded):** `accrual_key` is a PLAIN nullable VARCHAR(48) written by PHP (`"$bdPkgId:$skuId"`), NOT a STORED generated column вАФ MySQL 8.0.46 returns err 1215 when ALTER-adding a STORED generated col whose expr references a FK column that has ON DELETE SET NULL (`bd_packaging_id_fk`). `uq_ssl_accrual` UNIQUE on it gives idempotency (NULLs don't collide). *(Generalizes the mig-288/mig-292 generated-column lessons вАФ here the SET-NULL FK was the blocker, not the FK type.)*
- **DISTINCTNESS (critical):** this is the PACKAGING-remainder fact, wholly distinct from the SALES-side `sale_class='giveaway'` (migs 300/301, sales-commercial-surface arc). NOT COGS (unit counts only; never `inv_consumption` / `ref_sku_bom` / CHF). Production-site-homed. OUT of `fg_stock_compute()` FG legs вАФ `app/fg-stock.php` byte-unchanged (verified).
- **Writer (`form-packaging.php`):** accrual banked per-format row, hung off the per-format `resolve_packaging_sku_id()` result `$rSpec['sku_id_fk']` вЖТ **mig-265-safe parallel -4/-B attribution** (each leg shares session recipe_id, differs by format_suffix вЖТ own SKU). `complete-a-box` draw field (`side_stock_complete_box`) with refuse-don't-NULL balance check (French error, rollBack). `units_per_pack=1` (keg/cuv) вЖТ remainder 0 вЖТ no accrual.
- **Re-save / edit idempotency = TOMBSTONE-PRIOR-THEN-REINSERT** (caught + fixed on RULE-2 review; first build had 3 lifecycle bugs): on every packaging-row write, prior live `accrual`+`complete_box` rows for that `bd_packaging_id_fk` are tombstoned + `accrual_key` NULLed, then fresh rows inserted. Fixes: complete_box no longer double-inserts on edit; accrual qty updates when prod_total edited; tombstone frees the key. `giveaway`/`year_end_offered`/`adjustment` rows UNTOUCHED (distinct real-world events, not run-derived).
- **Surface (`expeditions.php ?view=side-stock`):** per-SKU live balances + ledger breakdown; operator giveaway entry (CSRF + balance-checked refuse-don't-NULL); admin tombstone (CSRF + `is_admin` gated; UPDATE sets `accrual_key=NULL` + `log_revision`); 60s live-refresh JS (maltyweb-prefers-live-visibility canon). CSS in `/public/css/`, JS in `/public/js/`.
- **Operator decisions baked in:** per-SKU keying; giveaways accumulate + settle year-end; parallel-run attribution.
- **Verification:** 22 assertions incl. full AвАУF edit lifecycle (B no double-insert on re-save; C accrual qty updates; F tombstone re-bank); render-smoke 302 (not 500); idempotency confirmed; clean tree.
- **рЯФі OPEN DOWNSTREAM (the remaining Item 2 work) = YEAR-END-SETTLE CRON, DOCUMENTED-NOT-BUILT.** Beer-tax hook inline-JOIN shape recorded in mig 303: `SELECT sku_id_fk, SUM(qty_units) FROM inv_side_stock_ledger WHERE movement_type='year_end_offered' AND fiscal_year=? AND is_tombstoned=0` вЖТ unitsвЖТHL via `ref_skus.hl_per_unit`. No-double-count rationale included (accruals untaxed; `complete_box`вЖТFG via normal path; giveaways net into year-end residual, taxed once). NOT YET BUILT: a year-end-close cron that WRITES the `year_end_offered` draws + feeds beer-tax. **Canonical balance: ќ£(prod MOD upp) вИТ ќ£(complete_box) вИТ ќ£(giveaway) вИТ ќ£(year_end_offered) ¬± ќ£(adjustment).**

**STILL-OPEN CARRYOVERS:** sales-leg per-location settlement (stock-movement-saisie arc). **вЫФ NO DATEвЖТDATETIME migration to do вАФ REDUNDANT, do NOT dispatch one.** Same-day settlement is ALREADY fully solved with NO migration: prod-leg via Option-2 tiebreak (`d3fb954`), and ESHOP + cross-site TRANSFER legs via **Task A** (`2192153`, 2026-06-10, `app/fg-stock.php`, NO mig). Mechanism = the EXISTING `inv_fg_stocktake.created_at` (already a `timestamp` вАФ live-verified 2026-06-10; `counted_at` STAYS `date` = business truth) used purely as the same-day tiebreak. The only same-day gaps that REMAIN are **B2B** (no ship-time finer than `requested_date`) and **taproom** (month-grained period). Nothing is gated on the Mon 2026-06-15 cage count for this вАФ the cage count just lands an anchor. **рЯФі CORRECTION 2026-06-10: the B2B gap is NOT "intentional/safe" вАФ it is a REAL computation bug (global anchorDate pollution drops legitimate same-day ships); reclassified + ruled in ¬ІB2B EXPEDIE LEG = REAL COMPUTATION BUG below. The taproom month-grained gap is still genuinely deferred.**

### вЬЕ TWO PF-STOCK FIXES SHIPPED 2026-06-09 (committed + pushed + deployed; outage fix `ae297c2`, production-leg fix `566b9d3`; EQUIP coder+sql)
**Both on origin/main (afe1dcd..566b9d3), deployed (selective rsync + chown www-data). No migration вАФ data + PHP only.**

1. **Exp√©ditions OUTAGE FIX (`ae297c2`) вАФ 500 on the whole PF-stock page.** `exp_dow_fr()` (the French-weekday helper added in `afe1dcd`, the fresh-chip feature, an earlier same-day session) was defined NESTED inside the stocktake render function вЖТ undefined at the EARLIER call site (~L2824, the "вЬУ compt√©" fresh-chip branch). PHP nested function defs are **runtime-declared in call order**, so a helper used before its (later) nested definition fatals. That branch only fires when a count EXISTS this week вЖТ today's stocktake tripped "Call to undefined function exp_dow_fr()" вЖТ 500. **Fix: hoisted `exp_dow_fr` to the top-level date-helper section** (compile-time hoisted; also kills a latent cannot-redeclare on double render). **DURABLE LESSON: keep page helpers TOP-LEVEL вАФ never nest a helper inside a render function if any earlier code path may call it.** (Convention candidate for the `coder`/`ui` skill if it recurs.)

2. **`fg_stock_compute()` PRODUCTION-LEG FIX (`566b9d3`) вАФ partial count poisoned the global cutoff, dropped same-day production.** The bug PM predicted: R4 anchor SUM is per-(sku, location) but the flow windows still ran off a single global `$anchorDate`. A partial count (today: Taproom/pos-site only, 2026-06-09) advanced the global cutoff вЖТ same-day production-site packaging vanished from physique (DIV4 9901 btl, DIVB 2592 btl invisible). **Fix applied exactly as consulted:**
   - **Production site id(s) DB-derived** from `ref_sites WHERE site_type='production' AND is_active=1` (id=1 Zgeg/Renens today; **set-valued, no hardcode**).
   - **Per-SKU production cutoff = MAX(counted_at) for that SKU at the production site(s)**; `COALESCE` fallback to global `$anchorDate` for SKUs never counted there.
   - **`run_type='cuv'` EXCLUDED from the prod leg** (cuve-de-service = filled-at-client = sold, never FG stock). Three independent guards make cuv SKUs (EMBV/MOOV/ZEPV) vanish from the computed FG table with no negatives: cuv has no anchor + no `ord_order_lines` depletion path + `stocktake_scope='none'`.
   - **Sales legs (expedie/eshop/taproom) STILL on the global cutoff** вАФ per-location settlement DEFERRED to the stock-movement-saisie arc; documented inline with a SCOPE NOTE near `$anchorDate` (prod-fixed вЙ† all-fixed; taproom period>anchorMonth can exclude the current month on partial-count days).
   - **Verified live (www-data probe):** DIV4 prod_qty=412.54 (9901/24), DIVB=108 (2592/24), ZEPV absent; non-production-anchored SKUs (DIB4/DIVF/EPH4B) compute prod_qty=0, no crash.

**DURABLE вАФ packaging-inflow site model:** packaging inflow ALWAYS lands at the **production site (Renens, DB-derived)**. Inter-site moves (RenensвЖТCrissierвЖТNausikraftвЖТTaproom) = the future **stock-movement saisie arc** (NOT built). `ref_sites` today: id1 Zgeg/Renens (production, holds_fg), id2 Zeubi/Crissier (warehouse, holds_fg), id3 Taproom/Renens (pos, holds_fg), id4 Nausikraft (consignment, holds_fg, customer_id_fk=1).

**OPEN / DEFERRED (flag at stock-movement-saisie arc):**
- **Sales-leg per-location settlement** вАФ expedie/eshop/taproom legs still use the global `$anchorDate`; per-location settlement deferred to the stock-movement saisie arc (the prod leg is now per-SKU-per-site; the sales legs are NOT). Documented inline as a SCOPE NOTE.
- **Same-day count+package edge вАФ `counted_at` is a DATE with strict `>`** вЖТ a SKU counted AND packaged on the same date can mis-settle (the count and the production happen on the same calendar day; DATE granularity + `>` cannot order them). Needs **DATETIME granularity on `counted_at`** вАФ **worth doing before/with the Monday 2026-06-15 cage count** (cage anchor is the next big partial-count event that could re-trip this class).

## вЬЕ SAME-DAY TIEBREAK SHIPPED 2026-06-09 вАФ same-day count+package carryover CLOSED via Option 2 (surgical tiebreak, NO migration; committed `d3fb954`, pushed, live; data-layer only вАФ `app/fg-stock.php`; EQUIP coder+sql)
Closes PF-stock carryover (1) WITHOUT the DATEвЖТDATETIME migration. The bug: a beer counted AND packaged on the SAME date (e.g. EMBF 2026-06-08) had its same-day production-site packaging DROPPED, because the per-SKU production anchor used a strict `event_date > prod_anchor` cutoff against a DATE `counted_at` вАФ the same-day packaging tied the cutoff and fell out.

**Implementation (`fg_prod_since_anchor()`):**
- Per-SKU production anchor now uses a single **`ROW_NUMBER() OVER (PARTITION BY sku_id_fk ORDER BY counted_at DESC, id DESC)`** window pick (rn=1), exposing the WINNING production-site count's BOTH `counted_at` (вЖТ `prod_anchor`) AND `created_at` (вЖТ `prod_anchor_ts`). **NOT two blind MAXes** вАФ the PM-flagged gotcha (two independent MAX() could pair a `counted_at` from one row with a `created_at` from another). One window row = one coherent count.
- Cutoff predicate: `event_date > COALESCE(prod_anchor, $globalAnchor) OR (prod_anchor IS NOT NULL AND event_date = prod_anchor AND submitted_at > prod_anchor_ts)`.
- **Primary ordering on business `event_date`**; `submitted_at > prod_anchor_ts` (created_at) only breaks SAME-DATE ties. NULL-safe for never-counted SKUs (collapses to pure `$globalAnchor` cutoff). Empty-prodSites fallback unchanged. All prior guards kept (cuv-exclude, tombstoned, white_label, FLOOR-per-event, COALESCE).
- SINGLE helper вЖТ both `fg_stock_compute()` AND `fg_stock_location_snapshot()` inherit the predicate; card vs SKU-total can't drift.

**OPUS INDEPENDENT VERIFICATION (old-vs-new predicate diff across ALL SKUs):** exactly ONE SKU changed вАФ **EMBF**, the genuine 2026-06-08 collision (prod-site count `created_at` 13:54:13; EMBF packaging `event_date` 06-08 submitted 14:53:07 вЖТ after the count вЖТ tie-broken IN вЖТ **OLD dropped=0, NEW=300 kegs recovered**). NO other SKU perturbed: DIV4=412 / physique=511, DIVB=108, ZEPV absent, never-counted (DIB4/DIVF/EPH4B)=0. **ќ£(locations)==ќ£physique=8312.**

**Decisions LOCKED (durable):**
- `counted_at` STAYS DATE вАФ business-truth column, mirrors `bd_packaging_v2.event_date`.
- `created_at` is canonically "when counted" for maltyweb-form / manual rows.
- `form_timestamp` NULL = latent Google-Form-era gap; NOT fixed now.
- **NO DATETIME migration** вАФ rejected for blast radius on every DATE-equality consumer.
- Sales legs (expedie/eshop/taproom) STILL deferred to the stock-movement-saisie arc.

**ACCEPTED RESIDUAL (inline SCOPE NOTE in `app/fg-stock.php`):** a run physically-before but submitted-after a same-day count вЖТ rare double-count, left un-clamped ON PURPOSE. If it ever bites, the fix is an explicit count timestamp вАФ NOT a clamp.

**Smoke:** 302 login-redirect (no page creds in this context); change is data-layer only, both stock functions proven non-throwing + data hand-verified вЖТ accepted. **NO migration number consumed** (293/294/295 are parallel sessions'). MIGRATION HEAD = 295; NEXT FREE = 298 (296/297 pending on VPS, BBT-vide arc) вАФ re-check `migrate.php --status` + `ls db/migrations` before assigning.

## 2026-06-08 вАФ Multipack display-family split (mig 287; SHIPPED+verified+committed `f97bcb9` local-only; PM-verified live)
**Stocktake (`expeditions.php` `?view=stocktake`) now groups curated/assortment gift packs under their own "Multipacks" header, split away from Bouteille.**

**CONFIRMED TAXONOMY (Kouros via AskUserQuestion 2026-06-08) вАФ Multipacks = the curated/assortment gift packs ONLY:** Pack D√©couverte (PD8, format_id **19**), Xmas Pack (XMASPACK, **20**), Pack Louis (PAL, **21**), Pack du Chef (PAC, **23**), + future DGD pack when it exists. **The 6√Ч4 packs (-4 SKUs) STAY under Bouteille/Canette** вАФ a 6√Ч4 is a presentation of the same-beer 24-pack, not a multipack. The 24-pack carton itself stays Bouteille (that's the "bottle" the multipacks are split away from). Rule of thumb: multipack = **cross-beer assortment**; -4/-B = same-beer presentation.

**Mechanism (the PM-recommended one вАФ a per-format display-grouping column, NOT a hardcode):**
- **Mig 287 `287_ref_packaging_formats_display_family.sql` (APPLIED, head=287, 0 pending; PM live-verified вАФ NEXT FREE = 288):** `ALTER TABLE ref_packaging_formats ADD COLUMN display_family VARCHAR(32) NULL` (placed after `derived_from_format_id`; `run_type` is not the last col вАФ no functional difference) + `UPDATE вА¶ SET display_family='multipack' WHERE id IN (19,20,21,23)`. All other formats keep `display_family NULL`. **Live-confirmed 4 seed rows = 19/20/21/23.**
- **`expeditions.php` (view=stocktake):** `$stAllSkus` LEFT JOINs `ref_packaging_formats` and selects `COALESCE(f.display_family, s.format) AS display_family`; family-grouping groups by `display_family` (fallback to format); `'multipack'` added to `$stFamilyOrder` (after Keg) + label "Multipacks"; `exp_format_family()`/`exp_family_label()` gained the `'multipack'` case. **Cage extraction (suffix -X) and `stocktake_scope` visibility logic UNCHANGED.** JS is DOM-driven (`data-family`) вАФ no JS change.
- **Practical render today:** only **PD8 + XMASPACK** appear under "Multipacks" (both `stocktake_scope='base'`); **PAC/PAL are `scope='none'` вЖТ stay hidden** until activated (matches "packs d√©couvertes et xmas currently are the ones we have activated").
- **Verified:** 153 active SKUs (count unchanged after the JOIN), `php -l` clean, curl 302. **ZERO COGS/SOT impact** вАФ `fg_stock_compute()` keys on `sku_id`, untouched.
- **Commit `f97bcb9` on maltyweb main вАФ NOT pushed (local only).**

**FORWARD COUPLING (carry into the cited future builds):**
- **Task #12 (Stock-config admin section):** `ref_packaging_formats.display_family` is now the **editable per-format display-grouping field**, alongside `ref_skus.stocktake_scope` вАФ BOTH get exposed in that config UI.
- **Task #10 (Stock PF board rebuild reading `fg_stock_compute`):** the Stock PF tab's OWN format-family grouping was **deliberately NOT changed** in this commit вАФ **multipacks must be split there too** when `fg-stock.php`'s query is rebuilt; carry `display_family` into `fg_stock_compute()` then. (This is the one place the new grouping is not yet honored вАФ flag at Stock PF rebuild time.)
