---
*(The pre-build spec below is retained as the model reference; the candidate-set / create-path / scope-lever reasoning is now as-built above.)*

**Context:** Olivier inputting taproom inventory. Taproom counts singles (-BU bottle / -CU can). Some beers have a 24-box (-B, `format_id=1`) but NO single-unit SKU вЖТ operator stopgap entered fractional packs (e.g. 21/24 against DGDB) to make HL come out right. Kouros: create the missing single SKUs (so they appear in taproom stocktake going forward) вАФ NO hardcoding, reroute from the SKU master.

**THE SKU MASTER + VOLUME DERIVATION (verified live):**
- **`ref_skus` is the SKU master.** Key cols: `recipe_id`(вЖТref_recipes.id), `format_id`(вЖТref_packaging_formats.id), `format`(display label e.g. 'Bot'/'Can'), `hl_per_unit`(DECIMAL вАФ COPIED from the chosen format's hl_per_unit at create), `units_per_pack`(NOT NULL DEFAULT 1), `stocktake_scope` ENUM('base','cage','single','none') DEFAULT 'none', `is_packaging_line`, `is_direct_sales`, `row_hash`.
- **Single-unit вЙ† a column on the pack вАФ it is its OWN `ref_skus` row** on the SAME recipe but a DIFFERENT `format_id`. A pack and its single are siblings under one recipe, NOT parent/child. Bottle pack = `format_id=1` (B, 24√Ч33cl, hl_per_unit 0.0792). Bottle single = `format_id=5` (BU, "Bottle unit single 33cl", hl_per_unit 0.0033). Can single = `format_id=14` (CU, single 50cl, hl_per_unit 0.005). So DGDBU = a NEW ref_skus row: recipe 31, format_id 5, format 'Bot', hl_per_unit 0.0033, units_per_pack 1, stocktake_scope 'single'.
- **Volume auto-derives, NEVER hardcoded:** `ref_skus.hl_per_unit` is copied from `ref_packaging_formats.hl_per_unit` of the chosen format (itself = units_per_format √Ч `dbc_container_types.hl_per_unit`, zero-drift chain вАФ volume-dimension.md). A new DGDBU created via the canonical path inherits 0.0033 from format 5 automatically.

**WHAT MAKES A SKU APPEAR IN TAPROOM STOCKTAKE = `ref_skus.stocktake_scope` (the channel flag вАФ NO hardcoding needed).** `expeditions.php` `exp_st_scope_allowed($scope,$siteType)` (the visibility matrix, ~L1626): `base`вЖТall sites; `cage`вЖТproduction+warehouse; **`single`вЖТpos ONLY (= Taproom)**; `none`вЖТnever. So a single-unit SKU **MUST be `stocktake_scope='single'`** to show for Olivier at Taproom (site_type='pos'). This is also the **DOCB exclusion lever**: DOCB/DOCF are `scope='base'` today; we simply do NOT create a DOCBU (or if created, leave scopeвЙ†'single') вАФ no hardcode, the absence of a 'single'-scoped Docks SKU keeps it out of taproom count. The 26 existing 'single'-scope SKUs are exactly the BU/CU singles.

**THE GAP (verified live 2026-06-09) вАФ recipes with a bottle/can PACK but NO single sibling, active SKUs:**
- **r31 DGDB (DrunkBeard - Galactic Drift)** вЖТ missing **DGDBU** (THE live problem; DGDB has stocktake rows incl. the 8/24 + 121 stopgaps at loc1).
- **r20 BAMB (Chien Bleu - Bamse, Contract)**, **r21 JASPB (Chien Bleu - Jasper, Contract)** вЖТ missing BU. **Contract beers вАФ likely NOT taproom-sold; confirm with Kouros before creating + scoping 'single'.**
- **r29 DOCB (Docks - NEIPA)** вЖТ **EXCLUDED per Kouros (not sold in taproom).**
- The `recipe_id NULL` group (COLLAB12/COLLAB4PACK/PAC/PAL/PD8/XMASPACK) is a FALSE POSITIVE вАФ composites/multipacks, not single-beer packs; ignore.
- **So the real "create a single" candidate set = DGDBU (now/deferred), + BAMBU/JASPBU IFF Kouros confirms Chien Bleu sells singles at taproom.** All core Neb beers already HAVE their BU/CU (the 26 'single' SKUs). DOC excluded. Verify the list with Kouros вАФ do NOT auto-create contract singles.

**CANONICAL CREATE PATH = format-activation in Salle de contr√іle (`public/modules/salle-de-controle.php` ~L262, action that INSERTs ref_skus).** Operator picks recipe + format вЖТ INSERT `(sku_code, recipe_id, format_id, format, hl_per_unit FROM the format, is_active=1, row_hash=sha256(recipe_id|format_id|sku_code), bom_template_id, last_modified_by='web', last_seen_at, imported_at)` + `log_revision` + post-commit `sdc_recompile_recipe_packaging($recipeId)`. **вЪ†пЄП GAP in that action: it does NOT set `stocktake_scope` (defaults 'none') or `units_per_pack` (defaults 1).** For a single, units_per_pack=1 is correct, but **scope stays 'none' вЖТ the new single would NOT appear in taproom until scope is set to 'single'.** Two clean options: (a) one-shot direct SQL after creating via SDC (set scope='single'); (b) better/durable вАФ the planned **task #12 stock-config admin** exposes `stocktake_scope` (alongside `display_family`) as an editable field, which is the proper home for flipping a SKU's channel visibility. PM rec: create DGDBU via SDC format-activation (auto-correct hl_per_unit + audit + BOM recompile), then set scope='single' (direct SQL one-shot now; task #12 UI later). `sku_code` is operator-chosen ('DGDBU'); UNIQUE collision-guarded on (recipe,format).

**COGS / derivation implications:** a single-unit SKU is a REAL packaging line (`is_packaging_line=1` like its siblings) and gets a BOM via `sdc_recompile_recipe_packaging` вАФ it = 1√Ч (bottle+cap+label+TEA+liquid), the INTRINSIC single-bottle BOM (walkthrough RULE #3). It maps to the **SAME recipe** as the pack (recipe 31 for DGDBU) вЖТ same liquid/COGS basis; only the format (and thus units_per_pack=1, hl_per_unit=0.0033) differs. NOT a pure count surface вАФ it flows into BOM/COGS like any SKU. Double-count guard (walkthrough cardinal invariant): a bottle is produced+consumed ONCE вАФ selling a single vs selling it in a box are different sale events drawing the same physical bottle; no double-count AT SALE.

**STEP 1 (deferred, AFTER stocktake input) вАФ correct the DGDB stopgap вЖТ DGDBU:** counts live in **`inv_fg_stocktake`** (cols: sku_id_fk, location_id_fk, counted_at, month_closed, qty DECIMAL(10,4), source ENUM, is_active, **`row_hash` = STORED GENERATED** `sha256(fgct|sku_id_fk|location_id_fk|counted_at)` since mig 288 вАФ location & hash can't diverge). Correcting = (i) create DGDBU; (ii) the stopgap row was qty=8 (or 21) recorded against DGDB sku_id at the 24-box scale вАФ to "move into DGDBU as 21 units": INSERT/UPSERT a DGDBU row qty=21 at the same location/counted_at AND zero-out (or delete via is_active=0 + audit) the fractional DGDB stopgap row. **Do it via the EXISTING edit feature** (`expeditions.php` FG-stocktake date-scoped edit, manager/admin) NOT ad-hoc SQL вАФ the row_hash incident (2026-06-08, see ¬ІINCIDENT) proves ad-hoc UPDATEs that touch sku/location WITHOUT going through the form/generated-hash path corrupt the dedup key. The generated row_hash now makes a sku-change auto-rehash, but route through the audited edit path regardless. Snapshot + log_revision.

**SEQUENCING:** (a) NOW = identify gap (done above) + confirm the create-list with Kouros (DGDBU yes; BAMBU/JASPBU only if Chien Bleu taproom-sold; DOC excluded). (b) Create the singles via SDC format-activation + set scope='single'. (c) DEFERRED to after taproom input = the DGDBвЖТDGDBU count correction via the edit feature. **EQUIP for the build: sql + coder + ui + webapp-testing** (the create touches SDC PHP + a scope flip + a stocktake correction via the UI edit path; smoke ?view=stocktake at Taproom shows the new single).

## 2026-06-08 вАФ INCIDENT + DURABLE FIX: `inv_fg_stocktake.row_hash` divergence (hash-keyed row mutated without rehash)
**INCIDENT (root cause understood, data ALREADY repaired+verified by operator):** the 06-08 misfile *correction itself* corrupted 28 rows. The stocktake dedup/upsert key is `row_hash = sha256("fgct|{sku_id_fk}|{location_id_fk}|{counted_at}")`, app-written, `UNIQUE uniq_row_hash`, INSERT вА¶ ON DUPLICATE KEY UPDATE (qty only, NOT location). The ad-hoc SQL `UPDATE location_id_fk 1вЖТ2` did **NOT recompute row_hash** вЖТ 28 rows sat at loc2 still hashed as loc1; the operator's later loc1 (Production) submit hash-COLLIDED with them and overwrote qty. **Repaired** in one txn from `audit_row_revisions` (before=Crissier/batch1, after=Production/batch3): restored 23 Crissier + recreated 23 Production + fixed 5 stale hashes; final loc1=27/550u, loc2=28/5976u, loc4=26/554u; **row_hash integrity 0 mismatch across all 81 June rows.** Data clean.
**DURABLE FIX вАФ PM RULING 2026-06-08 (APPROVED, with one mandatory amendment): convert `row_hash` to a STORED GENERATED column** `CHAR(64) AS (SHA2(CONCAT_WS('|','fgct',sku_id_fk,location_id_fk,counted_at),256)) STORED`, UNIQUE preserved вЖТ location_id_fk and hash can NEVER diverge again (fix-by-construction; the "remember to recompute hash on location change" lesson is thereby MOOT). Generated col, NOT a trigger (a trigger is bypassable by direct UPDATE exactly as this incident was; generated col is structural). STORED not VIRTUAL (UNIQUE index stability). **PM-VERIFIED LIVE before ruling:**
  - **SOLE writer = `expeditions.php:746` INSERT.** Every other ref to `inv_fg_stocktake` (warehouse.php, warehouse-export.php, app/fg-stock.php, maltytask lib/inventory*.{js,ts}, mysql-inventory.ts) is **read-only SELECT**. `sync-stocktake.js` writes BSF Sheets, never MySQL. **`source='bsf-stocktake'` has ZERO code writers** (appears only in mig 066's ENUM def). вЖТ converting is safe from rejected-INSERT; the form INSERT drops `row_hash` from its column list, ON DUPLICATE KEY fires off the generated UNIQUE.
  - **рЯФі MANDATORY AMENDMENT вАФ the premise "data is 100% hash-consistent" is FALSE for 41 rows.** `WHERE row_hash <> SHA2(CONCAT_WS('|','fgct',sku_id_fk,location_id_fk,counted_at),256)` = **41 rows**, ALL the `source='bsf-stocktake'` **April anchor** (`month_closed='2026-04'`, `counted_at IS NULL`), hashed by the OLDER legacy-import formula. June (81) is consistent; April (41) is NOT. On DROP+ADD, those 41 silently re-mint to `fgct|sid|loc` (CONCAT_WS SKIPS NULL counted_at вАФ note PHP `sha256` would emit a trailing `|`, so PHP-formula вЙ† generated-formula in the NULL case; generated col is the more-correct canonical). **Tolerable ONLY because nothing re-derives those hashes** (no bsf-stocktake writer). **Collision check PASS: all 122 rows вЖТ 122 distinct generated hashes (0 collisions); 2nd UK `uniq_sku_month_location_response` also 122/122 distinct.** Build must do this KNOWINGLY + document it in the migration comment; verify post-convert: 0 rows where `row_hash <> SHA2(...)`, 122 distinct, April-2026 active anchor still 41 rows.
  - **BUILD: own migration (confirm next free # via `migrate.php --status` + `ls db/migrations` вАФ parallel sessions take numbers, the 278 collision is precedent; local index showed head 287). DDL = DROP INDEX uniq_row_hash вЖТ DROP COLUMN row_hash вЖТ ADD generated STORED (collation `utf8mb4_unicode_ci` to match, or mixed-collation throw) вЖТ ADD UNIQUE uniq_row_hash. No new schema_meta row (existing table). `expeditions.php` edit: drop row_hash from INSERT col-list + binding (~L748/749/763/782); KEEP the `$rowHash = hash('sha256',вА¶)` compute вАФ still used by the before-snapshot `SELECT вА¶ WHERE row_hash=?` at L767; ON DUPLICATE KEY UPDATE stays (counted_at no-op since match is BY the hash). EQUIP: sql + coder (NO ui вАФ pure backend). Proof: dry-run 0 mismatch; idempotent double-submit вЖТ 1 row; UPDATE location_id_fk auto-shifts hash; self-clean test rows.**
  - **рЯФЧ FORWARD COUPLING for task #12 stock-config admin + task #10 Stock PF:** once row_hash is generated, any admin UI editing `location_id_fk` on a stocktake row AUTO-REHASHES вАФ desired, but it can now collide into an existing (sku,loc,date) row вЖТ the UNIQUE rejects/the ON DUPLICATE merges. The admin edit path MUST handle the UNIQUE-violation/target-exists case (the exact scenario that caused this incident). Note in the #12 brief.

**вЬЕ SHIPPED + LIVE (mig 288, 2026-06-08 вАФ agent conn dropped mid-run; PM live-verified + reconciled).** Generated col IS live and working: `row_hash CHAR(64) GENERATED ALWAYS AS SHA2(CONCAT_WS('|','fgct',sku_id_fk,location_id_fk,counted_at),256) STORED NOT NULL`, `UNIQUE uniq_row_hash`. 122 rows / 122 distinct hashes / 0 collisions; June repair intact (loc1=27/550u, loc2=28/5976u, loc4=26/554u); April anchor 41. Form deployed (row_hash dropped from INSERT). 0 orphan + 0 NULL sku_id_fk.
  - **FK RULING (PM, decisive): `fk_fg_sku` re-added as ON DELETE RESTRICT.** To add the generated col referencing sku_id_fk the agent had to DROP `fk_fg_sku` (was sku_id_fkвЖТref_skus.id ON DELETE **SET NULL** вАФ MySQL 8 forbids SET NULL/CASCADE on a generated-col input) and did NOT re-add it ("app-level integrity"). PM ruled: RESTORE the FK as **ON DELETE RESTRICT** (MySQL 8 ALLOWS RESTRICT/NO ACTION on a generated-col input; 0 orphans/0 NULLs вЖТ clean; strictly stronger than the moot SET NULL; a NULL sku_id_fk on a count row is a corrupt fact, not a tolerable orphan вАФ aligns w/ FK-discipline + minimize-NULL). `fk_fg_stocktake_location` (location_id_fkвЖТref_sites ON DELETE RESTRICT) was KEPT throughout (RESTRICT always allowed on gen-col inputs). **Both FK columns are now BOTH FK-enforced (RESTRICT) AND row_hash inputs** вАФ fully-wired canonical state; any future mig touching either column's type/nullability must account for both the FK and the generated expression.
  - **RECONCILIATION (schema_migrations drift вАФ DDL live but unrecorded; agent applied DDL without recording).** Ruled: (1) EDIT the 288 file so it fully describes live = gen col + uniq_row_hash + `DROP FOREIGN KEY fk_fg_sku` + `ADD CONSTRAINT fk_fg_sku вА¶ ON DELETE RESTRICT` (fold the FK re-add into 288, NOT a separate 289 вАФ the FK drop+re-add is a consequence of the gen-col DDL, one atomic migration matching live exactly). (2) Run ONLY the missing ALTER on live (gen col + UNIQUE + DROP already live; only the RESTRICT re-add outstanding): `ALTER TABLE inv_fg_stocktake ADD CONSTRAINT fk_fg_sku FOREIGN KEY (sku_id_fk) REFERENCES ref_skus(id) ON DELETE RESTRICT;`. (3) `INSERT INTO schema_migrations (filename, applied_at) VALUES ('288_inv_fg_stocktake_row_hash_generated.sql', NOW());` (the known drift pattern; confirm exact on-disk filename first). (4) `migrate.php --status` must show 288 no longer pending + nothing to apply вАФ migrate.php must NOT re-run 288 (would error re-DROPping/re-ADDing). schema_meta needs no new row (existing table); verify the existing row is present (don't duplicate). EQUIP sql+coder.

## 2026-06-09 вАФ WeeklyOrders SHEET INGESTION arc: PM PRE-BUILD RULINGS (dry-runвЖТmatch-reportвЖТKouros reviews unmatchedвЖТapply)
Goal: ingest the live WeeklyOrders sheet (Production/Logistic Masterfile, Google Sheet `1WA-GfwrD-lgMiWJ2ejg-92zq1Ps0CZaK6Sn11isbXyI`, tab WeeklyOrders, row-6 SKU header, per-week blocks) into `ord_orders` so operators continue on the web "where they left off." Revenue/fulfilment-bearing вЖТ never-speculate rule applies HARD; dry-run-first, flag-over-decide.

**LIVE STATE VERIFIED (PM-probed 2026-06-09):** `ord_orders`=12 / `ord_order_lines`=56 / `ord_order_status_events`=39. **The "12 test orders" ARE NOT throwaway вАФ they are real KW24 customer orders, `source='web'`, requested_date 2026-06-08/09, all BC-matched (ids 3-14; e.g. 6=AlloBoissons BC1393, 7=Bevanar BC1579, 8=March√© Flag Aubonne shipped, 9=D√©partement Marketing BC1807, 14=Sophie Degrauwe priv√© no-BC).** They have full event cascades (entered+confirmed+picked stamped at one timestamp). **NO `source_ref`/dedup column on ord_orders; NO UNIQUE business key** вАФ only PK + non-unique indexes (requested_date, status, customer, source+review_status). This is the crux of Q6.

**THE 7 RULINGS (decisive):**
1. **SCOPE = AGREE.** Import KW24 full current week (incl. already-delivered Mon/Tue) + ALL future booked (next-Monday + coming-weeks, through last dated future row before the Feb archive). **EXCLUDE the KW6/Feb archive** (delivered months ago = not operational handoff; "past" is satisfied by KW24's delivered rows). No bounded recent-past window вАФ the handoff is "continue where you left off," not "rebuild history." If Kouros wants a longer past tail for the Commandes range-view, that's a SEPARATE future-history-backfill arc, not this ingestion.
2. **STATUS = rightmost-checked-wins AGREE; emit EVERY reached stage as an event (events=truth), NOT just final.** Same pattern the 12 web rows already use (entered+confirmed+picked all stamped). occurred_at = requested_date (00:00) for ALL reached stages вАФ we have no per-stage timestamps from Excel; stamping reached stages at the order date is the honest reconstruction (collapsing to final-only would LOSE the audit fact that the order passed through them). Mark imported events `comment='import:weeklyorders'` so they're distinguishable from operator-driven transitions. Cache `status`=rightmost stage. (`user_id_fk` NULL on import events вАФ matches the existing 12.)
3. **INTERNAL CHANNELS = SKIP Taproom/Eshop/samples/Marketing-as-internal/priv√©-marketing notes вАФ DO NOT import as ord_orders.** This is the R1 one-fact-one-depletion rule. Eshop depletes via `inv_sales_orders`, Taproom via `inv_sales_bc` (the `fg_stock_compute()` legs) вАФ creating ord_orders for them = DOUBLE-DEPLETION on the board. WeeklyOrders Taproom/Eshop rows are operational notes, not the depletion truth. **CAVEAT (verify, don't assume): "(Marketing)"/"D√©partement Marketing" is AMBIGUOUS вАФ order id 9 is already a `customer` order to "D√©partement Marketing (BC 1807)" (a real BC sold-to that depletes via ord_*), NOT an internal channel.** So the skip-list is: rows whose CLIENT cell is literally Taproom / Eshop / "√©chantillons TS"/samples вАФ the internal-consumption channels that have their OWN depletion source. A BC-numbered Marketing sold-to is a customer order (keep). When in doubt вЖТ match report, never auto-skip a BC-numbered row.
4. **CUSTOMER MATCHING = AGREE, with the canon already established (no-fuzzy-links).** Precedence: parens BC# вЖТ `ref_customers.bc_customer_no` (exact); else name вЖТ exact, then `'alias:'`-noted rows from the merge pipeline, then **STOP** вАФ **NO fuzzy auto-link** (the ¬І2026-06-07 LATE item-2 + ¬ІOVERNIGHT canon: ¬ЂArches¬ївЖТ¬ЂMarch√©s¬ї 0.92 false match proves it). Fuzzy вЙ• threshold = SUGGESTION in the match report ONLY, never an auto-link. Unmatched/below-threshold/priv√©-not-validated вЖТ SURFACE in match report, NEVER auto-create or guess (revenue-bearing). Point the agent at the EXISTING infra: the merge-suggestion engine (`scripts/` merge pipeline, `9803849`) + the Carnet-clients typeahead ranking (bc-linked first, вЪ†-√†-valider last) вАФ REUSE that resolver, don't write a new one. priv√© individuals вЖТ match to validated private customers (the 89 priv√©s bucket from ¬ІOVERNIGHT) else flag.
5. **CIT√Й MULTI-LOCATION FESTIVAL = AGREE, N separate ord_orders.** One customer (BC 1823), ~13 distinct delivery rows = 13 ord_orders, each its own `requested_date` + line(s) + sub-location (Courtine/Grand Canyon/Pierre Viret/Stock F&BвА¶) in `comment`. The order grain is the delivery event, not the customer вАФ distinct dates/locations are distinct fulfilment obligations. (No festival-grouping entity needed in v1; comment carries the sub-location string verbatim.)
6. **DEDUP/IDEMPOTENCY = the real architectural decision. RULING: ADD a `source_ref VARCHAR` column to `ord_orders` capturing the sheet-row identity, with a UNIQUE/idempotency guard вАФ do NOT rely on a (customer,date,line-hash) heuristic.** Rationale: (a) the 12 existing rows are `source='web'` real orders that OVERLAP KW24 вАФ a content-hash dedup would either falsely-merge a legit second same-day order to the same client or fail to recognise the operator-entered twin; (b) line-hash is brittle (qty edits on the sheet, parallel -4/-B). **`source_ref` = stable sheet coordinate** e.g. `weeklyorders:{tab_gid}:{week_label}:{row_index}` (or a sheet-row content fingerprint if row indices shift). New mig: `ALTER TABLE ord_orders ADD COLUMN source_ref VARCHAR(190) NULL` + `UNIQUE uniq_ord_source_ref (source_ref)` (NULL allowed вЖТ web/email orders unaffected; only import rows carry it) вЖТ re-run = INSERTвА¶ON DUPLICATE KEY skip/update, structurally idempotent. **The 12 web rows: do NOT reconcile/replace/import-over them.** Match report flags any KW24 sheet row that collides with an existing web order (same customer_id_fk + same requested_date) as "вЪ† possible duplicate of existing web order #N вАФ operator decides keep-both / skip-import." NEVER auto-delete an operator's web order; NEVER auto-merge. The 12 are the operator's ground truth for the rows they already entered; the importer fills the REST of KW24 + the future book around them.
7. **OFF-TRADE = AGREE, customer attribute not order attribute.** The col2 OFF flag is `ref_customers.trade_channel` (already bootstrapped by explicit-ID list, ¬І2026-06-07 LATE item-4 вАФ Cobra-channel, substring-UNSAFE). Ignore it on the order; trust ref_customers. If a sheet row's OFF flag DISAGREES with the customer's stored trade_channel, that's a data-quality signal вЖТ surface in the match report (don't silently override either way).

**DIVERGENCE FLAGS for this build:** (i) double-depletion if Taproom/Eshop become ord_orders (ruling #3 prevents); (ii) fuzzy auto-link corrupting a revenue-bearing customer FK (ruling #4 вАФ flag-only); (iii) the 12-web-row overlap silently double-creating KW24 (ruling #6 вАФ source_ref UNIQUE + collision-flag); (iv) a BC-numbered Marketing/priv√© sold-to wrongly skipped as "internal" (ruling #3 caveat). **SEQUENCING:** mig (source_ref col + UNIQUE) вЖТ parser/dry-run producing match report (matched / fuzzy-suggested / unmatched / internal-skipped / web-overlap-collision buckets) вЖТ Kouros reviews unmatched+collisions вЖТ `--apply` (single txn per order; ord_orders + lines + cascaded events; log_revision; idempotent on source_ref). **EQUIP: sql + coder + xlsx-or-sheets-read** (the source is a live Google Sheet вАФ service-account read; the existing bootstrap used a downloaded xlsx, mirror that or read via the sheets client; NO ui unless a match-report viewer page is wanted вАФ recommend a plain markdown/CSV report first, like the bootstrap report). Mig number: re-run `migrate.php --status` + `ls db/migrations` first (parallel sessions; head was 290, next free likely 291 вАФ VERIFY).

### 2026-06-10 вАФ WeeklyOrders AUDIT-RESIDUALS RULINGS (priv√© double-deplete ¬Ј empty-order/event-material ¬Ј week-scoped search). PM-ruled, LIVE-DB-VERIFIED, pre-build.
**Three audit residuals after the import. All verified against live prod 2026-06-10.**

**вС† PRIV√Й / SHOPIFY-PICKUP ORDERS вАФ ruled SAFE TO WRITE AS CUSTOMER ORDERS; NO double-deplete on these two rows.** The two sheet rows (r285 Jo√Ђl Golinucci ZEPF√Ч2 EMBF√Ч2; r298 Alice Buache ZEPF√Ч2 MOOF√Ч1) are **NOT in `inv_sales_orders`** (LIVE-VERIFIED: surname search Golinucci/Buache = 0 hits; only same-first-name strangers) вЖТ they are **manual sheet click&collect entries, NOT Shopify-synced** вЖТ writing them as `ord_orders` (order_type='customer') has **no eshop-leg twin вЖТ no double-deplete**. So 1c sub-option **(ii) is the correct one for these rows.**
  - **a. NO canonical "Priv√©" fold-account exists** вАФ Kouros's "fold to one account" premise is NOT current reality. Live: **83 `is_private=1` rows, one per individual, all `trade_channel='on_trade'`, no `bc_customer_no`** (the 89-priv√© needs_review bucket largely became these). **RULING: do NOT invent a single shared Priv√© account in this build** вАФ it would CONTRADICT the existing per-individual model + the no-fuzzy-link/never-guess canon, and there's no operator-confirmed merge map. Per-individual priv√© rows ARE the convention; create the 2 missing ones as their OWN `is_private=1` rows (name as on sheet, `is_active=1`, `trade_channel='on_trade'`, `bc_customer_no=NULL`) вАФ exactly like the 83 that exist. If Kouros truly wants ONE fold-account, that's a SEPARATE merge-decision arc (reuse the Carnet merge tool вЖТ tombstone individuals `merged_into:`), not a side-effect of this import. FLAG the contradiction to Kouros; do not resolve it by guessing.
  - **b. Individual name preservation:** the per-individual `ref_customers.name` already IS the name (no fold). If Kouros insists on folding, the name lives in the **`ord_orders.comment`** free-text (there is **NO `contact_name` column** on `ord_orders` вАФ LIVE-VERIFIED schema) вАФ do NOT add one for 2 rows.
  - **c. рЯФі THE DOUBLE-DEPLETE MECHANISM (durable, generalized):** `fg_stock_compute()` eshop leg depletes **ALL `inv_sales_orders WHERE channel='eshop' AND DATE(created_at) >= anchor`** вАФ it does **NOT filter `fulfillment_status`** (LIVE-VERIFIED query in `app/fg-stock.php` ~L482). So pickup-vs-ship is INVISIBLE to depletion: any eshop order in `inv_sales_orders` already depletes. **THE GATING RULE (canonical): an order belongs in `ord_orders` (B2B/expedie leg) XOR `inv_sales_orders` (eshop leg) вАФ NEVER both. The discriminator is membership in `inv_sales_orders`, not a flag we invent.** For THESE two rows: absent from `inv_sales_orders` вЖТ ord_orders write is safe. **FORWARD HAZARD (the вС£ Phase-2 gate, still ON HOLD):** once the Shopify pickup-signal rework lands and pickup orders DO sync into `inv_sales_orders`, writing the SAME pickup order to `ord_orders` for the picking workflow WOULD double-deplete. The clean solution at that time = pickup orders deplete via the eshop leg (already do), and the Exp√©ditions picking view READS them from `inv_sales_orders` (like the existing muted read-only eshop/taproom rows on the Commandes board, expeditions.php ~L1591) вАФ it does NOT re-create them as depleting `ord_orders`. Do NOT solve this now; it's gated on the Shopify rework. (Note: `internal_channel` ENUM already carries `'cage','shop'` beyond taproom/eshop вАФ but internal_channel is for `order_type='internal'`, a different fact; a priv√© pickup is a real customer sale, not internal.)
  - **d. Write path:** these 2 rows resolve to NO customer today вЖТ the importer bucketed them UNMATCHED (it has no "fold to Priv√©" path вАФ confirmed by the priv√©-not-validatedвЖТflag ruling #4). Convention-correct write = **create the 2 `is_private=1 ref_customers` rows first (Kouros-authorized, name-as-stated = NOT speculative), THEN re-run `import_weeklyorders.php --apply`** (idempotent on `source_ref`; resolver now matches the new rows; lines DGDF/ZEPF/EMBF/MOOF all resolve). Do NOT hand-write ord_orders bypassing the importer/resolver/event-cascade path.

**вС° EMPTY-ORDER ALLOCATION вАФ split: ONE is a real FG order, the rest are NON-PRODUCT event/marketing material that must NOT become FG order lines.**
  - **a. `DGDF` EXISTS** (LIVE-VERIFIED `ref_skus` id=9, recipe 31 DrunkBeard "Galactic Drift", format 15 = keg/Fass, is_active=1). So **r80 Street Cellar "3 Galac f√їts" вЖТ DGDF√Ч3 IS a valid FG order line** (Galac = Galactic Drift = the keg). Kouros's "Galac f√їts = DGDF" is CONFIRMED correct. This one row becomes a normal customer order.
  - **b. `Cuves`, `T7`, `Galac` are NOT sku_codes** (LIVE-VERIFIED: T7/CUVES/GALAC exact + substring = 0 hits in `ref_skus`). "Cuves" (r102 Jardins de Louis) and "T7" (r199 Gotham/Marketing, r223 Gotham + "1 pack dec gratuit√©") do NOT resolve to any SKU.
  - **c. рЯФі RULING вАФ event/serving/marketing material does NOT live in `ord_orders` and must NOT deplete FG.** "T7" (a serving-tank / tap-tower style equipment loan), "Cuves" (serving cuves = equipment, NOT the -V cuv SALE SKU), and marketing giveaways are **non-product / equipment / promo**, not Neb FG beer. Forcing them into `ord_orders` lines = wrongly depleting beer SKUs (the never-guess-a-mapping + one-fact-one-table rule). **DO NOT allocate T7/Cuves to beer SKUs.** Options to put to Kouros (do not guess which): (i) these are equipment loans вЖТ out of scope for `ord_orders` entirely (skip; they have no FG depletion fact); (ii) the "1 pack dec gratuit√©" on r223 IS a real product giveaway вЖТ route to the **`inv_side_stock_ledger` `movement_type='giveaway'`** path (mig 303, the unit-count giveaway ledger ¬ІITEM 2) keyed to the actual SKU, NOT an ord_orders line вАФ that's the canonical home for "offered/gratuit√©" units. The "3 Galac f√їts" (DGDF) is the ONLY one of the 4 empty-orders that is a real product order. **Keep the other 3 in the held-out bucket pending Kouros: equipment-loan-skip vs giveaway-ledger; never auto-allocate as beer SKUs.**

**вСҐ WEEK-SCOPED SEARCH (Blind Tigers) вАФ CONFIRMED root cause; fix = drop the date window when a client search term is present. In scope as a quick follow-up.**
  - **Root cause LIVE-VERIFIED** (`expeditions.php`): Commandes defaults `mode=week` / current ISO week (L1205); the Commandes query ALWAYS seeds `$where=['o.requested_date BETWEEN ? AND ?']` (L1475) and ANDs `c.name LIKE` onto it (L1479-1481). Blind Tigers #84/#85 are req_date 2026-06-29 (~3 wk out) вЖТ current-week window returns nothing despite a name match. (NB the Carnet-clients directory search L1884-1886 is already date-unscoped вАФ only the Commandes ORDER list is week-trapped.)
  - **HOUSE-PATTERN RULING: when a client search term is present, the client-name filter spans ALL dates вАФ suppress the `requested_date BETWEEN` clause (or widen to an all-time bound) for that query.** Rationale: a name search is an intent to FIND a specific client's orders, not to browse a week; the date window is a browse affordance, not a search constraint. This matches Kouros's expectation and the already-date-unscoped Carnet search. Keep the week/range nav for the no-search browse case. Preserve the SKU/statut/canal filters as-is. Small, surgical, low-risk; **YES in scope as a quick follow-up.** Do NOT build a separate global-search surface вАФ reuse the existing Commandes `client` filter, just un-gate the date window when it's non-empty. **EQUIP: coder + sql + ui + webapp-testing** (read-only prod smoke: search "Blind Tigers" with no kw вЖТ #84/#85 appear).

**SEQUENCING:** вС† + вС° are data + a re-run of the existing idempotent importer (no new build needed beyond creating the 2 priv√© rows + DGDF allocation + putting the T7/Cuves/giveaway question to Kouros). вСҐ is the only code change вАФ a surgical edit to one query's WHERE assembly in `expeditions.php`. None are gated on each other. вС† forward-hazard (pickup double-deplete) stays PARKED behind the Shopify rework (вС£ Phase 2).

### вЬЕвЬЕ WeeklyOrders AUDIT FULLY CLOSED 2026-06-10 (all outcomes VERIFIED LIVE ON PROD)
**Audited the WeeklyOrders sheet (correct tab `gid=1955899648` вАФ the gid in Kouros's URL doesn't exist as a tab) vs `ord_orders`.** Of the apparent misses: **r107 Ailec = NOT a gap** (operator entered the wrong date; same row as web #83 вАФ dropped). **4 orders written** via the importer path (`source='import'` + `source_ref` + events + site + audit, idempotent on `source_ref`); the rest correctly held.

**The 4 writes (verified live):**
- **#101 Street Cellar** (id 833) вЖР r80, **DGDF√Ч3** (resolves вС°a вАФ Galac f√їts = Galactic Drift keg, the real-FG empty-order).
- **#102 Jo√Ђl Golinucci** вЖР r285, **ZEPF√Ч2 EMBF√Ч2** вАФ NEW `is_private=1` customer **id 3058** (resolves вС†d for this row).
- **#103 Alice Buache** вЖР r298, **ZEPF√Ч2 MOOF√Ч1** вАФ NEW `is_private=1` customer **id 3059** (resolves вС†d).
- **#107 D√©partement Marketing** (id 673, BC 1807) вЖР r223, **PD8√Ч1** `line_comment='gratuit√© 100%'`, order comment names the Gotham recipient (resolves вС°c for the giveaway вАФ see NEW CONVENTION below).

**CONVENTION CONFIRMED вАФ priv√© = individual `is_private=1` rows** (Kouros option A), NOT a single fold-account. This ratifies ruling вС†a: the per-individual model stands; #3058/#3059 created exactly like the existing 83. (Kouros separately wants a Shopify-integration plan-mode later вАФ distinct future arc.)

**рЯЖХ NEW CONVENTION вАФ marketing giveaways (order-attached):** a 100%-rebate giveaway is booked as an `ord_orders` line to the central **D√©partement Marketing account (id 673, BC 1807)**, with the actual recipient named in the **order comment**, the **real SKU at real qty**, so that **ќ£(that account's lines √Ч SKU value) = the annual marketing-giveaway total.** This **SUPERSEDES** the earlier вС°c suggestion to route order-attached giveaways to `inv_side_stock_ledger movement_type='giveaway'` вАФ that ledger remains the home for loose-unit/non-order giveaways, but an order-attached giveaway is booked on the Marketing customer order. **`ord_order_lines` has NO price/rebate column** вАФ the 100% rebate is expressed via `line_comment='gratuit√© 100%'`; the value is DERIVABLE from SKU cost, not stored.

**SKU NOTE вАФ `PACKDEC` вЖТ `PD8`:** `PACKDEC` is an INACTIVE Shopify alias of the canonical active SKU **PD8 (id 137)** "Pack D√©couverte 8√Ч33cl" вАФ use PD8.

**вСҐ SEARCH FIX SHIPPED + DEPLOYED** (NOT committed вАФ parallel-session tree; `expeditions.php` Commandes): when a find-intent is active (client-name search, OR `status='ouvertes'`/`'expediees'`), the `requested_date BETWEEN <week>` clause is DROPPED so results span ALL dates; added a new **"Exp√©di√©es (toutes dates)"** status option; a **"R√©sultats вАФ toutes dates ¬Ј N"** banner + greyed-out week-nav when find-intent active; `LIMIT 500` surfaced. Browse-mode (no filter) unchanged. Fixes the "can't find Blind Tigers" symptom (#84/#85 dated 2026-06-29 were week-trapped). Matches the вСҐ house-pattern ruling above (un-gate the date window on search-intent; reuse the existing Commandes filter, no separate global-search surface).

**рЯФі IMPORTANT BUG RECORDED вАФ `import_weeklyorders.php` line-level idempotency is BROKEN (latent data-integrity risk).** `scripts/import_weeklyorders.php` (~L665) does a plain `INSERT INTO ord_order_lines (order_id_fk, sku_id_fk, qty)` with **NO `ON DUPLICATE KEY UPDATE` and NO UNIQUE on (order_id_fk, sku_id_fk)**. The HEADER is idempotent on `source_ref`, but the LINES are NOT вЖТ **re-running the importer DOUBLES every order's lines.** This actually bit us: an idempotency re-run doubled lines on #101/#102/#103 (DGDF√Ч3 became 2 rows, etc.); detected on verification and **deleted the dup line ids 314вАУ318 вАФ final state now correct.** **вЪ†пЄП This corrects the PM's prior "re-running import `--apply` is safe/idempotent" guidance вАФ that is WRONG at the LINE level** (only the header is idempotent). **RECOMMENDED FIX (do NOT apply yet вАФ needs team confirm):** add `UNIQUE KEY (order_id_fk, sku_id_fk)` + `ON DUPLICATE KEY UPDATE qty=VALUES(qty)`. **CAVEAT:** only safe if NO legitimate order ever carries the same SKU on two lines (different lot/tier/split) вАФ confirm with the team first. **Also note:** `log_revision` has no `'delete'` action (ENUM is insert/update only вАФ see migration-discipline canon), so the dup-line deletes were NOT audited.

### рЯФТ DURABLE RESOLVER RULE вАФ customer resolution MUST follow merge-tombstones to the canonical active record (REUSABLE вАФ all customer-resolving ingests inherit it)
**Generalizes the supplier-alias resolution rule to `ref_customers` + merge-tombstones. Record prominently вАФ this is a recurring-craft rule, candidate for the `sql`/`coder` skill if it bites a third surface.**

**RULE:** ANY customer resolution вАФ the WeeklyOrders importer, the future **commandes@ email-order ingest**, AND the **BC sales-ledger ingest** (the one ruled on in ¬ІITEM 1 / sales-commercial-surface) вАФ MUST:
1. **Follow `ref_customers.notes` `merged_into: N`** to the canonical record (depth-capped to avoid cycles), and
2. **REFUSE tombstoned (`is_active=0`) matches** вАФ never point an order/sale at a dead stub.

**WHY (the bug this prevents, observed in the original importer):** the first importer matched **tombstoned alias stubs** directly. Because a stub's id вЙ† its canonical's id, the `(customer_id_fk + date)` collision check **silently missed 7 of the 12 KW24 web-overlap duplicates** (stub-id never equals the web order's canonical customer_id_fk вЖТ no collision detected) AND would have written orders pointing at dead records. The merge-tombstone follow-through is what makes the collision check correct AND keeps FKs on live customers. **The BC sales-ledger ingest you ruled on (¬ІITEM 1) MUST inherit this exact rule when resolving N¬∞ origine вЖТ ref_customers** вАФ same tombstone-follow, same refuse-dead-stub discipline.

## 2026-06-09 вАФ ITEM 1: PER-SITE SALES ATTRIBUTION + INTER-SITE TRANSFERS вАФ FINAL SPEC (dispatch-blocking; Kouros's forks resolved)
**Scope = FULL** (transfers + per-order ship-from attribution); SKU total unchanged. Resolved against live code 2026-06-09.

**CODE-FACTS RESOLVED:**
1. **mig 294 `294_ord_orders_source_ref.sql` = `source_ref VARCHAR(190) NULL` + `UNIQUE uniq_ord_source_ref` вАФ the WeeklyOrders idempotency key (ruling #6), NOT a site/fulfilment column. ZERO collision with `fulfilment_site_id_fk`.** Both can ALTER ord_orders in separate migrations; additive ADD COLUMN, no overlap. Parallel session owns 294/295(submitted_by_user_fk on bd_*)/296(bbt_vide)/297(pertes threshold)/**298(journal_saisies, ALREADY taken locally)**. вЖТ THIS build's mig must be **вЙ•299** (verify at dispatch).
2. **Serving-tank-clients page = `public/modules/reglages-generaux.php` section `?sec=pkg_clients`** ("Clients packaging ¬Ј Livraison cuve de service ¬Ј venues ¬Ј festivals"), table `ref_packaging_clients` (mig 237; venues/events for cuv keg delivery; full CRUD: add ~L280, edit ~L315, toggle ~L337, list ~L1510+). **BUT: `ref_packaging_clients` = venues/events (cuv destinations), a DIFFERENT identity from `ref_customers` (B2B sold-to). The Nausikraft-delivered clients are `ref_customers` rows, NOT packaging-clients.** So the Nausikraft list is a SIBLING admin section on the same page (`?sec=` new tab) that flags `ref_customers` rows вАФ it mirrors the pkg_clients CRUD *pattern* but operates on `ref_customers`. (NB `ref_serving_tanks` mig 142 = in-house TANK capacity registry, irrelevant.)
3. **Order creation = `public/modules/expeditions.php`** saisie POST: INSERT `ord_orders` L521-551, UPDATE (edit) L467-490, lines DELETE+INSERT L497-551, status event L567. `transporter_id_fk` already follows the "customer default вЖТ per-order override" pattern вАФ **mirror it exactly for site.** `scripts/import_weeklyorders.php` is the bulk-import twin (must set fulfilment_site_id_fk via the resolver too).

**A. SCHEMA (types verified: `ref_customers.id` + `ref_sites.id` both `INT UNSIGNED`; `ord_orders.id` BIGINT UNSIGNED):**
- **`inv_stock_movements`** (NEW table) вАФ inter-site transfers: `id` BIGINT UNSIGNED PK; `sku_id_fk` INT UNSIGNED NOT NULL FKвЖТref_skus(id) RESTRICT; `from_site_id_fk` + `to_site_id_fk` INT UNSIGNED NOT NULL FKвЖТref_sites(id) RESTRICT (CHECK fromвЙ†to); `qty` DECIMAL(10,2) NOT NULL CHECK>0 (SKU units, mirror ord_order_lines); `moved_on` DATE NOT NULL; `comment` TEXT NULL; `is_tombstoned` TINYINT(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0 (admin tombstones, NEVER delete вАФ mirrors event-table discipline); `created_by_user_id` INT UNSIGNED NULL FKвЖТusers(id) SET NULL; created_at/updated_at. + schema_meta row (table_class='transactional', corrections_policy: tombstone-only). Both sites must `holds_fg_stock=1` (validate in handler, not CHECK).
- **`ord_orders.fulfilment_site_id_fk`** INT UNSIGNED NULL FKвЖТref_sites(id) ON DELETE RESTRICT (mirror `transporter_id_fk` nullability/FK-action). NULL = historical/pre-feature вЖТ resolver falls back to channel default at read. Separate migration from 294 вАФ no contention.
- **`ref_customers.default_delivery_site_id_fk`** INT UNSIGNED NULL FKвЖТref_sites(id) ON DELETE SET NULL (mirror `default_transporter_id_fk` exactly). This IS the "Nausikraft list" mechanism: Nausikraft-delivered clients = `ref_customers` rows with this set to the Nausikraft site (id4). NO separate flag/table вАФ a nullable default-site FK is the minimal, single-homed mechanism (mirrors the transporter default already proven). NULL = no client default вЖТ resolver uses channel default.

**B. RESOLVER (single source вАФ ONE helper both order-create-default AND snapshot-sales-attribution call):** `app/fulfilment-site.php` `resolve_fulfilment_site(PDO, $order_row): int` returning a ref_sites.id. **Precedence CONFIRMED (Kouros's inferred order is correct):**
  1. **per-order override** вАФ `ord_orders.fulfilment_site_id_fk` if NOT NULL (operator's explicit pick wins).
  2. **client default** вАФ `ref_customers.default_delivery_site_id_fk` (the Nausikraft list) if order_type='customer' and set.
  3. **channel default** вАФ wholesale/B2B (order_type='customer', no client default) вЖТ Crissier (warehouse, id2); internal eshop вЖТ Crissier (id2); internal taproom вЖТ Taproom (id3). (Kouros: eshop default=Crissier, taproom base=Taproom.)
  Channel-default site ids come from `ref_sites` (DB-derived by site_type/role, NOT hardcoded вАФ eshop/wholesaleвЖТwarehouse site, taproomвЖТpos site; if multiple, the canonical default is config вАФ recommend a `commissioning_settings` row or the lowest-sort warehouse). The resolver is PURE (no writes); used at order-create time to seed the selector default AND at fg-stock snapshot time to attribute sales.

**C. fg_stock_location_snapshot() sales attribution:** per-site sales = ќ£(sales legs) WHERE `resolve_fulfilment_site(order)` = this site. MUST reuse the ONE resolver (no inline channelвЖТsite map). Keep the ќ£(cards)==physique invariant: the prod leg already credits the production site; sales legs now SUBTRACT from the resolved ship-from site (today they subtract globally per ¬ІPRODUCTION-LEG FIX OPEN/DEFERRED вАФ THIS build closes that "sales-leg per-location settlement" carryover). Historical orders with NULL fulfilment_site вЖТ resolver returns channel default (step 3) вАФ never errors, always attributes. eshop=`inv_sales_orders`, taproom=`inv_sales_bc`, B2B=`ord_*` (R1 source map unchanged).

**D. DISPATCH SEQUENCE (Kouros's order CONFIRMED, one reorder note):** (1) migrations [inv_stock_movements + ord_orders.fulfilment_site_id_fk + ref_customers.default_delivery_site_id_fk вАФ 3 ALTERs/CREATE, can be ONE migration file or three; recommend ONE]; (2) **resolver helper `app/fulfilment-site.php`** (build BEFORE both consumers вАФ it's the single-source spine); (3) order-creation ship-from selector in expeditions.php (defaulted by resolver, overridable) вАФ **do this BEFORE snapshot attribution** so test orders carry real sites; (4) snapshot sales-attribution rewire (consumes resolver); (5) Nausikraft-client admin list on reglages-generaux.php (sets `ref_customers.default_delivery_site_id_fk`); (6) Mouvements transfer tab on expeditions.php (operators+ record; admin tombstone). **EQUIP per sub-build:** (1) sql+coder; (2) coder+sql; (3) coder+sql+ui+webapp-testing; (4) sql+coder+webapp-testing; (5) coder+sql+ui; (6) coder+sql+ui+webapp-testing.

**E. MIGRATION NUMBERS:** local head includes 298 (journal_saisies, parallel/untracked). NEXT FREE = **299** for this build (re-verify `migrate.php --status` + `ls db/migrations` AT DISPATCH вАФ parallel sessions lead; 294-298 all parallel/untracked). If three separate migs: 299/300/301; if one: 299. Recommend ONE migration `299_fulfilment_site_attribution.sql` (CREATE inv_stock_movements + 2 ADD COLUMN + 2 FK + schema_meta) вАФ atomic, fewer numbers to contend.

**F. LANDMINES:** (i) **ord_orders contention** вАФ do NOT touch 294's source_ref; your ADD COLUMN is independent; never re-ALTER in a way that re-declares their column. (ii) **single-resolver** вАФ order-create default and sales-attribution MUST call the same `resolve_fulfilment_site()`; an inline duplicate map = the divergent-store anti-pattern вЖТ cards/total drift. (iii) **beer-tax neutrality** вАФ site attribution is a LOCATION fact, not a quantity fact; total packaged-HL and beer-tax base unchanged (ќ£ across sites = same total). (iv) **no parallel FG-depletion path** (R1) вАФ `inv_stock_movements` is a TRANSFER (moves stock between sites, net-zero to global physique), NOT a sale; it must NOT enter the global depletion legs, only shift the per-site split. fg_stock_compute() global total ignores transfers; ONLY fg_stock_location_snapshot() applies them (+to_site, вИТfrom_site). (v) **Nausikraft identity** вАФ Nausikraft is BOTH a `ref_sites` row (id4 consignment, customer_id_fk=1) AND its delivered clients are `ref_customers` вАФ don't conflate; the client list sets `default_delivery_site_id_fk=4`. (vi) **import_weeklyorders.php** must also resolve+set fulfilment_site_id_fk (else bulk-imported orders all NULLвЖТchannel-default, acceptable but flag). (vii) **transfers vs cuv** вАФ cuv (serving-tank) is filled-at-client = already excluded from FG; a transfer of FG between sites is distinct, don't let cuv leak into inv_stock_movements.

## вЬЕ TASK A SHIPPED 2026-06-10 вАФ same-day cutoff fix (eshop symmetric + transfer net-zero unit-gate); commit `2192153` origin/main; NO migration; data-layer only (`app/fg-stock.php`); EQUIP coder+sql
Closes KNOWN LIMITATION 1 of ITEM 1 for the **eshop + transfer** legs вАФ built to the PM (A)-corrected ruling exactly. The bug class: `fg_stock_compute()` (the consumption-stock derivation Tap&Shop + others call) and `fg_stock_location_snapshot()` (the per-site card view) used DIVERGENT same-day cutoff logic on the eshop leg вЖТ ќ£cards could drift from ќ£physique inside the same-day window; and the snapshot transfer leg admitted +to/вИТfrom per-side, so per-site anchor divergence could break per-row net-zero.

**FIX 1 вАФ eshop leg made SYMMETRIC (compute now mirrors snapshot).** `fg_stock_compute()` Step 5 (eshop) now uses the IDENTICAL per-(sku, warehouse-site) `>=` + `created_at` tiebreak as the snapshot eshop leg: built `fg_site_sku_anchor_map()` + one `resolve_fulfilment_site(['channel'=>'eshop'])` call at the top of Step 5; per-row pass test against that map; **fallback = strict `> $anchorDate`** for SKUs with no warehouse count. Symmetric by construction вЖТ ќ£cards==ќ£physique holds under the same-day window.

**FIX 2 вАФ snapshot transfer leg = atomic per-row UNIT-GATE.** `$fromPass`/`$toPass` still computed per-side from each site's per-SKU anchor, but admission is atomic: `$rowPass = ($fromPass || $toPass)`; both +qty(to) and вИТqty(from) apply together or neither вЖТ per-row net-zero GUARANTEED regardless of per-site anchor divergence. Compute stays transfer-exempt by construction (no transfer term вАФ correct; transfers are net-zero to global physique per ITEM 1 landmine-(iv)).

**FIX 3 вАФ SCOPE NOTE at top of `fg_stock_compute` rewritten** to the as-built PER-LEG cutoff table: eshop = per-site symmetric; B2B = strict-global symmetric; taproom = month-grained (deferred); transfers = unit-gate net-zero, compute-exempt.

**Intentionally UNCHANGED:** B2B leg (strict-global symmetric) + taproom leg (month-grained). These are NOT the same-day class.

**вЪ†пЄП ACCEPTED TRADE-OFF (PM-ruled acceptable):** the transfer unit-gate sacrifices per-site precision in the rare case of a same-day INBOUND transfer to a `to_site` that was ALSO counted later that same day вЖТ that card transiently OVERCOUNTS by qty until its next count, in exchange for the HARD global net-zero invariant. Per-site same-day-transfer settlement remains the DEFERRED stock-movement-saisie refinement.

**VERIFICATION (real, not empty-window):** synthetic same-day fixture вАФ eshop order (SKU60 qty5, today after warehouse anchor_ts) + a **DIVERGENT-ANCHOR transfer** (SKU39: from site2 counted 06-08, to site3 counted 06-09 12:43, moved_on 06-09 08:00 вЖТ fromPass=T / toPass=F). **10/10 assertions:** baseline 8599==8599; with fixtures ќ£cards==ќ£physique held; eshop physique вИТ5 exactly; transfer global unchanged (74) + cards ¬±5 net-zero; teardown restored baseline; no stray scripts. **The divergent-anchor transfer fixture WAS constructible** (PM-flagged to confirm) вАФ site2 warehouse vs site3 taproom anchors give the T/F split.

**Status:** Task A had NO migration вЖТ MIGRATION HEAD stays **299**. KNOWN LIMITATION 1 (eshop+transfer same-day) now CLOSED. Remaining deferred: per-site same-day TRANSFER precision (unit-gate trade-off) + taproom month-granularity.

## рЯЯҐ OUT-OF-ORDER TRANSFER ANALYSIS (2026-06-15, PM trace vs LIVE fg-stock.php + expeditions.php; NO code change вАФ analysis only) вАФ "move FG before the same-day packaging form is entered"
**Scenario:** team records a RenensвЖТCrissier transfer of a beer being packaged the SAME day, BEFORE the packaging form lands. As-built reaction (VERIFIED against live VPS code, not theory):
- **Movement form is NOT stock-gated.** `add_movement` (expeditions.php L989+) validates ONLY: active SKU, both sites `holds_fg_stock=1`, fromвЙ†to, qty integer >0, `moved_on` sane (not future / not <2020). **NO source-stock check** вАФ any active SKU/qty moves regardless of recorded on-hand. The `EXP_MOV_STOCK_MAP` over-transfer hint (L6458, JS) is **advisory amber only, NEVER blocks** (overselling/over-moving is legal вАФ production may be planned). So the move is NOT blocked.
- **It does NOT drive stock negative or strand.** The inter-site transfer leg lives in `fg_stock_location_snapshot()` ONLY (compute() is transfer-EXEMPT, transfers net-zero to global physique вАФ ITEM 1 landmine-(iv)). It applies as an **atomic per-row UNIT-GATE** (Task A FIX 2): `$rowPass = ($fromPass || $toPass)` вЖТ BOTH +qty(to_site) and вИТqty(from_site) apply together or neither вЖТ **per-row net-zero GUARANTEED**, ќ£cards==ќ£physique HELD regardless of which/whether the packaging exists yet. Cards CAN read negative (intentional honest signal, explicit `SCOPE NOTE: do NOT clamp to 0`, fg-stock.php ~L1391) but global is never corrupted.
- **No replay-ordering dependency.** Transfer gate is `moved_on >= anchorDate` + per-site DATE/created_at tiebreak вАФ date-keyed, NOT insert-order. Production credit lands at the **production site (Renens, DB-derived `site_type='production'`)** via `fg_prod_since_anchor()` keyed on packaging `event_date`. So **same-day input order does not matter to the end state.**
- **END STATE after packaging lands = CORRECT, self-healing, no defect.** Sequence: (1) transfer entered first вЖТ Renens card shows вИТqty (the moved units not yet produced), Crissier card +qty, ќ£ unchanged; (2) packaging form lands later same day вЖТ `fg_prod_since_anchor` credits +production to Renens вЖТ the transient вИТqty nets back up. No double-count (transfer is net-zero, never enters depletion legs), no strand (qty is at Crissier as intended), no global negative. The ONLY artifact is a **transient negative Renens card visible in the window between the two entries** вАФ cosmetic, self-resolving, honest.
- **Guards/visibility:** no review-queue flag, no negative-stock alert fires for this; the operator sees the advisory amber over-move hint on the movement form (if qty>live_futur) and the transient negative card on the Stock-PF snapshot. Both are signals, not errors.
- **RISK RANK: LOW / non-defect.** The architecture (transfer in snapshot-only + atomic net-zero unit-gate + production keyed on event_date not insert-order) makes the out-of-order case self-correct. **Lightest "fix" if the transient-negative cosmetics ever bother the operator:** none needed for correctness; could soften the snapshot card to annotate "en attente de conditionnement" when a negative is fully explained by same-day transfers exceeding counted+produced вАФ pure display, no model change. Do NOT add a hard stock-gate to the movement form (would break the legal "move planned production" workflow + contradict the never-block-overselling ruling).

## рЯФі B2B EXPEDIE LEG = REAL COMPUTATION BUG (2026-06-10 вАФ SUPERSEDES the earlier "label-only" / "intentionally-deferred B2B remainder" finding)
**The earlier ruling that the B2B same-day case was a benign deferred remainder ("count already reflects the shipment, double-count-safe") was WRONG.** Operator + live DOAF (sku 20) raw data confirm a genuine miscomputation. RECLASSIFIED: this is a CORRECTNESS bug in `fg_stock_compute()` Step 4 (and symmetrically in `fg_stock_location_snapshot()` Leg 1), NOT a label issue and NOT acceptably-deferred.

**ROOT CAUSE (CONFIRMED).** Step 4 deducts shipped B2B orders with `o.requested_date > $anchorDate` where `$anchorDate` = the **GLOBAL `MAX(counted_at)` across ALL sites** (fg-stock.php L276). The anchor SUM is correctly per-(sku,location), but the B2B cutoff is global. DOAF anchors: loc1 Production 06-08 (8), loc2 Warehouse 06-08 (36), loc3 Taproom 06-09 (1) вЖТ global anchorDate = **06-09** (polluted by Taproom counting a day later). ord#4 (req 06-08, shipped, 6u) fails `06-08 > 06-09` вЖТ NOT deducted вЖТ physique stuck at 45. Reality: warehouse+production were counted 06-08, the 6 shipped from them on 06-08 is NOT in those 06-08 counts вЖТ it MUST come off. **This is the exact production-leg pollution class that `566b9d3` already fixed for the production leg вАФ the B2B leg is the LAST surviving global-cutoff leg that has a per-site finer anchor available** (eshop closed by Task A; prod by 566b9d3/d3fb954).

**RULING вАФ the canonical fix is per-(sku, ship-from-site) anchor cutoff on the B2B leg, mirroring how the prod + eshop legs already settle.** Use the SAME `fg_site_sku_anchor_map()` the eshop leg + snapshot already build. The ship-from site = `resolve_fulfilment_site()` for the order (fulfilment_site_id_fk вЖТ customer default_delivery_site вЖТ channel default), which the snapshot Leg 1 ALREADY computes per order. Predicate becomes per-row: deduct when `requested_date > siteAnchorDate(ship-from)`, with **COALESCEвЖТglobal `$anchorDate`** for SKUs uncounted at that site (mirrors prod-leg COALESCE fallback). For DOAF: ord#4 ships from warehouse (loc2, anchor 06-08) вЖТ `06-08 > 06-08`? NO under strict `>`. вЖТ SAME-DAY BOUNDARY MUST BE RULED (below).

**SAME-DAY BOUNDARY RULING вАФ option (a): per-location anchor + INCLUSIVE `requested_date >= siteAnchorDate` for the B2B leg.** Operator needs the same-day-as-warehouse-anchor shipment (ord#4, req 06-08 == warehouse anchor 06-08) deducted. The created_at tiebreak the eshop leg uses is NOT available here вАФ the existing comment is correct that `ord_orders.created_at` is ENTRY time (back-datable), so it can't order a same-day ship vs count. Two sub-cases at the same calendar day: (i) order shipped from a site BEFORE that site's count that day вЖТ already in the count, must NOT re-deduct; (ii) shipped AFTER the count вЖТ not in count, must deduct. With only DATE granularity we cannot distinguish (i) from (ii). **OPERATOR'S OPERATIONAL MODEL resolves the tie: a same-day shipment is NOT yet reflected in that day's count (the count is a morning/point-in-time snapshot, shipments flow after) вЖТ default to DEDUCT same-day вЖТ inclusive `>=` on the SHIP-FROM site's anchor.** This does NOT reintroduce the genuine "shipped strictly BEFORE an earlier count" double-count: an order with `requested_date < siteAnchorDate` still fails `>=` and stays in the count (correct вАФ a 06-05 shipment is already absent from a 06-08 count). Option (b) (keep `>` but de-pollute the global max) would still drop the legitimate same-day ord#4; option (c) (explicit ship timestamp) is the eventual real fix but needs a SOURCE column (no DATETIME ship-time exists) вАФ DEFER, not required now. **CANONICAL = (a).**

**ACCEPTED RESIDUAL (inclusive `>=` trade-off, PM-ruled OK).** A B2B order shipped from a site on the same calendar day, where that shipment WAS already physically captured in that day's count, will be double-deducted (counted-out AND deducted). This is the symmetric inverse of the eshop residual and is rare (same-site count + same-day pre-count ship). Accept it for the operator's stated default (count = point-in-time, ships flow after). The only true fix is a ship timestamp (option c) вАФ log as the deferred precision item, same bucket as taproom month-granularity.

**Q3 вАФ SNAPSHOT IS NOT ALREADY RIGHT; both functions share the SAME global-cutoff B2B leg вЖТ they are SYMMETRIC, so there is NO ќ£cards != ќ£physique divergence today.** Verified in code: snapshot Leg 1 (L859-884) uses identical `o.requested_date > ?` against the same global `$anchorDate` (L832-836). So the invariant ќ£cards==ќ£physique HOLDS through this bug (both under-deduct ord#4 identically) вАФ which is precisely why the bug is invisible to the invariant gate and only the operator's ground-truth catches it. **CONSEQUENCE: the fix must land in BOTH legs in lockstep (compute Step 4 AND snapshot Leg 1) to PRESERVE symmetry.** Fixing only one breaks ќ£cards==ќ£physique. This is a both-functions fix, NOT compute-only.

**FIX LOCUS (precise).** `app/fg-stock.php`: (1) `fg_stock_compute()` Step 4 (~L370-390) вАФ the `o.requested_date > ?` global predicate; (2) `fg_stock_location_snapshot()` Leg 1 (~L859-884) вАФ the matching `o.requested_date > ?`. Snapshot Leg 1 ALREADY resolves the per-order ship-from site (`resolve_fulfilment_site`, L887) and ALREADY builds `fg_site_sku_anchor_map()` (L842) вАФ so the snapshot has every input; compute Step 4 must add the same per-row resolve + map lookup (compute currently SUM/GROUPs in SQL вАФ it will need to fetch per-order rows like the snapshot does, or resolve ship-from per (order) before aggregating). Update the SCOPE NOTE B2B bullet (L300-303) from "strict-global > (symmetric)" to "per-(sku, ship-from-site) anchor, inclusive >= same-day, COALESCEвЖТglobal; symmetric across both functions". Adjust comments at L859-864 (which currently justify the strict-`>` no-tiebreak as correct) to the new ruling.

**INVARIANTS THAT MUST NOT BREAK (canonical stock SoT):** (1) ќ£cards==ќ£physique вАФ fix both legs in lockstep; (2) the genuine "shipped strictly before a count" guard вАФ orders with requested_date < ship-from anchor stay un-deducted (the `>=`/`>` boundary only changes SAME-day behavior); (3) eshop + transfer same-day handling untouched (Task A); (4) beer-tax neutrality (location/cutoff fact, not a quantity fact вАФ total deducted qty changes only by genuinely-missed same-day ships, which is the correct correction); (5) no new FG-depletion path / single-home (R1) вАФ this is a predicate change inside the one existing B2B leg, no new store.

**THE 36-vs-39 GAP: NOT mine to resolve вАФ operator ground-truth.** Operator: "45 вИТ 6 on Monday вЖТ 36 today" but 45вИТ6=39. The 3-unit gap is invisible in the DB (no June flows: physique=45=anchor exactly). DO NOT invent a flow to close it. Orchestrator reconciles with operator (hypotheses: operator tracks warehouse loc2=36 as the operational number with 6 shipped from production loc1; or the 45 aggregation itself is being read differently). The compute fix makes physique = 45 вИТ 6 = **39** (ord#4 deducted), which is the architecturally-correct number; the operator's "36" is a separate reconciliation, NOT a target the code should hit.

**EQUIP: sql + coder + webapp-testing.** BOTH compute + snapshot (not compute-only). No migration (predicate change, data-layer `app/fg-stock.php` only вАФ DATETIME ship-time is the DEFERRED option-c, not this fix). Verification gate: synthetic divergent-anchor B2B fixture (warehouse 06-08 + taproom 06-09, shipped order req 06-08) вЖТ ord#4-class order DEDUCTED; ќ£cards==ќ£physique held; an order req < ship-from anchor NOT deducted (guard intact); teardown clean. DOAF live check: physique 45вЖТ39 after fix.

### вЬЕ SHIPPED + OPERATOR-CONFIRMED 2026-06-10 вАФ B2B expedie per-(sku, ship-from-site) anchor fix is LIVE and SETTLED
**The fix landed and is CORRECT per the operator.** Operator's verbatim ruling: *"inventory take is always at start of week. following orders, even same day, must deduct."* вЖТ the start-of-week count is the baseline; same-day-and-later shipments deduct. **LIVE-VERIFIED: DOAF (sku 20) physique = 39** (Zeubi warehouse 36 вИТ 6 Monday ship = 30; Production 8; Taproom 1); deployed + ќ£cards==ќ£physique held 7455==7455.
- **рЯФІ AS-BUILT = THREE-tier predicate (CORRECTS the earlier 2-tier ruling above; the 2-tier `>=`/COALESCEвЖТglobal model is SUPERSEDED).** Implemented IDENTICALLY in BOTH `fg_stock_compute()` Step 4 AND `fg_stock_location_snapshot()` Leg 1 (symmetric, lockstep вАФ invariant preserved):
  - **(a) SKU counted at the ship-from site** вЖТ `requested_date >= site_anchor_date` (INCLUSIVE вАФ operator's same-day-deducts model).
  - **(b) SKU counted elsewhere but NOT at this site** вЖТ `requested_date >= global anchorDate` (INCLUSIVE).
  - **(c) SKU NEVER counted anywhere** вЖТ `requested_date > global anchorDate` (STRICT `>`). Needed to keep ќ£cards==ќ£physique for never-counted SKUs (e.g. ZEPV sku 61): their anchor-date shipments would otherwise deduct ASYMMETRICALLY вАФ in the snapshot (вЖТ negative row) but NOT in compute (dropped via `!isset($byId)`). Tier (c) preserves the pre-fix behaviour for untracked SKUs and restores symmetry.
- The earlier "label-only / double-count-safe / intentionally-deferred remainder" finding (above ¬ІB2B EXPEDIE LEG header) is **FULLY SUPERSEDED** вАФ the bug was real, the fix is per-(sku,ship-from-site) anchor, and tier (c) is the symmetry-preserving addition the 2-tier ruling missed for never-counted SKUs. The ACCEPTED RESIDUAL (same-day pre-count ship double-deduct, option-c ship-timestamp the eventual real fix) STILL stands and is unchanged. Only same-day TRANSFER precision + taproom month-granularity remain deferred.

## рЯФі ANCHOR TIEBREAK BUG вАФ `MAX(id)` вЙ† latest COUNT вЖТ stale-count inflates the anchor (LOCALIZED 2026-06-12, PM read-only probe; operator-flagged via DOAF).
**Operator audit 2026-06-12: "DOAF (Double Oat 20L keg) is NOT 83 across all stocks вАФ inflated."** PM live-probe CONFIRMS 83 IS the bug, ground truth = 45. ROOT CAUSE: `fg_stock_compute()` / `fg_stock_location_snapshot()` define the per-(sku,location) anchor as **`MAX(id)` among `is_active=1`**, NOT `MAX(counted_at)`. When a location has >1 active count and they were INSERTED out of count-date order, `MAX(id)` picks the row with the highest **autoincrement id**, which is NOT necessarily the latest **physical count**.
- **DOAF (sku_id_fk=20, recipe_id=30, format_id=15 Keg 20L, scope='base') live rows:** loc1 Production = id27 (April, inactive) + **id377 counted 2026-05-31 qty 46 (active)** + **id286 counted 2026-06-08 qty 8 (active)**; loc2 Zeubi/Logistique = id209 counted 06-08 qty 36; loc3 Taproom = id320 counted 06-09 qty 1; loc4 Nausikraft = none.
- **The defect:** loc1 `MAX(id)=377` вЖТ anchor uses the 05-31 count of **46**, IGNORING the genuinely-later 06-08 count of **8** (id286 < id377 because the May row was entered AFTER the June row). Anchor = 46+36+1 = **83 (WRONG)**. Correct anchor (latest count = `MAX(counted_at)`, tiebreak `MAX(id)`) = 8+36+1 = **45**.
- **Why `MAX(id)` was chosen:** it was a same-day tiebreak (Task A / Option-2, `created_at`-as-tiebreak narrative). It is RIGHT for two counts on the SAME date, WRONG as the PRIMARY order key вАФ count recency must be `counted_at` FIRST, then id as the same-date tiebreak. The arc header (L11-22 of app/fg-stock.php) literally says "anchor = latest count per (sku, location) вАФ MAX(id) per pair" вАФ the doc conflates "latest count" with "MAX(id)". They diverge exactly when an older-dated count is inserted later (backfill, correction, parallel-run).
- **Naive `SUM(qty) WHERE is_active=1` = 91** (all 4 active rows incl. BOTH loc1 rows double-counted) вАФ that is the OTHER wrong number; neither 91 nor 83 is right; **45** is.
- **FIX (the correct anchor subquery):** per (sku, location), pick the row with `MAX(counted_at)`, tiebreak `MAX(id)` for same-date. NOT `MAX(id)` alone. Apply IDENTICALLY in BOTH `fg_stock_compute()` AND `fg_stock_location_snapshot()` (the ¬ІB2B invariant-coupling rule вАФ byte-symmetric or ќ£cardsвЙ†ќ£physique). The flow-window start (anchor_date) ALSO derives from this row's `counted_at` вЖТ fixing the tiebreak auto-fixes the depletion window. **EQUIP: sql + coder + webapp-testing.** No migration (data-layer predicate). Verify: DOAF anchor 83вЖТ45; ќ£cards==ќ£physique held; spot-check other SKUs with >1 active count per location (correction/backfill candidates) didn't shift wrongly. рЯФі Opus verifies INDEPENDENTLY (FG/COGS-adjacent вАФ the anchor feeds the COGS-fiche FG census).
- **вЪ†пЄП INTERACTS with the never-counted-SKU gap below (do NOT conflate):** that one is a ROW-EXISTENCE asymmetry for scope='none' SKUs; THIS one is a wrong-row pick for SKUs WITH counts. Both live in the same two functions; a combined fix pass is reasonable but they are DISTINCT defects.

## рЯФі NEVER-COUNTED-SKU ROW-EXISTENCE ASYMMETRY = the ќ£cardsвЙ†ќ£physique gap (LOCALIZED 2026-06-12, PM read-only probe). NOT same-day; NOT a predicate boundary; tier-(c)'s "restores symmetry" claim was WRONG.
**Live state 2026-06-12: ќ£physique(compute)=8177 vs ќ£cards(snapshot)=6255 вЖТ GAP 1922** (the operator's "22" was an earlier, smaller instance of the SAME class; magnitude grew with new ZEPV sales). Root cause is NOT a same-day cutoff and NOT the `>=`/`>` boundary вАФ it is a **ROW-EXISTENCE asymmetry between the two functions for SKUs that have NO anchor row anywhere** (`inv_fg_stocktake` has zero active rows for them; here `stocktake_scope='none'` cuve SKUs):
- **Dominant: ZEPV (sku 61, "Cuve de service", scope='none', NEVER counted).** Two B2B `shipped` orders req 2026-06-11 (1000 + 900 = 1900). `fg_stock_location_snapshot()` Leg 1 tier (c) (strict `>` global anchor 06-09; 06-11>06-09 passes) **manufactures NEGATIVE cards from the sales side alone** вАФ вИТ1000 at Zeubi warehouse (ship-from) + вИТ900 at Nausikraft consignment вАФ ќ£ вИТ1900. `fg_stock_compute()` deducts the same 1900 but the SKU **has no anchor entry, so Step 9 NEVER EMITS A ROW for it** (`!isset($byId[sku])` вЖТ dropped) вЖТ contributes **0** to ќ£physique. compute=0, snapshot=вИТ1900 вЖТ 1900 of the 1922 gap. **The вИТ112 on the Nausikraft consignment card is purely this (sales-only negatives on a never-anchored site).**
- **Tail (the other 22): sku 62/64/66/68/69/70/71/72/74/77/297/302** вАФ same class, 1вАУ4 units each, never-counted cuve/keg SKUs whose handful of B2B/eshop sales the snapshot admits as small negatives while compute drops the row. **THIS tail IS the operator's original "22-unit gap."** So the headline 1922 = 1900 (ZEPV alone) + 22 (the long-standing tail).
- **WHY tier (c) did NOT fix it (the recorded reasoning at ¬ІB2B вА¶THREE-tier (c) is mis-stated):** tier (c) only changes the *predicate boundary* to strict `>`. But ZEPV's orders are req 06-11, comfortably **>** the 06-09 global anchor вАФ they PASS tier (c) in BOTH functions identically. The divergence is downstream of the predicate: the **snapshot emits a row whenever a leg touches a (site,sku) pair** (sales create negative rows), whereas **compute only emits rows seeded by a positive anchor**. For a never-counted SKU there is no seed вЖТ compute has no row to deduct from вЖТ 0; the snapshot has nothing but the deduction вЖТ negative. Predicate symmetry вЙ† row-set symmetry. **The arc's line-560 claim "tier (c) preserves вА¶ ќ£cards==ќ£physique for never-counted SKUs" is FALSIFIED by live data вАФ correct it when the fix lands.**
**рЯФі OPERATOR-CORRECTED RESOLUTION (2026-06-12, PM-ratified) вАФ supersedes options (1)/(2) below.** Operator reframed + PM live-probe CONFIRMED: the 13 divergent SKUs are NOT "missing counts" вАФ they **legitimately do not belong in the packaged-FG depletion model at all**. All 13 carry `stocktake_scope='none'` + `is_direct_sales=1` and split into two classes: **ZEPV (61)** = -V cuve, goes BBTвЖТclient direct, never passes a packaged-inventory stage (belongs in WIP/liquid COGS + beer-tax via HL, already excluded once gated); **12 tail (62/64/66/68/69/70/71/72/74/77/297/302, format_id 2=B12 / 4=4PB)** = Shopify bundle SKUs whose real packaged inventory is the COMPONENT bottles, not the bundle line. вЯє **the FIX is to GATE the FG-depletion legs on `stocktake_scope != 'none'`** (don't deplete packaged FG by a SKU that isn't packaged-inventorised), NOT to surface them as honest negatives. This makes the derived FG view's membership predicate match the canonical fact the column already owns (one-fact-one-table; refuse-don't-NULL spirit preserved вАФ we're not zeroing a real depletion, we're declaring non-membership).
  - **Discriminator = `stocktake_scope` (CANONICAL), NOT `is_non_stock`.** Live: `stocktake_scope` fully populated across all 182 active SKUs (base 52 / cage 42 / none 61 / single 27); **`is_non_stock=1` on ZERO rows** вАФ it was mig 322 for T7 tap machines, but T7 was ruled OUT of `ref_skus` entirely (¬ІвС° equipment ruling), so the flag is inert and the eshop leg's existing `rs.is_non_stock = 0` filter defends a class that doesn't exist. Replace that dead filter with `stocktake_scope != 'none'` (or AND them). Flag-hygiene: decide `is_non_stock` fate w/ operator (backfill-from-scope OR scrap вЖТ scrapping-backlog RULE 1); do NOT split the gate across both flags.
  - **WHICH LEGS (verified against live `app/fg-stock.php`):** GATE the 3 SALES legs вАФ **Step 4/Leg 1 (B2B)** [ZEPV's path], **Step 5/Leg 2 (eshop)** [the 12 tail's path; replace the dead is_non_stock filter here], **Step 6/Leg 3 (taproom)** [no scope=none rows today but gate for symmetry] вАФ in **BOTH functions, identically** (the ¬ІB2B invariant-coupling rule: predicate must stay byte-symmetric or ќ£cardsвЙ†ќ£physique). Gate at the leg level so `salesBySiteSku` never contains a scope=none SKU вЖТ the snapshot's "sales-but-no-anchor вЖТ create row" block (~L1285-1316, the actual phantom factory) never synthesizes them. ALSO add the predicate to **Step 3 production leg** for defense (today it already excludes via run_type='cuv'/no-events). **Do NOT gate the TRANSFER leg** (unit-gated net-zero by design; scope=none SKUs shouldn't appear there, and gating risks breaking the atomic from/to pairing).
  - **рЯЯҐ SEPARATION PROVEN (the pressure-test that validates the gate):** live snapshot shows 18 negative rows / 17 SKUs = TWO classes. The gate removes ONLY the 13 scope=none phantoms (ZEPV вИТ1900, bundles вИТ1..вИТ4). It correctly LEAVES UNTOUCHED the genuine honest-negatives on REAL inventoried SKUs вАФ **ALTB(2,base вИТ1), DGDF(9,base вИТ3), DIB4(10,base вИТ2/75), STI4C(52,base вИТ6/30)** вАФ which are the designed "shipped from a site with less attributed than was there" signal (per-order site override + transfers correct those). `scope != 'none'` cleanly splits suppress-phantom from keep-honest-negative.
**SUPERSEDED EARLIER OPTIONS (kept for context, do NOT implement):** ~~(1) compute emits a negative row for any leg-touched SKU~~ / ~~(2) snapshot suppresses sales-only negatives for never-counted SKUs~~ вАФ both treated the 13 as un-anchored-but-belong; operator clarified they DON'T belong. The line-560 "tier (c) preserves ќ£cards==ќ£physique for never-counted SKUs" claim stays FALSIFIED; correct it when the gate lands.
**eshop-BUNDLE COMPONENT DECOMPOSITION = DEFERRED to Phase 4 (cage engine), NOT this fix.** A bundle sale DOES consume real packaged goods (component bottles + cage + box + labels) вАФ correct model = BOM decomposition (bundle sale вЖТ COMPONENT inventory drawdown), which is the вС£-Phase 2 cage/box/COGS engine (gated on 2026-06-15 cage anchor + Shopify pickup-signal ON HOLD). **Prerequisite before ANY bundleвЖТcomponent build = settle the baseвЖФsingleвЖФbundle UNIT NESTING** (24вЖТ1вЖТ12/4 ladder; which SKU is inventory-of-record) вАФ same dimension-discipline gate as F2; a "quick" bundleвЖТsingle decompose before that = the 24√Ч collapse hazard (`942431e` class). Base/single bottles ARE inventoried + anchored (DIBBU qty 33, etc.) so the target inventory exists. **Flag the "component depletion via eshop bundles not yet reflected" gap to operator NOW вАФ do not silently close it** (this was already the recorded вС£-Phase 2 position).
**EQUIP: sql + coder + webapp-testing** (+ ui only if `?view=stock` needs blank-state handling for the now-absent rows). No migration (data-layer `app/fg-stock.php`, predicate change in both fns + dead-filter swap). Verification gate (рЯФі Opus verifies INDEPENDENTLY вАФ COGS-adjacent): (a) zero negative rows from scope=none SKUs; (b) the 4 genuine honest-negatives ALTB/DGDF/DIB4/STI4C UNCHANGED; (c) `ќ£(snapshot per-sku) == compute physique per-sku` for every scope!=none SKU; (d) ќ£cards==ќ£physique to the unit. Probe recipe (read-only, reusable): `fg_stock_compute()` ќ£physique vs `fg_stock_location_snapshot()` ќ£total_units, then per-SKU diff.

## вЬЕ ROLE-BASED DUAL STOCK VISUALS вАФ SHIPPED + LIVE + COMMITTED 2026-06-10 (matched the PM ruling; NO migration; data/render-layer only; EQUIP coder+sql+ui +webapp-testing)
**As-built (LIVE-verified end-to-end on prod data):** each user now sees **physique total + their home-site physique** on the Exp√©ditions stock surfaces, home-site DERIVED teamвЖТsite_type per the ruling below вАФ NO new column, NO migration, zero new compute/store. Built exactly to the ruling (R1 single-home untouched, no second FG-depletion path).
- **Helper `exp_user_home_site_type(array $user): ?string` вАФ TOP-LEVEL** in `public/modules/expeditions.php` (top-level per the nested-fn-fatal lesson). Precedence: (1) `users.manager_scope` (`production`вЖТproduction, `logistics`вЖТwarehouse, `all`вЖТ**NULL** [all-scope = no single home вЖТ all-sites default, per ruling #4]); (2) else `ref_access_presets.preset_key` via `access_preset_id_fk` (`production_operator`вЖТproduction, `logistics_operator`вЖТwarehouse, `marketing`вЖТpos, else NULL). **preset_key resolved once per request via one prepared SELECT** on `access_preset_id_fk` (string key, not numeric id вАФ ruling honored).
- **`exp_resolve_home_site($snapshot, $siteType)`** matches the snapshot location by `site_type` вЖТ `{units,name}`, sourced from `fg_stock_location_snapshot()` (NO re-query, NO compute change вАФ ruling #3).
- **Renders on BOTH views:** `?view=stock` header (`exp-st-home-site` KPI) and `?view=commandes` pinned strip (`exp-cmd-stock-strip__kpi--home`); the commandes view got a `fg_stock_location_snapshot()` call ADDED (was missing per ruling #5). Both null-guarded вЖТ admin/all-scope sees total + all-sites, no home KPI (ruling #4). CSS in `public/css/expeditions.css` (oak-tint accent + responsive variants). Labels use canonical `ref_sites.name` from the snapshot (no-DB-nomenclature, ruling #6).
- **LIVE-verified:** Nathan(logistics)вЖТZeubi 5540u ¬Ј prod opsвЖТZgeg 1492u ¬Ј Olivier(marketing)вЖТTaproom 446u ¬Ј Kouros/Arthur(admin/all)вЖТtotal + all-sites (no home KPI). `php -l` clean, deployed, smoke 200 on both views.
