## 2026-06-10 вАФ ROLE-BASED DUAL STOCK VISUALS (physique total + team's home-site physique): PM PRE-BUILD RULING
Operator wants two figures per logged-in user on the Exp√©ditions stock surface: **physique total** + **the physique of the user's team's home site**. Logistics (Nathan/St√©phane/Joelson) вЖТ Zeubi/warehouse; Production вЖТ Zgeg/production; Marketing (Olivier) вЖТ Taproom/pos.

**LIVE USER/SITE MODEL (PM-probed 2026-06-10 вАФ verified, do not re-probe unless schema changes):**
- **NO `users.site_id_fk` / `home_site_id` exists.** `users` cols: role ENUM(`admin`,`operator`,`viewer`,`manager`), `manager_scope` ENUM(`production`,`logistics`,`all`) NULL, `access_preset_id_fk`вЖТ`ref_access_presets`. NO department/team/site column.
- **Team partition lives in TWO places, neither alone covers everyone:** managers carry `manager_scope` (production/logistics/all); **operators have `manager_scope=NULL`** and are partitioned ONLY by `access_preset_id_fk`. Presets: 1=manager, 2=production_operator, 3=logistics_operator, 8=marketing. Roster confirms: Nathan(8,mgr logistics)+St√©phane(9)+Joelson(10) on preset 3; Maxime/Charles/Xavier/Alex on preset 2; Olivier(19) on preset 8.
- **`ref_sites.site_type` ENUM(`production`,`warehouse`,`pos`,`consignment`)** is the clean SoT for the target-site dimension. Rows: 1 Zgeg=production, 2 Zeubi=warehouse, 3 Taproom=pos, 4 Nausikraft=consignment.

**RULING (decisive):**
1. **DERIVE teamвЖТsite_type at the SoT level вАФ do NOT hardcode names, do NOT add a `users.home_site_id_fk` migration.** The home-site is a TEAM attribute, not a per-user fact; a per-user FK would be a parallel/divergent store of something `manager_scope`+`preset` already encode. The mapping is **team вЖТ site_type**, then `ref_sites WHERE site_type=? AND is_active=1` (set-valued, exactly how `fg_stock_compute()` already derives prod sites). Mapping: **logisticsвЖТwarehouse, productionвЖТproduction, marketingвЖТpos**. `consignment` (Nausikraft) has no team вЖТ never a home site.
2. **Team resolution = a single helper `exp_user_home_site_type($user): ?string`** with this precedence: (i) if `manager_scope` set вЖТ `production`/`logistics`/`all`; (ii) else map `access_preset_id_fk` via `ref_access_presets.preset_key` (`production_operator`вЖТproduction, `logistics_operator`вЖТlogistics, `marketing`вЖТpos, `manager`вЖТall). Map by **`preset_key` (the stable string), NOT the numeric id** вАФ ids are environment data. `all`/admin/viewer/unmapped вЖТ NULL (no single home site). This reads existing columns, NO new column, NO migration. (NB: build the teamвЖТsite_type map from `preset_key` + the `manager_scope`/`site_type` enums вАФ both are stable enum vocabularies, so the only "config" is the 3-row correspondence table in PHP, which is the legitimate place for an enumвЖФenum mapping that has no DB home.)
3. **SOURCE the per-site physique from `fg_stock_location_snapshot()`, NOT a re-query.** It already returns `locations[]` each with `id`,`name`,`site_type`,`total_units`,`total_hl` (verified L1269-1277). The home-site figure = the snapshot location whose `site_type` == the user's home_site_type (sum if a team maps to >1 active site of that type вАФ currently 1:1, but keep it set-valued). Physique total = the existing TOTAL strip number (`fg_stock_compute()` physique sum) вАФ already computed. So this is a PURE RENDER-LAYER change reading two existing derivations; ZERO new compute, ZERO new store. **Confirmed: R1 single-home is untouched вАФ no new FG-depletion path.**
4. **GRACEFUL DEFAULT for no-home-site users (admin, manager_scope=all, viewer, unmapped):** show **physique total + a compact all-sites breakdown** (the 3-4 location cards already exist on `?view=stock`; on the strip, total only with a "tous sites" affordance). NEVER fabricate a home site; NEVER hide total. Admin/Kouros wants the full picture, not one site.
5. **RENDER LOCUS вАФ both surfaces, but reuse the snapshot:**
   - `?view=stock` header (`expeditions.php` render block ~L2591+) ALREADY calls `fg_stock_location_snapshot()` (L1653) вЖТ add the home-site highlight there for free.
   - The pinned `exp-cmd-stock-strip` on `?view=commandes` (~L2389) currently does NOT call the snapshot (only `fg_stock_compute` for `$cmdFgPhysique`, L2380). To show the home-site figure on the strip, **add a `fg_stock_location_snapshot()` call on the commandes view** (it's a pure-SELECT lib fn, operator-frequency load вАФ acceptable, same justification as the existing extra `fg_stock_compute` calls L1963/L1986). Strip shows: **physique total + physique <home-site-name>** (use the canonical `ref_sites.name` display string from the snapshot row, e.g. "Zeubi (Logistique)", NEVER re-derive from site_type).
6. **NO-DB-NOMENCLATURE:** label with the canonical site name from `ref_sites.name` (already in the snapshot payload), not the enum (`warehouse`/`pos`) and not a hardcoded "Zeubi". The teamвЖТsite_type derivation is internal; the operator sees "physique Zeubi (Logistique)".

**DIVERGENCE FLAGS:** (i) hardcoding the three names = the exact anti-pattern to refuse (ruling #1/#2 derive instead); (ii) a `users.home_site_id_fk` migration = a parallel store of team-encoded data (refused вАФ derive from `manager_scope`+`preset_key`); (iii) re-querying per-site stock instead of reading the snapshot = a second derivation path that can drift from the cards (ruling #3 forbids); (iv) `consignment` has no team вАФ never surfaces as a home site.

**SCOPE NOTE FOR ORCHESTRATOR вАФ one operator choice to confirm before dispatch:** the operator named individuals but described teams; the `manager_scope`+`preset_key` derivation covers all of them today (verified). The only judgment is the no-home-site default for `manager_scope='all'` / admin (Gonzalo/Yves are production managers вЖТ production; but a future `scope='all'` manager, and Kouros-admin, get the all-sites breakdown per ruling #4). Confirm with the operator that an `all`-scope user seeing total + all-sites (not one site) is the intended behaviour. Everything else is derivable with no choice.

**EQUIP: ui + sql + coder + webapp-testing** (render-layer change in `expeditions.php` + the teamвЖТsite_type helper reading `ref_access_presets`/`users`; smoke `?view=stock` and `?view=commandes` as a logistics user shows physique total + physique Zeubi; as admin shows total + all-sites). NO migration (HEAD stays 303). Files: `app/fg-stock.php` (NONE вАФ read-only reuse), `public/modules/expeditions.php` (helper + strip + stock-header render), `public/css/expeditions.css` (strip second-figure styling, no inline CSS).

### вЬЕ SHOPIFY-INGEST VPS REHOME вАФ EXECUTED + LIVE + COMMITTED 2026-06-12 (OPTION 2; PHP-rewrite REJECTED). The brief's blocking premise ("VPS has NO Node/tsx toolchain") was FALSE вАФ it's just not on the login PATH.
> **DONE:** Option 2 executed exactly as ruled. `/opt/maltytask-pipeline` synced to current HEAD (`bin/deploy.sh --apply-pipeline`; stale 05-22 copy gone, ingest md5-matches local + has shipping_lines/fulfilment_mode; npm ci ran); `secrets/shopify.env` on VPS (640, maltytask:www-data); cron `db/cron/maltytask-shopify-ingest.cron` вЖТ `/etc/cron.d/maltytask-shopify-ingest` (`*/15`, maltytask user, nvm idiom, DB 127.0.0.1:3306 via db.env, NO tunnel); **commit `5ade521`.** VPS dry-run + a real freshening run (board now seconds-fresh, 3164 eshop orders); **autonomous fire CONFIRMED** (11:00 UTC tick wrote the log, idempotent no-op). Local-WSL `*/15` tunnel crontab RETIRED вАФ VPS cron is sole runner. The /opt-sync GATE is CLEARED (the sync IS what fixed the stale-script hazard the ruling flagged). Ruling rationale retained below for provenance.
> Trigger "shopify rehome"/"rehome ingest"/"shopify cron VPS"/"php rewrite shopify"/"node on VPS" вЖТ read THIS block first.
**LIVE-VERIFIED VPS GROUND TRUTH (2026-06-12, ssh maltyweb):**
- **Node IS on the VPS** under nvm: `/var/www/maltytask/.nvm/nvm.sh` вЖТ **node v22.22.2**; **tsx binary present** at `/opt/maltytask-pipeline/node_modules/.bin/tsx`. `which node` empty ONLY because nvm isn't on the login PATH вАФ the `document-ingest`/`ingest-recap` crons ALREADY invoke it via `NVM_DIR=/var/www/maltytask/.nvm bash -c '. nvm.sh && node_modules/.bin/tsx вА¶'`. So the "PHP-only box" framing is wrong: it's a DUAL PHP+Node(nvm)+Python3 box.
- **The maltytask PIPELINE repo is ALREADY deployed to the VPS at `/opt/maltytask-pipeline`** (lib + scripts + node_modules + secrets + package.json) вАФ SEPARATE from the PHP app at `/var/www/maltytask`. **`scripts/ingest-shopify-orders.ts` is ALREADY PRESENT there** (`/opt/maltytask-pipeline/scripts/ingest-shopify-orders.ts`, 23516 bytes, dated 2026-05-22). The script doesn't need porting вАФ it's on the box.
- **The TS ingest is ALREADY VPS-runnable verbatim:** it connects via `lib/repos/mysql-pool.ts` which reads `DB_HOST`/`DB_PORT` from env; the pool's own doc comment says *"On the VPS itself DB_PORT=3306 (direct, no tunnel)."* On the VPS, MySQL is local вЖТ NO tunnel, NO 13306. Two env vars (`SHOPIFY_STORE`/`SHOPIFY_ADMIN_TOKEN`) + a VPS `secrets/shopify.env` (mode 640, www-data group, NOT committed) are all that's missing. line-idempotency already fixed (`bac5501`).
- **The RE-1 / BC external-API-pull pattern on the VPS is PYTHON, not PHP** вАФ `maltytask-bc-sales` cron runs `scripts/python/ingest_bc_sales_ledger.py` (OAuth2 client-credentials against `login.microsoftonline.com`, `requests` + `pymysql` localhost:3306, watermark anti-join, ON DUPLICATE KEY idempotency, creds `config/bc.env` keys BC_TENANT_ID/CLIENT_ID/CLIENT_SECRET/ENVIRONMENT, mode 640). It is currently DISABLED-pending-smoke. So there is NO "PHP-on-VPS external-API-pull" pattern to converge with вАФ the established external-pull connector pattern is a stand-alone Python/`requests` cron. Converging Shopify onto a *PHP* skeleton would mean inventing a 3rd pattern, not reusing one.
**RULING:** **Option 2 вАФ rehome the proven TS ingest as `/etc/cron.d/maltytask-shopify-ingest`** running from `/opt/maltytask-pipeline` (mirror the `document-ingest` cron's nvm-bash idiom + a flock), DB_HOST=127.0.0.1 DB_PORT=3306, with `secrets/shopify.env` landed on the VPS. **Option 1 (PHP rewrite) REJECTED:** it would reimplement a mature, COGS-adjacent, fulfilment-fact-bearing classifier (`shipping_linesвЖТfulfilment_mode`, the canonical pickup-signal list per [[feedback_canonical_list_call_not_copy]]) in PHP/curl with real regression risk on a proven path вАФ and gain NOTHING, since Node is already on the box and the script is already deployed. **Splitting the classifier across two languages is the exact divergence smell to avoid:** `fulfilment_mode` is the load-bearing pickup/delivery fact; it must stay SINGLE-HOMED in the TS ingest (one writer, one classification, `ref_shipping_methods` as the only mapping store). A PHP twin = two implementations of one fact = silent drift. **Architecture verdict:** this IS the "consume the host" pattern correctly applied вАФ the host being consumed is the ALREADY-PRESENT `/opt/maltytask-pipeline` Node runtime + VPS cron infra, NOT a PHP rewrite. Strangler doesn't mandate PHP; it mandates the compute homing on the VPS via the standing cron mechanism, which Option 2 satisfies.
**BUILD (small, low-risk):** (1) land `secrets/shopify.env` on VPS (operator, not committed); (2) author `db/cron/maltytask-shopify-ingest.cron` (source-of-truth in maltyweb repo, deployed via `bin/deploy.sh --apply` вЖТ `/etc/cron.d/`) mirroring the `document-ingest` nvm idiom: `*/15` or `*/30`, user=`maltytask`, `flock -n /tmp/maltytask-shopify-ingest.lock`, `cd /opt/maltytask-pipeline && HOME=вА¶ NVM_DIR=/var/www/maltytask/.nvm bash -c '. $NVM_DIR/nvm.sh && DB_HOST=127.0.0.1 DB_PORT=3306 node_modules/.bin/tsx scripts/ingest-shopify-orders.ts --since "$(date -d "2 days ago" +%F)"' >> /var/log/maltytask/shopify-ingest.log 2>&1`; (3) ensure `/opt/maltytask-pipeline` carries the `bac5501` version of the script (it's dated 05-22 вАФ PRE-`bac5501`; the line-idempotency/shipping_lines/`--until`-default fixes must be synced to /opt before arming вАФ VERIFY); (4) pre-create the log (`maltytask:www-data`); (5) dry-run on VPS first (the ingest `--dry-run` ROLLBACKs); (6) keep the board freshness-chip (already shipped) вАФ it's the staleness sentinel that justified this whole rehome and stays valuable. **OPEN op-decisions:** OK to put `shopify.env` on VPS + install the cron; pick cadence. **GATE:** sync /opt pipeline to post-`bac5501` HEAD before arming (else the rehomed cron runs the OLD pre-fix script). **SIZE:** ~S (one cron file + secret + a /opt sync + dry-run smoke), NOT the M-to-L PHP rewrite. **EQUIP: coder + sql + webapp-testing** (cron/CLI/host = coder; the freshness-chip + any board verification = webapp-testing smoke; sql only if the dry-run distribution check touches the DB). NB cross-repo: cron source lands in **maltyweb** `db/cron/`; the ingest script lives in **maltytask**/`/opt`.

### рЯФС KEY FINDING вАФ the pickup/click&collect signal lives in `shipping_lines[].title` (LIVE Shopify-API-probed during planning), NOT a tag and NOT `fulfillment_status`.
- `fulfillment_status` is a COMPLETION-state field (a false friend for pickup-vs-ship вАФ do NOT use it to classify mode). The ingest does **NOT currently fetch `shipping_lines`** at all.
- **Live pickup titles:** "La Tap & Shop (mercredi - samedi ; 14h-22h)", "RETRAIT A CRISSIER"/"√† CRISSIER", "La N√©buleuse SA".
- **Live delivery titles:** "La Poste - Vinologue (fragile)", "Vinologue Suisse - Fragile", "Standard Suisse", "Livraison Offerte/offerte/gratuite".
- Messy free-text (team is mid-standardization) вЖТ **curated map + `review` bucket, NEVER guess** (never-guess-a-mapping canon). The plan threads this directly into the ¬ІвС† pickup double-deplete forward-hazard: once pickup orders carry a mode and sync into `inv_sales_orders`, they deplete via the eshop leg and the picking view READS them вАФ they are NEVER re-created as `ord_orders` (XOR holds).

### Approved phased roadmap
- **Phase 0 вАФ FEED FOUNDATION (buildable NOW, do FIRST; zero depletion risk):** (1) fix the ingest **line-idempotency bug** (below) FIRST; (2) capture `shipping_lines` вЖТ raw `shipping_method_title` on `inv_sales_orders`; (3) curated classification вАФ new **`ref_shipping_methods`** (title_norm UNIQUE, `fulfilment_mode` enum pickup/delivery, seeded from the verified live titles) вЖТ ingest sets new **`inv_sales_orders.fulfilment_mode ENUM('pickup','delivery','review')`** (unknownвЖТ`review`, operator-actionable); (4) fix the hardcoded `--until 2026-05-01` (cause of the **Apr-30 data gap**) вЖТ default "now" + one backfill run + **cron the ingest on a trailing window with a flock**. Mig `320_inv_shipping_method_map.sql` (table + the 2 `inv_sales_orders` cols). NO gate.
- **Phase 1 вАФ PER-ORDER ESHOP PICKING SURFACE (buildable now, READ-ONLY re depletion):** replace the date-aggregate eshop auto-row on the Commandes board with **per-order eshop rows** (customer, SKU pills, **pickup/delivery badge** рЯПђ Retrait / рЯЪЪ Livraison / вЪ† √† classer, per-day pickup-vs-ship counters). Pure read from `inv_sales_orders`+lines (XOR trivial). Rows carry `data-eshop-order-id` (NOT `data-order-id`) so existing status JS never touches them; no actions yet. Include eshop in the cross-date search. Gate: Phase-0 `fulfilment_mode`.
- **Phase 2 вАФ FULFILMENT TRACKING + BIDIRECTIONAL SHOPIFY WRITE-BACK (the big piece; build after 0+1):** eshop workflow state in a **dedicated 1:1 side table** `inv_sales_fulfilment` (keyed on `inv_sales_orders.id`) + `inv_sales_fulfilment_events` (append-only) вАФ MIRRORS the `ord_orders` + `ord_order_status_events` pattern; lazy-created on first action (absent row вЗТ implicit `new`/`idle`); mode-aware lifecycle (delivery newвЖТpickingвЖТpickedвЖТfulfilled; pickup вА¶вЖТready_for_pickupвЖТpicked_up); cols incl. `shopify_sync_state` enum idle/pending/pushed/failed + `shopify_fulfillment_id` + push_error/attempts. Mig `321_inv_sales_fulfilment.sql`. UI: `exp_render_eshop_chips()` + sync badge + `public/js/eshop-fulfilment.js`. API: `public/api/eshop-fulfilment-status.php` (clone of `expeditions-status.php`; one txn = event + cache upsert + audit; push-triggering status sets `shopify_sync_state='pending'`, does NOT call Shopify inline). Worker: **`scripts/push-shopify-fulfilment.ts`** (cron+flock) drains `pending` вЖТ Shopify Admin **Fulfillment Orders API** (delivery=create fulfillmentвЖТfulfilled; pickup=ready_for_pickupвЖТpicked_up); idempotent (check open fulfillment-order + stored id; "already fulfilled"=convergence); capped retry + operator re-arm. **Reverse reconcile** via the now-idempotent ingest (`source='shopify_reconcile'`). **CONFLICT POLICY: maltyweb-wins-forward вАФ reconcile only ever ADVANCES local to match Shopify, never reverts an operator action.** GATE: confirm the Shopify Admin token has fulfillment **write** scopes (read-only blocks write-back).
- **Phase 3 вАФ PICKUP HARDENING + TAP MACHINES (gated on the team standardizing shipping-method names):** prune/extend `ref_shipping_methods` once names settle (drive `review`вЖТ0; admin to map unknowns without deploy; split board into Retrait/Livraison lanes). **Tap machines (T7) = NON-STOCK:** new `ref_skus.is_non_stock` flag (mig `322_*`, orthogonal-flag doctrine per mig 210); fulfillable + on the picking view but excluded from FG sum via `AND rs.is_non_stock = 0` added **SYMMETRICALLY** to the eshop leg in BOTH `fg_stock_compute()` AND `fg_stock_location_snapshot()` вАФ verify `ќ£cards==ќ£physique` after. (Resolves the ¬ІвС° "T7/Cuves = equipment, must NOT deplete FG" ruling at the SKU-config level.)
- **Phase 4 вАФ CAGE/BOX COGS ENGINE = OUT OF SCOPE (named only).** The Stage-2 / вС£ Phase-2 cage/box draw-down engine (downstream CONSUMER of this fulfilment data, gated on the 2026-06-15 cage anchor) is a SEPARATE arc, not designed here.

### Hard constraints carried (non-negotiable)
- **XOR depletion:** order вИИ `ord_orders` XOR `inv_sales_orders`, never both. Eshop fulfilment workflow creates **NO** `ord_orders` rows. The discriminator is membership in `inv_sales_orders`, not a flag we invent (¬ІвС†c canon).
- **Single-homed FG derivation:** `fg_stock_compute()` is the only FG depletion. ANY filter added to its eshop leg (`app/fg-stock.php` ~L462-515) MUST be mirrored in `fg_stock_location_snapshot()` (~L814-850) or `ќ£cards вЙ† ќ£physique`. **P0/P1 add NO fg-stock filter вЖТ zero depletion risk. The only symmetric-filter change is P3 (`is_non_stock`).**
- **Raw vs computed:** `inv_sales_orders`/`inv_sales_order_lines` are `class='source'`, `corrections_policy='blocked_with_redirect'` (LIVE-VERIFIED 2026-06-10) вАФ operator workflow state goes in the `inv_sales_fulfilment` SIDE TABLE, NEVER on the raw table. An ingest-derived `fulfilment_mode` column IS OK on `inv_sales_orders` because it's a PURE FUNCTION of the Shopify pull (same class as the existing `fulfillment_status`/`financial_status`/`period` derived cols), not operator-entered state.

### рЯФі INGEST LINE-IDEMPOTENCY BUG (Shopify side вАФ must fix FIRST, Phase-0 item 1)
`scripts/ingest-shopify-orders.ts` `insertOrderBatch()` L378-384: `const wasDupe = orderRes.affectedRows === 0; if (wasDupe) { ordersDupe++; continue; }` вАФ when an order PRE-EXISTS (INSERT IGNORE no-op), it `continue`s at ORDER level вЖТ **its lines are never re-evaluated and mutable header fields never updated.** So a re-pull of a CHANGED order silently no-ops; you can NEVER enrich existing orders with `shipping_lines`/`fulfilment_mode`, advance `fulfillment_status`, or do reverse-reconcile. **Fix: on pre-existing order, still (a) `INSERT IGNORE` the lines (already row_hash-idempotent), (b) `UPDATE` the mutable header fields (`fulfillment_status`, `shipping_method_title`, `fulfilment_mode`).** This is the SHOPIFY-side parallel of the already-recorded `import_weeklyorders.php` `ord_order_lines` UNIQUE/ODKU bug (¬ІWeeklyOrders status one-liner) вАФ same "header idempotent, lines/mutables not" class, different table.

### Phase-0 build facts (PM-verified live 2026-06-10)
- **MIGRATION HEAD = 319 applied (`migrate.php --status`); next free = `320`.** (Parallel sessions live вАФ re-`--status` + `ls db/migrations` at build-start per checklist; 312 already collided once 312_drop_invoice_validate_topbar vs 312_kpi_sales вАФ so a fresh check is mandatory.)
- **`schema_meta` for the NEW `ref_shipping_methods` table:** `table_class='reference'`, `corrections_policy='allowed'`, `upstream_hint` вЙИ "Shopify shipping-method title вЖТ pickup/delivery classification map. Seed from verified live titles; add/edit via Exp√©ditions admin or direct MySQL; unknown titles land orders in fulfilment_mode='review'." (Mirrors `ref_transporters`/`ref_customers` which are exactly `reference`/`allowed`.) ONE `schema_meta` row required per the per-new-table rule.
- **The TWO new `inv_sales_orders` columns** (`shipping_method_title` VARCHAR, `fulfilment_mode` ENUM('pickup','delivery','review')): **NO schema_meta change needed** вАФ the table is ALREADY `class='source'`/`blocked_with_redirect`; ALTER-adding ingest-derived columns does NOT change its classification (schema_meta is per-TABLE, not per-column). Just add the columns; do not touch its schema_meta row.
- **INGEST HOST / CRON = the maltytask LOCAL host, NOT the VPS.** `ingest-shopify-orders.ts` runs `npx tsx scripts/ingest-shopify-orders.ts` on the maltytask box: it reads `secrets/shopify.env`, connects to MySQL **over the SSH tunnel (13306)** via `withConnection`/`withTransaction`, emits `logAudit` to `data/audit-log.jsonl`. It is run MANUALLY today (no cron). **There is NO existing maltytask user crontab** (`crontab -l` empty). The flock pattern to MIRROR = **`scripts/send-ingest-recap.ts`** (the only flock-guarded script; "designed to be run by a flock-guarded cron", writes preview to `/tmp`, exits 0 silently when nothing to do). Follow its lock idiom for the P0 ingest cron (and the P2 worker cron). NB: the SSH tunnel needs `-o ServerAliveInterval=30 -o ExitOnForwardFailure=yes` for an unattended cron run (existing keepalive convention).
- **APR-30 GAP cause = hardcoded `--until 2026-05-01`** in the ingest's default window (`'fulfillment_status','total_price',вА¶` field set is fine; the date bound is the gap). Default it to "now" + run one backfill to today, THEN cron a trailing window. Dry-run-verify the backfill BEFORE going live (double-run = 0 orders/lines inserted but a changed `fulfillment_status` updates; FG totals UNCHANGED since no eshop-leg filter is added in P0).

### EQUIP вАФ Phase-0 Sonnet build: **coder + sql** (+ webapp-testing only if P0 surfaces any rendered page вАФ it does NOT, P0 is ingest+migration only, so coder+sql suffices). The TS edit (`ingest-shopify-orders.ts`, maltytask) = coder; the maltyweb migration `320` = sql. ### Phase-0 gotchas (durable)
- **TS ingest edit:** preserve the `logAudit({...})` discipline вАФ the `wasDupe` branch currently SKIPS audit; the new "update existing order" path must emit a `logAudit` event (e.g. `action:'order-updated'`) so the change shows in `data/audit-log.jsonl`. Keep `--dry-run` working (the `DryRunRollback` throw + ROLLBACK pattern at L425-434) for both the line re-eval and the header UPDATE. The order **INSERT IGNORE вЖТ upsert** change: do NOT switch the INSERT to `ON DUPLICATE KEY UPDATE` blindly вАФ `row_hash` is part of the UNIQUE; a content change yields a NEW row_hash, so the upsert key must be the STABLE key (`UNIQUE(source, external_order_id)`), and the UPDATE must target only the mutable header cols (not re-stamp `created_at`/`period`). row_hash stays a change-detector, not the upsert key.
- **Migration:** MySQL 8 (no `IF NOT EXISTS` on `ADD COLUMN`; no bare SELECT in the .sql вАФ `migrate.php` exec() leaves result sets open). FK type on `ref_shipping_methods` PK and any FK = match exactly. The `inv_sales_orders` ALTER adds 2 columns (INSTANT DDL on MySQL 8 вАФ cheap). ENUM `fulfilment_mode` default should be `'review'` (so an un-classified order is operator-visible, never silently mis-moded). schema_meta INSERT for `ref_shipping_methods` in the same migration.

### Sequencing verdict (CONFIRMED)

The first fg-stock change in the whole roadmap is P3's symmetric `is_non_stock` filter. P0+P1 ship first (immediate value, no depletion risk), then P2 (bidirectional sync, gated on the Shopify write-token scope), then P3 (gated on team name-standardization + the cage anchor).
- **Cron/backfill MUST be dry-run-verified before going live** (the ingest's `--dry-run` already ROLLBACKs; verify the `fulfilment_mode` distribution + a small `review` bucket + a double-run = 0 new rows but a changed `fulfillment_status` updates + FG totals unchanged, BEFORE arming the cron).

FK-type mismatch = our #1 migration-failure class.
- **schema_meta вАФ MIRROR THE `ord_*` SIBLINGS, do NOT default to `'allowed'`:** `inv_sales_fulfilment` is the eshop twin of `ord_orders` вЖТ copy `ord_orders`'s schema_meta `corrections_policy` exactly; `inv_sales_fulfilment_events` is the twin of `ord_order_status_events` (append-only) вЖТ copy that row, NEVER `'allowed'` on an immutable event log. Both `table_class='operational'`; one schema_meta INSERT per table in mig 322; writer hint = "eshop-fulfilment-status.php API + future push-shopify-fulfilment.ts worker".

ROLE GATE = login-only, NO role check** (PM-verified live: `expeditions-status.php` gates purely on `current_user() !== null` вЖТ 403 if not logged in; access control is at the PAGE level via the Exp√©ditions `ref_pages` gate, NOT in the handler). Clone that: CSRF first-gate w/ fresh-token retry hint, ONE txn (event insert + `inv_sales_fulfilment` upsert + `log_revision`), PRG/JSON. **Push-deferral CONFIRMED + load-bearing:** reaching `fulfilled`/`ready_for_pickup`/`picked_up` sets `shopify_sync_state='pending'` and returns вАФ does NOT call Shopify inline. This is why 2A is LIVE-safe pre-scopes (nothing in 2A touches the Shopify API).
- **2A GOTCHAS (flag all to the agent):** (1) lazy-create = `INSERT вА¶ ODKU` on UNIQUE `order_id_fk` inside the txn (not SELECT-then-branch race); render treats "no row" as `new`/`idle`, never NULL-crash. (2) **`fulfilment_mode='review'` order has NO lifecycle вЖТ handler must REFUSE advance** ("√† classer d'abord"), not pick a default map (never-guess applies to lifecycle selection). (3) `data-eshop-order-id` namespacing (Phase-1 convention) вАФ `eshop-fulfilment.js` binds ONLY on it; verify no collision with `expeditions-status.js`'s `data-order-id` delegation. (4) **`log_revision` ENUM has no `'delete'`** вАФ any cancel/abandon tombstones via `action='update'` + an event row, never a delete (and the roadmap lifecycle has no cancel terminal вАФ decide cancel semantics explicitly, don't add a delete path). (5) **DIRTY-SHARED-TREE HAZARD ACUTE** вАФ tree holds foreign session work (financier-data.php, in-flight 168-hunk expeditions.css overhaul, kpi-handlers churn); deploy SURGICALLY (file-scoped scp + diff deploy-delta, `coder` skill "Dirty shared tree"), NOT `bin/deploy.sh --apply`; commit by PATHSPEC; put new chip CSS in a NEW file `eshop-fulfilment.css` to dodge the expeditions.css collision (same dodge as expeditions-sku-history.css).

## вЬЕ FULL SHOPIFYвЗДMALTYWEB FULFILMENT BUILD COMPLETE вАФ autonomous run 2026-06-11 (Kouros away; reviews on return)

### Phase 0 вАФ shipping-method classification + ingest (maltyweb mig **321**; maltytask ingest `bac5501`)
- `ref_shipping_methods` (16 rows) + `inv_sales_orders.shipping_method_title` / `fulfilment_mode`. Ingest now captures `shipping_lines`, classifies pickup/delivery/review, **line-idempotency bug FIXED** (the ¬ІINGEST LINE-IDEMPOTENCY BUG above вАФ pre-existing order now re-evals lines + UPDATEs mutable header), `--until=now` default.
- **LIVE BACKFILL: May+June ingested вЖТ 3127 orders total; FG delta вИТ5 units (corrective, recorded).**

## ¬ІFG STOCKTAKE вЖТ SAISIES SURFACING + month_closed ATTRIBUTION вАФ PM RULING 2026-06-11 (pre-build; triggered by May-2026 COGS close blocked on missing 2026-05 FG anchor)
**Context:** Closing May 2026 COGS. Of the 4 close inputs (RM closing / WIP tank_balances / sales / FG stocktake), only the **FG May-31 stocktake** is missing. Live DB (PM-probed 2026-06-11): `inv_fg_stocktake` active rows = **ONLY `month_closed='2026-06'`** (107 `maltyweb-form` counted 06-08/06-09 + 1 `manual-adjustment`); the **April anchor is GONE** (re-anchored to June) вЖТ no 2026-05 row AND no April fallback. Kouros asked: create the FG month-end stocktake and "have it sit on Saisies."

**KEY FINDING вАФ the FG count form ALREADY EXISTS and is the canonical writer.** It is `expeditions.php?view=stocktake` (the 2026-06 rows came from it, `source='maltyweb-form'`). `inv_fg_stocktake` has **ONE writer = `expeditions.php:746` INSERT** (mig 288 generated `row_hash`; every other ref is read-only SELECT). The "absence" is purely **discoverability** вАФ Saisies has 5 cards (packaging/racking/brewing/fermenting + **RM stocktake** `form-rm-stocktake.php`) but NO FG card. FG's count surface was built later inside the Fulfilment arc, so it never got a Saisies card.

**RULING 1 вАФ SURFACE, don't FORK. Add a Saisies card LINKING to `expeditions.php?view=stocktake`. Do NOT factor a `form-fg-stocktake.php`; do NOT migrate the writer.** Factoring the form = a SECOND writer to a single-writer COGS-bearing table = the parallel-store divergence smell. The FG form is entangled with the Exp√©ditions view (per-location anchor, `exp_st_scope_allowed` channel matrix, `display_family` grouping, mig-288 generated-hash UPSERT, manager-backdate, freshness chips) вАФ re-homing is large surface, zero canonical benefit. Saisies is a **card-grid of LINKS (discovery hub)**, not a rule that every count form physically lives there (RM's own module is incidental). The racking split-card already links OUT (`form-racking.php` "Saisie classique вЖТ") вАФ same pattern. `inv_fg_stocktake` stays Fulfilment-owned; Saisies gains a 6th card "Inventaire produits finis (PF)" вЖТ `/modules/expeditions.php?view=stocktake`. Additive вАФ nothing superseded, no scrapping.

**RULING 2 вАФ CORRECT the operator's premise: RM does NOT auto-attribute early-next-month counts to the prior month.** RM gives an explicit `period` month-picker (`form-rm-stocktake.php` L28-32, default = current month) and the operator CHOOSES `2026-05`. FG instead derives `month_closed = substr(counted_at,0,7)` (`expeditions.php:785`) with NO override. So the real inconsistency = **"FG has no period control; RM does"** вАФ NOT "RM has a вИТ1-month rule." Fix = give FG the SAME operator lever (explicit, default-but-overridable `month_closed` field), NOT a silent "if day вЙ§ N attribute to prior month" heuristic (= a guessed COGS-impacting attribution; would silently mis-file a legitimately-late June count into May). **Explicit operator choice over silent inference on a COGS key, always.** Note: managers CAN already backdate FG (`$stDefaultCountedAt = $stSelDate` for managers; operators always today) вАФ so the May close is reachable today with `counted_at=2026-05-31`.

**SEQUENCING:**
- **Phase 0 (NO build вАФ unblock May NOW):** Kouros opens `?view=stocktake`, manager-date = `2026-05-31`, enters the May-31 FG census вЖТ `month_closed='2026-05'`. вЪ†пЄП **Per-SKU anchor means a PARTIAL May census silently leaves some SKUs anchored elsewhere вАФ enter a COMPLETE May set.** вЪ†пЄП **If no real May-31 physical count exists (only the June-8 one), that is a DATA-AVAILABILITY question вАФ do NOT synthesize a May close from June data; surface it to Kouros for an explicit nearest-count decision (never-guess-COGS line).**
- **Phase 1 (small follow-up build):** Saisies 6th card вЖТ `?view=stocktake`. `saisies.php` + `saisies.css` only; NO mig, NO writer/schema change. RULE 3: card links to `expeditions` (already tour-covered) and `saisies` is tour-special-cased вАФ check the tour saisies-chapter form-card map; dispatch tour-steward only if `tour-gap-check.php` flags. **EQUIP: ui + coder + webapp-testing.**
- **Phase 2 (small, deferrable вАФ the durable RM/FG consistency fix):** explicit operator-chosen `month_closed` field on the FG form (default `substr(counted_at,0,7)`, overridable) mirroring RM's period picker вАФ lets an operator count June 1-2 and attribute to May WITHOUT backdating the physical count date. `month_closed` column already exists вЖТ NO schema change, populate-path change only. **EQUIP: ui + coder + webapp-testing.**
- Phases 1 & 2 independent; BOTH safe to defer past the May close. **Do NOT gate the May close on either.**

**DIVERGENCE FLAGS:** (1) refuse any `form-fg-stocktake.php` = 2nd writer to single-writer COGS table; (2) no silent prior-month heuristic; (3) partial-May-census trap (per-SKU anchor); (4) don't fabricate a May count from June data.

Do NOT let a coder pull cage retarget into this build.
- **рЯФі REPACK FG-LEG MODEL вАФ DISAMBIGUATED + CORRECTED 2026-06-16 (PM, live-verified; SUPERSEDES the struck "Model-B `+loose_units` credit" that a prior same-day session recorded WRONG).** The deployed `fg-stock.php` leg (Step 5.5 + snapshot) is ALREADY the correct model ("M0"): **the ONLY stock effect of a repack event is `вИТfrom_qty` on `from_sku` (the base box). NO positive credit term вАФ not `+loose_units`, not `+from_qty√Чupp`, not a `+to_sku` term.** Live comment verbatim: *"Net contribution: вИТfrom_qty on from_sku_id (base box only)вА¶ Do NOT add a positive term for to_sku here."* WHY: the countable FG universe = scope вИИ {base, cage} only; everything a repack PRODUCES (the bundle `to_sku`, the loose remainder) lands in scope='none' SKUs already excluded by the `stocktake_scope <> 'none'` JOIN (the `d9f7976` gate). So opening a base box removes the WHOLE box (shipped portion + remainder) from countable FG вЖТ correct FG delta = `вИТfrom_qty √Ч base_upp` bottle-equiv, achieved by `вИТ1 box` and nothing else. **The struck `+loose_unitsвЖТsingle` credit is BOTH unresolvable AND wrong-signed:** live events open ALT4 (recipe 6) вЖТ produce EPH24PB (id=75, scope='none' 4-pack) вАФ the loose remainder is NOT ALTBU singles, and crediting the scope='single' ALTBU (countable) would mint phantom countable inventory no physical count reconciles. `loose_units`/`to_*` stay EVENT-ROW METADATA, never arithmetic inputs (live code already ignores them вАФ verified). **NO eshop-leg bundleвЖТsingle/component decomposition** вАФ that is the deferred Phase-4 cage-COGS engine (OUT OF SCOPE), and adding it would DOUBLE-COUNT against the operator-confirmed `inv_repack_events` row (which is the SOLE stock mover for a box-open, written by `expeditions-repack.php`). Eshop leg KEEPS its `<> 'none'` exclusion. MUST land byte-symmetric in BOTH fns (R1 lockstep) вАФ but symmetric on the `вИТfrom_qty` leg, no credit.
- **VARIANT LINKER = new bridge `ref_sku_shopify_variants`** (`shopify_variant_id BIGINT UNIQUE`, `sku_id_fk INTвЖТref_skus.id`, `shopify_product_id`, `title_snapshot`, SCD2 dates) + schema_meta вАФ NOT a ref_skus col (mirrors ref_sku_aliases family; numeric key). Ingest: no-code+has-variant вЖТ bridge lookup вЖТ existing decompose; unmatched вЖТ RQ. **Historical backfill DEFERRED to RQ review CSV (COGS-bearing, never auto-map).**
- **3 TITLE-ONLY PACKS:** Beer Des Rosses = single-recipe, just link variantвЖТEPH1BU(91), no slots. Pack de No√Ђl = composite slots DOA(30)/MOO(44)/EMB(32)√Ч1 member_fmt 5 + verre 25cl via `ref_sku_packaging_choices`вЖТPKG_VERRE_25CL(186) (XMASPACK pattern). ## ¬ІBCвЖФord_orders PHASE 1 вАФ ORDER INTEGRATION SCOPED + PM-RULED 2026-06-15 (pre-build; "on lance phase 1 pour s√їr")
**GOAL:** Logistics double-enters every B2B order (BC + WeeklyOrders sheet). Phase 1 ELIMINATES the sheet: pull OPEN B2B BC sales orders вЖТ `ord_orders`/`ord_order_lines`/`ord_order_status_events`; logistics works them in the Exp√©ditions "Commandes" tab (pickingвЖТBLвЖТshipped). Net: logistics enters once (in BC), maltytask shows it. READ-ONLY toward BC. Phase 2 (input-on-maltytask вЖТ write-back to BC) = LATER arc.

**LIVE STATE VERIFIED 2026-06-15 (PM read-only probe):**
- `ord_orders` schema: `source ENUM('web','email','import')` DEFAULT 'web'; `source_ref VARCHAR(190)` **UNIQUE** (71/122 populated); `internal_channel ENUM('taproom','eshop','cage','shop')`; `status ENUM(entered,confirmed,picked,bl_printed,shipped,cancelled)` DEFAULT 'entered'; `transporter_id_fk`, `customer_id_fk`, `requested_date`, `parse_confidence`, `review_status ENUM(none,pending,accepted)`, `source_file_id_fk`. Distribution: web 16e/2c/4p/3blp/25sh/1canc; import 34e/4c/1p/32sh.
- `ord_order_lines`: `order_id_fk`, `sku_id_fk INT UNSIGNED` (RESTRICT), `qty DECIMAL(10,2)`, `line_comment`.
- `ord_order_status_events`: append-only TRUTH вАФ `order_id_fk`, `status`, `occurred_at DATETIME def CURRENT_TIMESTAMP`, `user_id_fk`, `comment`.
- **WeeklyOrders importer = `scripts/import_weeklyorders.php` is a MANUAL one-shot** (reads `/tmp/wo-parsed.json`, dry-run default / `--apply`). **NO cron exists** вАФ so "stop the cron" is a non-issue; just stop running it. Writes `source='import'`, `source_ref='weeklyorders:1955899648:r<N>'`.
- **BC connector already live = `scripts/python/ingest_bc_sales_ledger.py` (maltyweb deploy, user maltytask), cron `/etc/cron.d/maltytask-bc-sales` every 4h** вАФ encodes the OData S2S OAuth2 + customer resolver (`bc_customer_no вЖТ ref_customers.id`) + SKU resolver (`ref_skus.sku_code WHERE is_active=1` вЖТ `ref_sku_aliases` вЖТ raw; `hl_resolved = qty √Ч hl_per_unit`). REUSE these idioms verbatim.
- **`app/fg-stock.php` `fg_stock_compute()` has 3 DEPLETION LEGS:** Step 4 = `ord_orders` lines WHERE status='shipped' (ALL order_types deplete); Step 5 = eshop via `inv_sales_order_lines`/`inv_sales_orders` (Shopify); Step 6/taproom = `inv_sales_bc.qty_invoiced` channel='taproom'. **THIS is the double-deplete surface.**

**THE 7 RULINGS:**
1. **SOURCE = standard `salesOrders` API as set-driver** (29 live, doc-state-scoped, drops posted/shipped automatically; the custom `SalesOrder` web service returns stale 2020 orders = filtering liability). **Custom web service = TARGETED by-No lookup ONLY** to enrich each in-set order with `ShpfyOrderNo` + `Shipping_Agent_Code` IF the standard header lacks them. **PROBE FIRST** whether standard `salesOrders` exposes `ShpfyOrderNo` (some BC tenants surface it as a custom API field) вАФ if yes, skip the hybrid entirely. Reuse OData idioms verbatim: S2S OAuth2 client-creds `config/bc.env`, OR-chained `$filter` at **50 ids/batch (BC rejects the `in` operator, HTTP 501)**, **nextLink paging, NO `$top`** ($top suppresses @odata.nextLink вЖТ silent truncation). `Shipping_Agent_Code` вЖТ `ref_transporters`.
2. **SHOPIFY DOUBLE-COUNT EXCLUSION = `ShpfyOrderNo` non-empty вЖТ EXCLUDE.** A BC sales order carrying ShpfyOrderNo IS an eshop sale already in `inv_sales_orders` (channel='eshop', deplets fg-stock Step 5). Pulling it into ord_orders double-counts on the board AND in fg-stock. Belt-braces: ALSO exclude system customers `1080` (eshop priv√©) + `3822` (taproom) вАФ a B2B open order should never be for them. Net filter = `ShpfyOrderNo empty AND Sell_to_Customer_No NOT IN (1080,3822)`. No other channel leak today (Lightspeed has no feed).
3. **CUTOVER = sequenced cut, NO dual-live window.** Stop running `import_weeklyorders.php`. Add ENUM val: `ALTER TABLE ord_orders MODIFY source ENUM('web','email','import','bc') NOT NULL DEFAULT 'web';`. BC orders key `source='bc'`, `source_ref='bc:<BC OrderNo>'` (e.g. `bc:ORD201126`) вАФ `source_ref` already UNIQUE вЖТ idempotent upsert. **Existing web/import rows AGE OUT вАФ do NOT migrate/reconcile** (50 import + 16 web = real operator-worked orders; shipped ones won't reappear as open BC orders since BC closes on full shipment). The ~39 genuinely-open import/web rows MAY collide with the open BC set вЖТ 1st dry-run **match-report flags (customer, requested_date, lines) collisions** вЖТ operator decides per-row (cancel legacy vs skip BC pull). NEVER auto-merge. After one operator backlog-clear pass, BC is sole feed.
4. **рЯФі CRUX вАФ STATUS PRESERVATION on recurring pull.** Single rule: *the BC pull is a HEADER/LINE refresher gated on `status IN('entered','confirmed')`; status + status_events are OPERATOR-OWNED and NEVER written by the pull.* On INSERT: create order (status='entered') + lines + ONE 'entered' event. On re-pull of existing (matched by source_ref): UPDATE only `customer_id_fk`/`requested_date`/`transporter_id_fk`/`comment`/line qtys+SKUs вАФ DO NOT write `status`, DO NOT append a status event. Freeze lines once status >= 'picked' (a BC line edit must not silently change what's being picked вЖТ flag divergence to review). `Completely_Shipped=true` / order leaves the open BC set = a **reconciliation SIGNAL surfaced on the board** ("BC reports shipped"), NOT an auto-advance/cancel вАФ auto-advancing would (a) write unauthorized status and (b) fire fg-stock depletion on a pull not an operator action (wrong lane). Order leaving the open set must NOT delete/cancel the local row (it's mid-fulfilment locally).
5. **SKU RESOLUTION = `(Item_No, Unit_of_Measure_Code)` вЖТ ref_skus.** Item No ALONE is insufficient (same beer item ships in multiple formats; UoM code e.g. 24B selects the format/SKU). Ledger connector resolved on bare Item_No only because the ledger export is already SKU-grain; an ORDER line is item+UoM. Build/confirm a `(bc_item, bc_uom) вЖТ sku_id` resolver, reuse `ref_sku_aliases` where it already encodes the combination. **REFUSE-DON'T-NULL:** an unresolved line does NOT create a `sku_id_fk=NULL` line (RESTRICT FK forbids it anyway; a NULL line silently under-picks + under-deplets). Emit a self-sufficient review-CSV row (order No + raw item + UoM + qty, same pattern as the ledger connector's unresolved-SKU CSV) and hold the order out of apply OR apply flagged `review_status='pending'` with the bad line surfaced вАФ operator-decided, NEVER guess item+UoMвЖТSKU from a pattern.
6. **REFRESH = VPS cron `*/15`** (match `maltytask-shopify-ingest` cadence; open set tiny ~29 + operationally hot вАФ logistics wants new orders visible fast; do NOT use the ledger's 4h). User maltytask, `--apply`, log to `/var/log/maltytask/`. NOT local. Webhook = Phase-2-era nicety, don't build now.
7. **MIGRATION = ONE:** the `source` ENUM extension above (MySQL-8, no IF NOT EXISTS; ENUM extension is INSTANT). `source_ref` UNIQUE already exists. **No new table вЖТ no schema_meta row.** Possibly a small `bc_uomвЖТformat` lookup if not derivable via aliases вАФ prefer reusing `ref_sku_aliases` over a new table; confirm in build. Pre-flight: `migrate.php --status` (head was 345 at last check вАФ RE-VERIFY, parallel sessions lead), next free number, no bare SELECT.

**DIVERGENCE FLAGS:**
- **рЯФі #1 fg-stock DOUBLE-DEPLETE (live, concrete):** a Shopify-origin BC order leaking into ord_orders + getting shipped depletes BOTH Step 4 (ord_orders) AND Step 5 (eshop/Shopify) вЖТ physical FG under-counts. The ShpfyOrderNo exclusion (ruling 2) is exactly what prevents it. Same hazard class as the 2026-06-12 eshop-repack/stale-fg-stock.php double-deplete incident. **OPUS MUST INDEPENDENTLY VERIFY** the no-double-deplete invariant before done (COGS/inventory-bearing; a sub-agent PASS = a claim): assert no `ord_orders.source='bc'` row maps to a BC order with ShpfyOrderNo; spot-check an eshop order does NOT appear on the Commandes board.
- **Status clobber on re-pull** (ruling 4) вАФ guarded by the header/line-only refresher gate.
- **NULL/guessed SKU line** (ruling 5) вАФ refuse-don't-NULL + review CSV.
- **Parallel sale-side store drift:** `ord_orders` (open-operational) vs `inv_sales_ledger` (posted-fiscal) are DISJOINT facts joined only by BC order No вАФ different lifecycle stages. Don't let anyone "reconcile" ord_orders qty against ledger qty as same fact. Burn engine (semaines_stock) keeps reading the ledger, NOT ord_orders.
- **off-trade / sale_class = customer attribute** (`ref_customers`) вАФ ignore on the order pull (already ruled in WeeklyOrders arc); don't leak channel classification onto ord_orders.

**SCOPE = tight 3-4 working days** вАФ OData/auth/customer-resolver/SKU-alias-resolver/ord_* tables/status-event model/Commandes board/match-report-dry-run discipline all REUSED. New = one connector (model on `ingest_bc_sales_ledger.py` + `import_weeklyorders.php`), one ENUM mig, the cron, the item+UoMвЖТSKU resolver. Two well-defined seams (Shopify exclusion, status-preserving upsert). Only stretch risk = open-order collision reconciliation = one-time operator pass.
**BUILD SEQUENCE:** (a) probe standard salesOrders for ShpfyOrderNo вЖТ decide hybrid; (b) ENUM mig; (c) connector dry-run вЖТ match-report (Shopify-excluded set, customer/SKU resolution, collisions flagged); (d) Kouros reviews unmatched/collisions; (e) `--apply`; (f) cron `*/15`; (g) Opus-verify fg-stock no-double-deplete invariant.
**EQUIP coder+sql+webapp-testing** (Sonnet codes; status-preserving upsert is the careful part; webapp-testing smokes that Commandes shows BC orders + does NOT show eshop orders, read-only vs prod). Trigger "phase 1"/"BC order"/"salesOrders"/"ShpfyOrderNo"/"ord_orders BC"/"WeeklyOrders cutover"/"order integration" вЖТ READ this section.

## рЯЯҐ BC ORDERS READER вАФ NEAR-REAL-TIME LATENCY (PM-RULED 2026-06-16, Kouros "√† chaque commande imm√©diat")
**Operator directive: the BC open-orders sync must feel per-order/immediate, not 15-min вАФ logistics works the Commandes board LIVE and can't keep up with a 15-min lag.** PM VERDICT: this is a LATENCY-TUNING decision with ZERO COGS/SOT risk (the reader is the INTENT-layer refresher; it NEVER writes status/status_events вАФ depletion keys on operator-set `status='shipped'` only; `ord_orders` never feeds COGS/COP/WAC/BOM/beer-tax). NB this is a DIFFERENT lane from the Shopify-ingest "host fragility not frequency" ruling (¬ІShopify VPS rehome, line ~186): the BC-orders reader is ALREADY VPS-resident (`/etc/cron.d/maltytask-bc-orders`, MySQL local, no tunnel), so for THIS cron frequency genuinely IS the lever.
- **OPTIONS:** A=BC webhook subscriptions (event-driven; cost = public endpoint + 5s validationToken handshake + renewal cron for вЙ§3-day-TTL subs + missed-notification recovery + don't-trust-payload GET-the-resource security). B=tighten poll to `*/1`. C=hybrid (webhook + low-freq safety-net poll).
- **рЯФС RECOMMENDATION: ship B (1-min poll) NOW; do NOT pre-build A.** A 60s worst-case lag is imperceptible to a human picker; A's marginal latency win (вЙ§60sвЖТ~2s) is not felt, while its overhead (subscription-expiry = SILENT-death failure mode worse than a poll that just retries next minute; new public attack surface; renewal-cron fragility) is permanent. The robust end-state IS C, but C is only worth building if 1-min latency proves to ACTUALLY hinder the team. The poll is NOT throwaway: under C it becomes the mandatory 15-30min safety-net leg covering missed notifications / sub-expiry. So B is the foundation of every option.
- **рЯФі MANDATORY with the frequency bump = `flock` single-flight guard.** At 15-min an overlap was impossible; at `*/1` a slow run (token refresh + larger open set) can exceed 60s вЖТ two importers race the same upsert (real divergence risk вАФ this, not the frequency itself, is the unsafe part). House idiom (already used by `maltytask-kpi-recap` + `maltytask-ingest-recap`): `flock -n /tmp/maltytask-bc-orders.lock <cmd>` (`-n` = skip if a run is still going; next minute catches up). Importer itself is idempotent (echo-leg `mt:<id>`вЖТ`bc:<No>` + collision guard + full-open-set pull; no `--order` flag вАФ full pull is cheap, ~29 rows).
- **CRON EDIT:** source = `db/cron/maltytask-bc-orders.cron` in the maltyweb repo (NEVER the deployed `/etc/cron.d/*` вАФ overwritten on deploy). New line `*/1 вА¶ flock -n /tmp/maltytask-bc-orders.lock /usr/bin/python3 /var/www/maltytask/scripts/python/ingest_bc_sales_orders.py --apply >> /var/log/maltytask/bc-orders.log 2>&1` (drop `cd`, use absolute path, OR keep `cd && flock -c 'вА¶'` if the script is cwd-dependent вАФ verify first). Update header rationale + flock note. Deploy via `bin/deploy.sh --apply` AFTER confirming the shared tree is clean (parallel sessions live; deploy pushes the WORKING TREE). Verify: `/etc/cron.d/maltytask-bc-orders` shows the new line; watch one clean 1-min cycle in the log; `ps -ef | grep ingest_bc` shows no overlapping runs.
- **IF C is ever built (reference, not now):** endpoint `public/api/bc-order-webhook.php` (greenfield JSON endpoint, NOT a `require_login` page; self-authenticates via `clientState` secret in `config/bc.env`, e.g. `BC_WEBHOOK_CLIENT_STATE`); echo `?validationToken` as text/plain <5s on subscribe; never trust payload вЖТ GET the resource via existing `bc.env` OData creds; renewal cron `db/cron/maltytask-bc-webhook-renew.cron` daily (2-day slack on вЙ§3-day TTL), flock-guarded, MUST alarm to the operator-visible failure channel on failure (silent-death mode); fast-return via dirty-marker + the safety-net poll (avoid php-fpm exec of Python вАФ empty-PATH + ownership hazards). Demote the then-existing `*/1` poll to `*/15`-`*/30` safety-net.
- **EQUIP:** `coder`+`sql` for the cron edit (step 1 is a one-line cron change + flock wrap + deploy verify вАФ `coder` alone covers it; cite the flock single-flight idiom + commit-before-deploy/clean-shared-tree discipline). Add `webapp-testing` ONLY if/when the webhook endpoint (C) is built.
- **SEQUENCING:** (1) ship B+flock now вЖТ (2) re-evaluate after the team works live days вАФ only if 1-min lag is genuinely felt вЖТ (3) build C (webhook + demote poll to safety-net).
- **Trigger** "per-order"/"imm√©diat"/"near-real-time"/"webhook"/"15-min"/"1-min"/"poll frequency"/"latency"/"flock"/"subscription"/"bc-order-webhook" вЖТ this section.

## вЬЕ BC ORDERS READER вАФ DELIVERY-DATE SEMANTICS FIX + LEAD-TIME TRACKING вАФ SHIPPED 2026-06-15 (commit `9e2adfb`, LOCAL; mig 368)
**Corrects the fulfilment date that feeds the burn/couverture engine + the displayed "jour d'enl√®vement". Reader-only edit вАФ touches `ingest_bc_sales_orders.py` + mig 368 (NOT the 4 cage-session files).**
- **рЯФі ROOT CAUSE (Opus-audited LIVE):** the reader mapped `ord_orders.requested_date вЖР BC `Shipment_Date``, but BC leaves `Shipment_Date = Order_Date` (creation day) on **24/25** orders; header AND line `Requested/Promised_Delivery_Date` are EMPTY (**0/25**). The REAL delivery/loading-at-client date is BC **`Document_Date`** вАФ operator convention: *"la date du document est la date de chargement/livraison chez client"*; populated **25/25**, differs from creation in **21/25**. The 2026-06-15 BC-sole-source cutover dropped the delivery date the retired WeeklyOrders sheet used to carry вЖТ **burn/couverture (semaines_stock, forward seasonal sim) + the "jour d'enl√®vement" were running on CREATION dates** (systematically early вАФ false-early demand timing).
- **FIX:** `ingest_bc_sales_orders.py` now maps `requested_date вЖР Document_Date` on the INSERT leg, the refresher UPDATE leg, AND the echo-leg; collision date-compare aligned to Document_Date. Backfilled existing bc rows via `--backfill-dates` (**10 updated, 1 skipped: ORD210069 gone from the endpoint**).
- **рЯЖХ LEAD-TIME TRACKING (out-of-process orders вАФ Kouros: late / same-day orders must be flagged; normal ask = 24-48h processing).** **mig 368** adds `ord_orders.order_created_date DATE вЖР BC `Order_Date`` (backfilled). The flag is **DERIVED, NO stored column:** `lead_days = DATEDIFF(requested_date, order_created_date)`; convention `<=0` jour-m√™me (critical), `<2` tardive/sous-48h (warning), `>=2` normal. **рЯФі Threshold MUST live in a `system_settings` row** (section `'fulfilment'`, e.g. key `order_lead_time_warning_days` default 2) вАФ to be created in the UI phase, **NOT hardcoded** (house rule: never hardcode a system setting).
- **VERIFIED (Opus):** requested_date == Document_Date on live orders; `lead_days` across all 11 bc orders correct, **zero negative anomalies, all 3 tiers present (2 jour-m√™me ¬Ј 3 tardive ¬Ј 5 normal).**
- **вЬЕ UI BADGE SHIPPED 2026-06-15 (commit `3b69225`, on origin; mig 369 `369_fulfilment_lead_time_thresholds.sql`) вАФ closes this fix.** `expeditions.php` Commandes board shows **вЪ° <24h (critical, incl. jour-m√™me / negative-lead anomaly) / вП± 24-48h (warn) / вЙ•48h none.** `lead_days = DATEDIFF(requested_date, order_created_date)`, **DERIVED at display (NO stored column).** Thresholds in `system_settings` section `'fulfilment'`: `order_lead_time_critical_days=1` + `order_lead_time_warn_days=2` (r√©glables вАФ house rule honored, NOT hardcoded). NULL `order_created_date` вЖТ no badge. Smoke-verified: **2 critical / 3 warn / 5 normal.** рЯФі **IMPLEMENTATION NOTE (durable): `expeditions.php` needed an explicit `require_once` of `app/settings.php` at top вАФ `system_setting()` was NOT transitively loaded.** (Don't assume the settings accessor is in scope; grep before calling it from a page that doesn't already pull it.)
- **NB:** the EMAIL-ORDER INGESTION arc is now UNDER WAY вАФ Build B SCHEMA + SCAFFOLDING SHIPPED 2026-06-15 (migs 370; `646e18c`/`0c0bb5e`), see email-order-ingestion-arc.md ¬ІAS-BUILT. Still gated externally (Gmail DWD super-admin вЖТ Arthur; real per-sender parsers вЖТ Kouros sample .eml).
- **Trigger** "jour d'enl√®vement"/"date de chargement"/"Document_Date"/"Shipment_Date"/"lead time"/"jour-m√™me"/"tardive"/"sous-48h"/"order_created_date"/"requested_date semantics"/"couverture date" вЖТ this section.

**FRAME:** Phase 1 (read pull BC open orders вЖТ ord_orders, cron `*/15`) is LIVE (now incl. id=142/143/144 first --apply; was 4 bc rows pre-go-live), `source='bc'`, connector `scripts/python/ingest_bc_sales_orders.py`, cron `/etc/cron.d/maltytask-bc-orders`. This program makes maltytask the OPERATIONAL source of truth on top of BC (accounting record). Governing principle = operational metric вЙ† accounting ledger: stock/COGS derive from maltytask operational truth; BC = invoiced/shipped reality (locks at BL/posting) + reconciliation. **рЯФі `ord_orders.requested_date` = BC `Document_Date` (delivery/loading-at-client), NOT `Shipment_Date` вАФ fixed 2026-06-15 `9e2adfb`, see the BC ORDERS READER section directly above.**

**LIVE-STATE VERIFIED 2026-06-15 (PM probe), load-bearing for this program:**
- `ord_orders` = pure BC-mirror today (no operational-vs-mirror field split, no `origin` col beyond `source`). Cols as enumerated in the Phase-1 ¬І. `ord_order_lines` = `order_id_fk,sku_id_fk,qty,line_comment` вАФ **NO line_status col, NO BC-line snapshot.**
- **рЯФі NO BC line-snapshot store exists.** The connector pulls `SalesOrderSalesLines`, resolves `(bc_item,uom)вЖТsku_id`, writes `ord_order_lines`, and DISCARDS the BC line representation. Build B's divergence detection (maltytask line вЙ† BC line) has nothing to diff against вЖТ B REQUIRES persisting a BC line snapshot (per-line: bc_no, line_no, bc_item, uom, qty, resolved sku_id) so "what BC holds" is retained alongside "what maltytask holds".
- **рЯФі CONNECTOR DEVIATES FROM PHASE-1 RULING 4:** as-built it AUTO-ADVANCES status to `bl_printed` on `Completely_Shipped=True` (`should_advance_to_bl_printed()`, cron comment confirms). Ruling 4 said `Completely_Shipped` is a reconciliation SIGNAL surfaced on the board, NEVER an auto status write. This is a STANDING divergence to resolve as part of B (it writes unauthorized status from a pull). NB it does NOT fire depletion (fg-stock Step 4 keys on `status='shipped'` only, which the pull never writes) вАФ so no double-deplete today, but it IS the pull writing operator-owned status.
- **fg-stock Step 4** (`app/fg-stock.php`) sums ALL `ord_order_lines.qty` for `o.status='shipped'`, NO line-status filter. вЖТ Build C MUST add the line-status exclusion here or 'non_livre'/'rupture' lines deplete physical stock. (Also appears in snapshot Leg 1 ~L628/647/718/1079 вАФ the predicate must stay symmetric; grep all `ord_order_lines` reads.)
- **Manual form** `public/modules/expeditions.php` POST handler (L348, `view=form`): writes `order_type вИИ customer|internal`. `order_type='customer'` = the B2B double-entry path. `internal` (taproom/cage/shop/eshop-manual) is legitimately maltytask-native. Edit mode `?view=form&edit=<id>` read-only when statusвИИshipped|cancelled.

**RULING вАФ DATA MODEL (decision 2):** ord_orders evolves from "BC-mirror" to "operational record that may be BC-fed". Field classes:
  - **BC-mirror (pull-owned, refresher-gated on statusвИИentered|confirmed):** customer_id_fk, requested_date, transporter_id_fk, comment, line qtys+SKUs. NEVER status/status_events (operator-owned, ruling 4).
  - **maltytask-operational (NEVER flow to BC):** status + status_events, line_status (B/C), divergence flag (B). 
  - **origin:** keep `source` as the origin discriminator (`bc` vs `web`/`import`/`email`); when Phase 2 lands, a maltytask-born order = `source='web'`(or new `source='maltytask'`) that maltytask CREATED in BC вЖТ it carries a `bc_no` once BC assigns one, but its origin stays maltytask. Do NOT overload `source='bc'` for maltytask-born-then-echoed orders (that's the echo-loop trap, see D).
  - **Corrections (Pepitium, B):** edit-in-place + FLAG, do NOT create a new line revision. ord_order_lines stays the live operational truth; the BC-line snapshot retains the divergent BC value; the `divergence_status` flag on the order says "maltytask вЙ† BC, comptable correction required". Line-revision history lives in `ord_order_status_events`-style append log only if Kouros later wants an audit trail вАФ NOT needed for v1.

**SEQUENCING (decision 1):** **A вЖТ (B вИ• C) вЖТ D.**
  - **A FIRST (small, urgent, stops active bleeding).** Block manual B2B (`order_type='customer'`) creation in the saisie form. DECISION: block-B2B-but-ALLOW-internal вАФ `internal` orders (taproom/cage/shop/eshop-manual) are legit maltytask-native and have no BC source. Hide/disable the customer-order branch of `view=form` POST + UI; keep `internal` create; keep EDIT of bc-sourced orders (logistics still needs to correct lines вАФ that's exactly what feeds B). Server-side reject `order_type='customer'` on create (defence-in-depth, not just hide the radio). ~0.5 day. Mig: none.
  - **B вИ• C (operational-layer additions, parallelizable, both small):**
    - **C (line status 'non_livre'/'rupture'):** mig adds `ord_order_lines.line_status ENUM('to_fulfil','non_livre','rupture') DEFAULT 'to_fulfil'` (or 2-val if ruptureвЙ°non_livre вАФ confirm w/ Kouros whether they need to distinguish "supplier rupture" from "operationally undeliverable"). Excluded from fg-stock Step 4 + ALL ord_order_lines depletion reads (add `AND l.line_status='to_fulfil'`); NEVER flows to BC (it's a maltytask-only fact вАФ nothing shipped); reportable as a backorder/lost-sales view on the Commandes board. ~1 day.
    - **B (divergence flag + BC line snapshot):** mig adds (1) BC line-snapshot store вАФ prefer a sibling table `ord_order_bc_lines` (bc_no/source_ref, line_no, bc_item, uom, bc_qty, resolved_sku_id, snapshot_at) over widening ord_order_lines (keeps the two facts cleanly separable; schema_meta row required); (2) `ord_orders.divergence_status ENUM('none','correction_compta_requise') DEFAULT 'none'` (+ optional divergence_detail). Connector change: on each pull, persist the BC snapshot AND diff resolved BC lines vs current ord_order_lines вЖТ if they differ AND the order is frozen (statusвЙ•picked, ruling 4) OR an operator edited a line away from BC вЖТ set divergence flag + surface (Commandes badge + doc_review_queue type `bc-order-correction-required` for admin). Also RESOLVE the ruling-4 deviation here (auto-advance bl_printed вЖТ reconciliation signal, not status write). Operational truth (maltytask DGDB) drives stock/COGS; admin issues the BC credit-note+re-invoice manually (interim). ~2 days incl. the connector refactor + Opus-verify the snapshot/diff doesn't perturb the live status-preserving upsert.
  - **D LAST but STARTS IN PARALLEL as a spike (the big arc).** Architecture decisions below; build after A/B/C land the model it writes against.

**RULING вАФ PHASE 2 WRITE-BACK ARCHITECTURE (decision 3), the hard parts:**
  - **(a) ECHO-LOOP:** maltytask creates order in BC вЖТ `*/15` reader pulls it back вЖТ MUST NOT duplicate. Mechanism = maltytask writes a maltytask-owned external ref into a BC field the reader keys on; reader's source_ref upsert (`bc:<No>`) is already idempotent on BC OrderNo, but the maltytask-born order has a LOCAL id BEFORE BC assigns a No. **Resolve by: maltytask-born order gets a provisional local source_ref (`mt:<localid>`); on successful BC create, store the returned BC No and REKEY source_ref вЖТ `bc:<No>` in the SAME write transaction; the reader then matches it as existing on next pull (UPDATE not INSERT).** Do NOT rely on External_Document_No for echo identity (see b).
  - **(b) рЯФі External_Document_No DUAL-USE COLLISION вАФ FLAG:** Kouros ALREADY uses BC `External_Document_No` to distinguish SPLIT orders (same customer, different location). Writing maltytask refs into it would COLLIDE with that operational use. вЖТ Phase 2 must NOT hijack External_Document_No for the maltytask echo ref. Use a DISTINCT BC field (a custom field e.g. `MaltytaskRef`, or `Your_Reference`, or the Shopify-style `ShpfyOrderNo` pattern of a dedicated custom column) вАФ confirm with Kouros which BC field is free. This is a hard prerequisite for D's create path.
  - **(c) IDEMPOTENCY + PARTIAL FAILURE:** every write carries the maltytask local id as the dedup key (the provisional ref); a create that times out but actually landed in BC must not double-create on retry вЖТ before create, GET BC by the maltytask ref; create only if absent. Wrap create+rekey in a local transaction; if BC create succeeds but local rekey fails, a reconcile pass (the reader) recovers by matching the BC ref back to the local provisional row.
  - **(d) CREDIT-MEMO (Pepitium):** create avoir (`salesCreditMemos`) for the wrong locked invoice + corrected re-invoice. Start with CREATE only (per Kouros: CREATE orders + credit memos; POST stays human in BC). The B-flag (`correction_compta_requise`) is the queue that feeds D's credit-memo generation.
  - **(e) BC API CHOICE:** standard `salesOrders` / `salesCreditMemos` POST (the standard Business Central v2.0 API) for CREATE вАФ cleaner than OData web services for writes, supports the standard entity shapes. Reuse the S2S OAuth2 client-creds from `config/bc.env`. (The read side uses OData `SalesOrder`/`SalesOrderSalesLines` web services for richer fields; writes can use the standard API independently.) BC write permission = Kouros's BC-side permission-set change (SUPER role, Entra has API.ReadWrite.All) вАФ he does it himself; we build assuming it lands. **Start with CREATE, NEVER POST (no posting/invoicing from maltytask initially вАФ keep that human in BC).**

**RULING вАФ PHASE-1 READER CHANGES when Phase 2 coexists (decision 4):**
  - Status-preserving upsert UNCHANGED in spirit (status operator-owned), but the reader must learn to RECONCILE maltytask-born orders: a pull row whose maltytask-ref matches a local `mt:`/rekeyed `bc:` row = UPDATE (the echo), never a new INSERT. вЖТ reader keys on the maltytask ref FIRST, then `bc:<No>`.
  - **Collision logic is NOT YET External_Document_No-aware (deferred per Phase-1).** With B/C/D: it STILL doesn't need External_Document_No for echo (we use a distinct maltytask ref, decision 3b). BUT вАФ because External_Document_No legitimately splits same-customer/different-location orders вАФ the reader must NOT treat two BC orders sharing a customer as one; it already keys on BC OrderNo (unique), so split orders stay distinct. **No change forced by B/C/D, but the deferred External_Document_No-awareness should be revisited IF Kouros ever wants the board to GROUP split orders вАФ flag, don't build.**
  - `bc_completely_shipped вЖТ bl_printed` auto-advance: REMOVE it (ruling 4) as part of B; replace with reconciliation signal. Once removed, the reader never writes status at all вАФ clean separation Phase 2 depends on.

**DIVERGENCE FLAGS (this program):**
  - **рЯФі Echo-loop double-create** (D) вАФ guarded by maltytask-ref-first reconcile + GET-before-create idempotency.
  - **рЯФі External_Document_No dual-use** (D) вАФ do NOT use it for echo identity; it's Kouros's split-order key. Use a distinct BC field.
  - **рЯФі Double-deplete via new line statuses** (C) вАФ fg-stock Step 4 + all ord_order_lines depletion reads MUST exclude non_livre/rupture; Opus independently verifies the no-deplete invariant (COGS/inventory-bearing).
  - **рЯФі Breaking the LIVE Phase-1 reader** вАФ B refactors the connector (snapshot + diff + remove auto-advance); regression-gate the status-preserving upsert (no unauthorized status writes, no spurious INSERT) before `--apply`. The reader is operationally hot (`*/15`).
  - **Parallel store** вАФ `ord_order_bc_lines` (BC snapshot) is NOT a second copy of ord_order_lines; it is the retained BC-side fact for diffing. Keep them distinct-by-purpose; never let anyone "reconcile" them as one (they DIVERGE by design вАФ that's the whole point of B).
  - **COGS coupling** вАФ operational truth (ord_orders/lines, post-correction) drives fg-stock depletion + COGS; BC reconciled via avoir. A correction (Pepitium DGDFвЖТDGDB) changes which SKU depletes вЖТ COGS-bearing вЖТ Opus verifies the corrected line depletes the right SKU.

**EQUIP per build:** A вЖТ `coder`+`ui`(+`webapp-testing` smoke the customer-create block + internal-create still works). C вЖТ `sql`+`coder`+`ui`(+`webapp-testing`) [DONE `59bd1f7`]. B вЖТ `sql`+`coder`(+`ui` badge +`webapp-testing`); COGS/status-bearing вЖТ Opus independent verify [DONE `2f0087e`]. D вЖТ `coder`+`sql`(+`webapp-testing`); spike the BC standard-API CREATE against a test order first; the credit-memo path is the careful part. **MIGRATIONS:** A=none; C=line_status ENUM on ord_order_lines (INSTANT) [357]; B=`ord_order_bc_lines` table (schema_meta row) + `ord_orders.divergence_status` ENUM [354/355]; D=likely `bc_no` col on ord_orders + the maltytask-ref handling (confirm at build). Re-`migrate.php --status` at build-start (parallel sessions lead; head was 357 + 59bd1f7). Trigger "block manual B2B"/"double-entry"/"Pepitium"/"correction compta"/"avoir"/"credit memo"/"non livr√©"/"rupture"/"backorder"/"write-back"/"Phase 2 BC"/"External_Document_No"/"echo loop"/"divergence flag order" вЖТ READ this section.
