## ¬ІD LAUNCH-READY SCOPE вАФ Phase 2 write-back maltytaskвЖТBC (PM-scoped 2026-06-15, A/B/C all landed)

> Greenfield. No BC-write code exists in either repo. D is OUTWARD-FACING (the first thing maltytask ever writes back to the accounting system) вЖТ **the disarm discipline below is non-negotiable: NO agent POSTs to BC live without Kouros's explicit go.** Built assuming Kouros's BC write perm-set lands; confirm the exact perm name (¬І3) before any live test.

**SPLIT D INTO TWO SUB-PHASES вАФ D1 (order-create) ships and proves first; D2 (credit-memo) is the careful Pepitium path, built after D1's echo-loop+idempotency are proven live.** Reason: D1 exercises the WHOLE write spine (OAuth2 S2S create, provisional-ref вЖТ rekey, GET-before-create idempotency, reader-reconcile) on the simpler entity; D2 reuses that proven spine for the harder `salesCreditMemos` + DGDFвЖТDGDB correction. Don't build D2 until D1's echo loop is verified non-duplicating on a live `*/15` pull.

### 1. BUILD STEPS вАФ dependency order

**D0 вАФ SPIKE (read-only, no writes, do FIRST):**
- Stand up an OAuth2 S2S token call against the standard BC v2.0 API (`/v2.0/companies({id})/salesOrders`) reusing `config/bc.env` client-creds вАФ confirm the standard API endpoint authenticates with the SAME app reg the OData read side uses (the read side uses OData web services; the standard API is a different base path вАФ verify the token scope covers both, this is the #1 spike risk).
- **GET-probe the chosen echo field is free across the live order set** (¬І3b): the prior probe found `Your_Reference` 0/21 empty вАФ RE-RUN it at build-start (orders move). Pick the BC field for `MaltytaskRef` and confirm with Kouros it doesn't collide with anything BUT `External_Document_No` (which is reserved for his split-order key вАФ HARD do-not-touch).
- Output: a dry-run module that can READ a salesOrder by the echo field and print "would create" вАФ zero writes. Gate D1 on this passing + Kouros confirming the perm name + echo field.

**D1 вАФ ORDER-CREATE (build after D0 + A/B/C):**
- **Schema (mig, confirm number at build вАФ head 357+):** `ord_orders.bc_no VARCHAR(40) NULL` (the BC-assigned OrderNo, populated on successful create вАФ distinct from `source_ref`); reuse `source` as origin (a maltytask-born order = `source='maltytask'` NEW enum value, or `'web'` вАФ confirm; do NOT overload `'bc'`). The provisional/rekey identity rides on the EXISTING `source_ref` col (`mt:<localid>` вЖТ `bc:<No>`). schema_meta: ord_orders already classified вАФ update its row note, no new table for D1.
- **Writer/worker module path:** `scripts/python/push_bc_sales_orders.py` (mirror the read connector `ingest_bc_sales_orders.py` вАФ same `_load_bc_env`/`_get_token`/company-id resolution; standard-API base path for writes). Drains maltytask-born orders flagged for push. **`--dry-run` DEFAULT, `--apply` explicit, flock'd, cron DISARMED at ship.** (Python to match the existing BC connector toolchain, NOT a PHP handler вАФ the BC integration lives in `scripts/python/`.)
- **What triggers a push:** a maltytask-NATIVE customer order created in the app. NB after A, manual `order_type='customer'` is BLOCKED in the saisie form вАФ so D1's create source is whatever NEW maltytask-native B2B entry path Kouros wants (confirm: is there a maltytask-born B2B order in v1, or is D1 purely the echo-safe plumbing for a future entry path? A blocked all manual customer entry, so D1 may have NO live producer yet вАФ clarify scope with Kouros; if no producer, D1 = build the spine + test against a synthetic flagged row, ship disarmed).
- **REKEY mechanism (echo-loop guard, ruling 3a):** maltytask-born order gets provisional `source_ref='mt:<localid>'` at creation. On successful BC create: in ONE local txn, store returned `bc_no` + REKEY `source_ref вЖТ 'bc:<No>'` + write `MaltytaskRef=<localid>` into the chosen BC field. The `*/15` reader (ruling 4) keys on the maltytask-ref FIRST then `bc:<No>` вЖТ matches the echoed pull as EXISTING (UPDATE, never INSERT).
- **IDEMPOTENCY guard (ruling 3c):** before every create, GET BC by `MaltytaskRef=<localid>`; create ONLY if absent. Wrap create+rekey in a local txn; if BC create succeeds but local rekey fails, the reader's reconcile pass recovers (matches BC ref вЖТ local provisional row). Every write carries the local id as dedup key.
- **Reader change (ruling 4 вАФ already partly done in B):** confirm the connector keys maltytask-ref-first; B already removed the `bc_completely_shippedвЖТbl_printed` auto-advance (reader writes NO status). D1 only adds the maltytask-ref-first match precedence if B didn't.
- **Excluded lines:** non_livre/rupture lines (C's line_status) MUST be EXCLUDED from the BC write вАФ nothing operationally-undeliverable gets written to the accounting order. Filter `line_status='to_fulfil'` in the push payload assembly (mirrors fg-stock's depletion gate).

**D2 вАФ CREDIT-MEMO (build after D1 proven live):**
- **Producer:** B's `ord_orders.divergence_status='correction_compta_requise'` flag (set when maltytask line вЙ† frozen BC line, e.g. Pepitium DGDFвЖТDGDB) is the QUEUE that feeds D2. D2 drains flagged orders.
- **Path:** create `salesCreditMemos` (avoir) for the wrong locked invoice + the corrected re-invoice, against the standard BC v2.0 API. Same OAuth2/idempotency/echo spine as D1 (GET-before-create on a memo-level ref; rekey). **CREATE ONLY вАФ NEVER POST the memo** (posting/invoicing stays human in BC).
- **COGS coupling (ruling, Opus verifies):** the correction changes which SKU depletes (DGDFвЖТDGDB) вЖТ operational truth (ord_order_lines post-correction) already drives fg-stock depletion; the avoir only reconciles BC. Opus independently verifies the corrected line depletes the RIGHT SKU before D2 writes anything.
- **Careful-path note:** credit-memo entity shape + the avoirвЖФre-invoice pairing is the riskiest write. Spike it read-only (GET an existing credit memo, map its shape) before any create.

### 2. DISARM / DRY-RUN DESIGN вАФ what MUST stay disarmed until Kouros's explicit go
- **Both `push_bc_sales_orders.py` and the D2 credit-memo writer ship `--dry-run` DEFAULT; live write requires explicit `--apply`.** NO cron entry at ship (the file may exist in `db/cron/` commented-out or simply absent вАФ DISARMED = no `*/N` schedule writing to BC).
- **Triple gate before any live `--apply`:** (i) Kouros confirms the BC write perm-set is live (¬І3); (ii) Kouros confirms the chosen echo field (¬І3b) is free + not `External_Document_No`; (iii) Kouros gives explicit "go for live BC write". Until all three: dry-run only, against a synthetic/test order, output = "would create {payload}" with the full JSON body printed for Kouros to eyeball.
- **PM standing order: NO agent issues a live BC POST/PATCH/create.** A build agent may build + dry-run + (with Kouros's go) run ONE supervised `--apply` against a single test order that Kouros nominates. Bulk/cron enablement is Kouros's hand only.
- **First live test = ONE order Kouros picks**, verified round-trip: create in BC вЖТ confirm `bc_no` returned + `MaltytaskRef` written вЖТ wait one `*/15` pull вЖТ confirm reader UPDATEs (no duplicate INSERT) вЖТ confirm no spurious status write. Only after that round-trip passes does D1 graduate from disarmed.

### 3a. ECHO-FIELD + READER-LEG RULINGS (PM 2026-06-15, D0-probe-driven вАФ supersede the earlier "echo=Your_Reference" line)

**вЬЕ D1 DONE + LIVE-PROVEN + DISARMED + COMMITTED (`7db6861` on main, LOCAL-ONLY вАФ awaiting Kouros "push"; recorded 2026-06-15).** Both Opus-flagged design issues below were RESOLVED and a live supervised round-trip passed clean (Kouros-authorized, executed by Opus). AS-BUILT:
- **Resolution: Path A taken** (write via OData `SalesOrder` entity, echo = `Your_Reference`; `External_Document_No` left untouched/reserved for Kouros's split-order key вАФ ISSUE 1 fork closed in favour of A).
- **Writer `scripts/python/push_bc_sales_orders.py`** (deployed): creates BC SalesOrder via OData `NAV.SalesOrder` + `SalesOrderSalesLines`; echo tag `Your_Reference='mt:<id>'`; GET-before-create idempotency on `Your_Reference`; atomic local rekey `mt:<id>`вЖТ`bc:<No>` + `bc_no` on success; ONLY `line_status='to_fulfil'` lines pushed (non_livre/rupture excluded вАФ C dependency); DISARMED = `--dry-run` default, live needs BOTH `--apply` AND `--i-have-kouros-go`, NO cron. Admin helpers `--delete-bc` (composite key + If-Match) + `--make-test-order`/`--cleanup-test-order`.
- **Reader `scripts/python/ingest_bc_sales_orders.py`** (deployed, LIVE on the `*/15` cron): echo-leg added as precedence 1 (ISSUE 2 fix) вАФ matches a pulled BC order by parsed `Your_Reference`вЖТlocal PK REGARDLESS of `source_ref` state, rekeys in one txn, writes NO status/status_events (Ruling 4). Closes the race/rekey-failure duplicate gap.
- **Shared helper `scripts/python/bc_echo.py`** = `bc_echo_format`/`bc_echo_parse`, imported by BOTH connectors (namespace can't drift вАФ [[feedback_canonical_list_call_not_copy]]).
- **mig 361 APPLIED** = `ord_orders.bc_no VARCHAR(40)` + `source` ENUM +`'maltytask'`.
- **LIVE ROUND-TRIP (2026-06-15):** synthetic maltytask order id=157 вЖТ live OData create вЖТ BC No=ORD210076, `Your_Reference='mt:157'` set, only the to_fulfil line (ALT4) pushed / rupture excluded вЖТ rekeyed local to `bc:ORD210076` вЖТ reader dry-run printed `[echo-leg] Would rekey local_id=157` + `Would INSERT: 0` (zero duplicate, no status write) вЖТ deleted ORD210076 from BC (composite-key + If-Match) вЖТ cleaned local back to 138. Nothing left in BC or DB.
- **рЯФі CRITICAL BC-PERMISSION LEARNING (cost many cycles вАФ durable):** writing sales orders via the BC API requires **`D365 BUS FULL ACCESS`** on the S2S app's BC user. `D365 SALES DOC, EDIT` + `POST` + `D365 READ` are NOT sufficient вАФ they don't cover the API entity buffer table **5495 (Sales Order Entity Buffer)**, giving a MISLEADING `HTTP 403 вА¶ TableData 5495 вА¶ Insert` that looks like a missing sales-doc grant. (This SUPERSEDES the ¬І3 guidance that `D365 SALES DOC, EDIT` is the load-bearing grant for D вАФ see ¬І3 note.) To EDIT the app's permission grid you must first set √Йtat=D√©sactiv√©, re-enable after (grid is locked while Activ√© вАФ why earlier add-attempts silently failed). Azure side was fine throughout (token carried `roles=['API.ReadWrite.All']`).
- **Two code gotchas found+fixed during the test:** (1) `NAV.SalesOrder` has NO text `Comment` property (it's a boolean flag) вЖТ HTTP 400 if sent; (2) `NAV.SalesOrder`/`SalesOrderSalesLines` use a COMPOSITE key (Document_Type+No / +Line_No) and DELETE needs `If-Match`.
- **рЯФі OPEN SCOPING (divergence flag вАФ still stands):** D1 has NO maltytask-native order PRODUCER in v1 (block A removed manual customer entry). The writer is proven plumbing with NOTHING to push in prod until either D2's producer materializes OR a re-opened maltytask-born B2B entry path exists. Flag, don't paper over.
- **вЮ°пЄП NEXT = D2 (salesCreditMemos for Pepitium DGDFвЖТDGDB), which REUSES this proven spine.**

---
_Pre-D1 ruling history (resolved above; kept for the reasoning trail):_
**Built disarmed: writer `push_bc_sales_orders.py` + mig 361 (`ord_orders.bc_no` + source enum +`'maltytask'`) exist, Python-only, apply path raises NotImplementedError, nothing committed. Opus verification caught 2 design issues вЖТ PM ruled.**

**ISSUE 1 вАФ echo field (REJECT the coder's `externalDocumentNumber`='mt:<id>' choice).** D0 found `Your_Reference` does NOT exist on the standard v2.0 write API (only OData `Your_Reference`); the only filterable echo on v2.0 is `externalDocumentNumber` = `External_Document_No` вАФ which is RESERVED as Kouros's split-order key (HARD do-not-touch). So the coder's choice collides with a reserved field вЖТ rejected. FORK (one Kouros decision, re-run D0 first):
- **Path A (PREFERRED) вАФ write via the OData `SalesOrder` entity (the SAME entity the reader reads), set `Your_Reference` there.** Keeps echo=`Your_Reference`, leaves `External_Document_No` free. Challenge the D0 "v2.0 is the only write surface" premise вАФ verify OData `SalesOrder` accepts POST/PATCH under the S2S token scope. Clean: write+read leg ride the same entity/field, no standardвЖФOData identity gymnastics.
- **Path B (fallback, only if OData write not viable) вАФ `External_Document_No` with strict `mt:` namespace, REQUIRES Kouros's explicit sign-off** (co-opts his field). Collision risk is REAL not moot: only ever write `mt:<id>` there pre-publish on maltytask-born orders that have NO customer external ref by construction; a maltytask-born order needing a real external ref = a DIFFERENT path, must not use this leg. Reader discriminates on `mt:` prefix. Strictly worse than A.
- **Field identity CONFIRMED:** standard-v2.0 `externalDocumentNumber` вЙ° OData `External_Document_No` вЙ° same BC SQL column; OData `Your_Reference` вЙ° BC `Your_Reference` column. Whichever the writer sets, the reader adds the same-named field to its OData `$select` (L262) and sees it. (Reader uses OData `SalesOrder`/`SalesOrderSalesLines` entities, NOT v2.0.)

**ISSUE 2 вАФ reader echo-tag leg is MISSING (real duplicate defect; coder's "uniq_ord_source_ref blocks it" claim is WRONG вАФ `mt:<id>` vs `bc:<No>` are different keys, no collision).** Reader (`ingest_bc_sales_orders.py`) matches ONLY `existing_bc.get(f"bc:{no}")` (~L669), never the echo field вЖТ if `*/15` reader runs between BC-create and local rekey (or rekey fails), it INSERTs a duplicate + orphans the `mt:<id>` row. DESIGN (the missing ruling-4 leg):
- **Precedence in `upsert_order()` + every sibling helper resolving `existing` from `existing_bc.get(source_ref)`, first-match-wins:** (1) ECHO-TAG LEG (NEW, FIRST): parse echo field; if `mt:<id>` вЖТ look up LOCAL row by PK `id=<id>` REGARDLESS of its current `source_ref`; if provisional `mt:<id>` вЖТ REKEY in one txn `SET bc_no=<No>, source_ref='bc:<No>'` (recovery path); if already `bc:<No>` вЖТ plain header-refresh; either way return `"update"` вЖТ duplicate INSERT impossible (matched on invariant local id). (2) EXISTING `bc:<No>` LEG (current). (3) COLLISION/BACKLOG/INSERT (current) вАФ only for genuinely new BC-originated orders.
- **Writes ONLY:** `bc_no`, `source_ref` rekey, `updated_at`, existing header-refresh fields. **NO status, NO status_events** (Ruling 4 вАФ reader writes no status; status operator-owned).
- **Idempotent** (keyed on invariant local id) + **status-safe** (respect the SAME refreshable-status gate as the existing UPDATE; if matched row's status is beyond refreshable = operator picked/printed вЖТ key-recovery ONLY (`bc_no` + rekey if still provisional), NO header refresh, NO status touch, NEVER re-advance вАФ mirrors leg-2 "frozen, key-only").
- **CONNECTOR-ONLY edit** (`ingest_bc_sales_orders.py` reader + `push_bc_sales_orders.py` writer); touches NONE of the 4 cage-session files. webapp-testing stays optional.
- **SHARED HELPER = MANDATORY:** one pair `bc_echo_format(local_id)->'mt:<id>'` / `bc_echo_parse(echo)->Optional[int]`, imported by BOTH connectors so the namespace can't drift ([[feedback_canonical_list_call_not_copy]] applied to the echo namespace вАФ never inline `'mt:'+str(id)` on both sides).
- `bc_completely_shippedвЖТbl_printed` auto-advance confirmed GONE вАФ does NOT change this design, it's a PREREQUISITE the echo leg depends on (reader writes no status).

**COMMIT SEQUENCE (PM-ratified):** do NOT commit the current disarmed state. (1) Resolve ISSUE 1 with Kouros FIRST (re-run D0 OData-write probe вЖТ pick A or B вЖТ Kouros sign-off if B) вАФ the field choice is a Kouros decision (touches his split-order convention), NOT a coder call. (2) THEN dispatch ONE coordinated coder: reader echo-tag leg + shared helper + writer sets resolved echo field via resolved surface. (3) THEN Opus independently dry-run-verifies the duplicate-prevention invariant (simulate broken path: local still `mt:<id>`, reader pulls `bc:<No>`+echo вЖТ assert UPDATE/rekey, zero INSERT) вАФ COGS/order-integrity-bearing, not on sub-agent's word. (4) THEN commit the disarmed whole (both connectors + mig, `--dry-run` default, no cron). Live write stays triple-gated on Kouros.

### 3. BC PERMISSION / SCOPE NAME вАФ confirm with Kouros BEFORE any live test
- **API auth scope (Entra/app-reg level):** the S2S app needs `API.ReadWrite.All` (application permission) on the Dynamics 365 Business Central API вАФ Kouros said Entra already has it. CONFIRM it's `API.ReadWrite.All`, not the read-only `API.Read.All`. This is the OAuth2 scope the token request asks for (`scope=https://api.businesscentral.dynamics.com/.default`).
- **рЯФі BC permission-set (in-product, per the S2S app's BC user) вАФ CORRECTED BY D1 LIVE TEST (see ¬І3a as-built):** the load-bearing grant is **`D365 BUS FULL ACCESS`**, NOT `D365 SALES DOC, EDIT`. EDIT+POST+READ do NOT cover the API entity buffer table **5495 (Sales Order Entity Buffer)** вЖТ misleading `HTTP 403 вА¶ TableData 5495 вА¶ Insert`. To edit the app's permission grid, set √Йtat=D√©sactiv√© first then re-enable. (The original guidance below was wrong вАФ kept struck for the trail.) ~~For D1 we need `D365 SALES DOC, EDIT`~~.
- **¬І3b echo field:** confirm which BC field carries `MaltytaskRef` вАФ `Your_Reference` (probed 0/21 empty) is the leading candidate; NOT `External_Document_No` (split-order key, reserved).

### 4. EQUIP line
**EQUIP D (D0 spike + D1): `coder` + `sql` + `webapp-testing`** (no UI surface in D itself вАФ it's a backend connector; webapp-testing only if a push-status badge gets added to the Commandes board, otherwise drop it). D writes Python in `scripts/python/` (BC-connector toolchain) вЖТ `coder` covers it; `sql` for the `bc_no`/source enum migration + the reader-reconcile query. **D2 adds nothing to EQUIP** (same skills). **GATING: external-write + COGS/order-integrity-bearing вЖТ Opus INDEPENDENTLY verifies (a) the echo-loop produces NO duplicate on a live pull, (b) D2's corrected line depletes the right SKU, (c) every write is GET-before-create idempotent вАФ sub-agent "it works" is a CLAIM.** Disarm discipline (¬І2) is a HARD gate, not advisory.

### 5. C DEPENDENCIES + SPLIT RECOMMENDATION
- **What D depends on from C:** D1's push-payload assembly EXCLUDES `line_status IN ('non_livre','rupture')` lines (only `to_fulfil` lines get written to BC) вАФ this is C's column. C is DONE+LIVE (mig 357), so the dependency is satisfied. No other C surface is load-bearing for D.
- **What D depends on from B:** B's `divergence_status='correction_compta_requise'` flag is D2's QUEUE; B's connector refactor (snapshot + reader keys on ref, auto-advance removed) is the reader side D1's echo-reconcile rides on. B is DONE (`2f0087e`) вАФ satisfied. **Verify at D-build-start that B actually removed the `bc_completely_shippedвЖТbl_printed` auto-advance** (it was flagged as a ruling-4 deviation to fix IN B; if B shipped without it, D1 must remove it as a prerequisite вАФ the reader must write NO status for the clean Phase-2 separation).
- **SPLIT: YES вАФ D1 (order-create) first, D2 (credit-memo) second.** D1 proves the write spine (OAuth2 create, provisionalвЖТrekey, GET-before-create, reader-reconcile, line_status exclusion) on the simple entity + the live echo-loop round-trip; D2 reuses the proven spine for the harder avoir/re-invoice + DGDFвЖТDGDB correction. Do NOT start D2 until D1's echo loop is verified non-duplicating live.

## рЯЧВпЄП ARCHIVED INDEX SHIPPED-ARCS-REGISTER POINTER (compacted from index 2026-06-15)
_Verbatim fat Fulfilment/Exp√©ditions pointer (eshop-repacking + forward-seasonal-burn + Historique + historical-Commandes lane + full Shopify build) relocated from the index during memory compaction. ## ¬ІRETURNED FG TRACKING (BC-DERIVED) вАФ ARC AS-BUILT 2026-06-16 (P0+P1+P2+P3-SYNTH√ИSE SHIPPED+LIVE; P3-RATE+P2b OPEN; 4 LOCAL COMMITS NOT PUSHED + 2 FRONTEND FILES DEFERRED-FROM-COMMIT)

**Scope (Kouros-APPROVED вАФ BC-DERIVED PIVOT, supersedes the earlier order-XOR scoped design that was "to be written once Kouros approves").** Returns are **BC-derived**: the bookkeeper books an *avoir de vente* (credit memo) in Business Central вЖТ it imports to `inv_sales_ledger` as `doc_type='credit'` (also `return_receipt` for some). **BC OWNS REVENUE вАФ the avoir reverses it; the app writes NO revenue/COGS-ledger entry.** The app owns DISPOSITION + physical FG only. **Default disposition = `quarantine`** (no FG effect until operator confirms restock).

**DISPOSITION TAXONOMY (per line, the cardinal decision) = enum extended to `restock / scrap / quarantine / rebate`:**
- `restock` = re-enters FG (resaleable) вАФ the ONE FG/COGS-bearing leg.
- `scrap` = write-off (hygiene/best-before) вАФ NO FG effect.
- `quarantine` = held pending decision (DEFAULT) вАФ NOT yet in stock.
- `rebate` = a beer-credit that is a price/defect rebate, NOT a physical return вАФ NO FG effect (added in mig 376).

**PM's earlier rulings CONFIRMED CORRECT against live data (recorded so nobody re-litigates):**
- `fg_stock_compute()` reads NO ledger `doc_type`s вАФ physique = anchor + prod вИТ shipped вИТ eshop вИТ taproom. So BC credits did NOT auto-replenish physique (they only affect the burn-velocity engine, which nets all doc_types). Therefore the restock leg is genuinely **ADDITIVE** (a new returns-in flow), NOT a suppression/avoid-double-count. The Q1 correction was right.
- **Beer-vs-deposit split = `ref_skus.recipe_id IS NOT NULL`** (CAUF/CAUAL/CO2 have NO recipe вЖТ deposit lines). Beer-credit lines = the returned FG; deposit lines вЙИ all kegs back. The queue lists only beer-SKU lines.

**P0 вАФ SCHEMA (APPLIED LIVE):**
- mig **373** `373_ord_returns.sql` вАФ `ord_returns` (header) + `ord_return_lines` (`sku_id_fk` RESTRICT, `qty>0` CHECK, per-line disposition enum). Originally carried an order-XOR origin CHECK `chk_ord_returns_exactly_one_origin`. schema_meta rows added.
- mig **376** `376_returns_bc_derived_origin.sql` вАФ the BC-derived pivot: **DROPPED the order-XOR CHECK**; **ADDED `origin_bc_document_no` + `origin_posting_date`** as the canonical origin (the avoir is the origin, not an order); **EXTENDED disposition enum to add `rebate`**; **ADDED `origin_ledger_sku_code`**. Both applied live. MIG HEAD now 376, next free = 377 (re-`migrate.php --status` at build start вАФ parallel sessions live).

**P1 вАФ DISPOSITION QUEUE (LIVE):** `?view=retours` in `public/modules/expeditions.php`. Lists beer-SKU `credit`/`return_receipt` ledger lines **awaiting disposition** (NOT EXISTS join on `bc_document_no` + `sku`), grouped by avoir; operator tags disposition per line (default **Quarantaine**). POST handler **re-queries the ledger for server-authoritative qty + posting_date** (operator CANNOT alter qty), **idempotent** (partial disposition supported вАФ only un-dispositioned lines insert), txn + `log_revision`. CSS `exp-ret-*` in `expeditions.css`.

**P2 вАФ FG RESTOCK LEG (LIVE + OPUS-VERIFIED):** `app/fg-stock.php`:
- **Step 6.7** (in `fg_stock_compute()`) + **Leg 4** (in `fg_stock_location_snapshot()`, 100% to the eshop-warehouse site, flagged `ASSUMPTION-restock-site-warehouse-2026-06-16`).
- Condition: `disposition='restock' AND origin_posting_date > anchor` (STRICT `>`) вЖТ adds to physique.
- **Opus-verified on LIVE DB** (rolled-back txn, anchor 2026-06-15, ZEPF): restock +5 вЖТ physique +5 exactly; **ќ£cards == ќ£physique held (diff 0.0000) at every step**; `scrap` вЖТ 0 movement; self-cleaned. VPS backup `fg-stock.php.bak-pre-p2-*`.
- DORMANT until a real `restock` disposition exists (0 today).

**P3-RATE вАФ RETURN-RATE KPI вАФ DEFERRED (needs Kouros design decision; SURFACE don't guess).** Denominator design is undecided: returned √Ј ordered вАФ **which denominator** (BC shipments vs `ord_orders`), and **how to match a return to its origin sale** given the avoir does NOT always link to the original invoice in our ledger. Do NOT guess the matching/denominator вАФ it is sales/COGS-adjacent. **DISTINCT from P3-SYNTH√ИSE below вАФ do not conflate.**

**P3-SYNTH√ИSE вАФ RETURNS 90-DAY SUMMARY вАФ DONE + LIVE 2026-06-16 (volume + disposition-mix, NOT a rate).** Kouros chose a **volume + disposition-mix synth√®se, NOT a ratio** (no denominator), surfaced on **BOTH** the Retours tab AND Mon-tableau. Shared-compute `app/returns-synthese.php::returns_synthese(PDO $pdo, int $periodDays=90): array`:
- `by_client` вАФ grouped **per `bc_document_no`** (customer resolved from `inv_sales_ledger`). рЯФі v1 KNOWN LIMIT: a client with 2 avoirs shows TWICE (grouping is per credit-note, not per customer) вАФ accepted; aggregate-by-customer later if wanted.
- `by_beer` вАФ `ref_recipes.name` (join ref_skus.recipe_idвЖТref_recipes.id).
- disposition mix % вАФ over PHYSICAL dispositions; **`rebate` EXCLUDED from ALL volume** (and from the mix).
- `pending_count` вАФ 180-day window matching the P1 queue predicate (beer-SKU credit/return_receipt ledger lines awaiting disposition; beer = `ref_skus.recipe_id IS NOT NULL`).

SURFACES (both smoke-passed 200, no fatal):
- Retours-tab panel **"Synth√®se вАФ 90 j"**.
- Mon-tableau KPI tracker **#283** (slug `returns_synthese`, viz `'bar'`, mig **380**, `data_ready=1`, Opus-verified payload; handler `kpi_logi_returns_synthese` in `kpi-handlers.php`).

Live pending backlog = **414 beer-credit lines** (includes rebates to dismiss + real returns to triage). MIG HEAD now **380**. NO tour-steward (panel inside already-toured expeditions; widget isn't a page).

**P2b вАФ BURN-MODEL LATENT BUG (OPEN, low urgency).** The seasonal-burn engine's blanket `вИТSUM(all doc_types)` over-nets beer-credit `rebate`s into velocity (a price-rebate credit is not a physical return-in, so it shouldn't relieve burn). Low urgency; flag when touching `app/seasonal-burn.php`.

**RECONCILIATION GUARD (unchanged, still stands):** the burn engine already nets BC `credit`/`return_receipt` rows into velocity. The `ord_returns` table is the OPERATIONAL/physical-disposition surface; it must NOT double-count against the BC ledger rows вАФ which is exactly why the restock leg is FG-only and the app writes NO revenue/COGS-ledger entry (BC owns that).

**GIT вАФ 4 LOCAL COMMITS NOT PUSHED + 2 FRONTEND FILES DEFERRED-FROM-COMMIT (held for Kouros review + two-session merge):**

- рЯФі **`public/modules/expeditions.php` + `public/css/expeditions.css` are DEFERRED FROM COMMIT** вАФ they carry THIS session's P1 queue + P3 synth√®se-panel changes INTERMINGLED with the CONCURRENT session's repack-helper-hoist + 11-tab-wrap refactor; committing would STEAL parallel work. They are **DEPLOYED + smoke-passed on the VPS (md5 parity)** вАФ **the VPS copy is the frontend source of truth until the two-session merge reconciles them.**
- **PM RECOMMENDATION (STRONG, recorded): do the two-session merge from a SEPARATE WORKTREE.** The SHARED CLONE is the root cause of the churn (orphaned `222cbb9`, the shared-index race, and now this expeditions.php/.css intermingling). Reinforces the standing separate-worktrees + commit-by-pathspec rules.

## вЬЕ PART A/B/C вАФ AS-BUILT 2026-06-16 (ALL THREE BACKENDS SHIPPED + PUSHED + Opus-verified; only UI/KPI WIRING deferred)

**All three backends SHIPPED + PUSHED + Opus-verified 2026-06-16. The SPEC below (retained as the architecture record) was followed; ONE spec deviation noted on Part B.**

- **PART A вАФ burn-rebate over-net fix: `5cd9788`.** `app/seasonal-burn.php` вАФ `NOT EXISTS (disposition='rebate')` guard joined on `bc_document_no + sku`, applied at all **3** netting sites (per spec). LATENT today (0 rebates dispositioned). Byte-identical verified.
- **PART B вАФ returns RATE: `e76e21a`.** Added a `'rate'` key to `returns_synthese()` (EXTENDED the fn per spec, no new fn). Trailing-365d. **Numerator = returned units (rebate EXCLUDED)** √Ј **denominator = gross BC sales `doc_type IN ('shipment','invoice')` beer SKUs.** Per-beer + per-channel (`trade_channel` вЖТ on_trade / off_trade / non class√©). Carries `basis_count` for honesty (so a fake-low rate from un-triaged backlog reads as low-N). Verified sold=222792; 2 unitsвЖТon_trade. **рЯФі SPEC DEVIATION (correct, recorded): `inv_sales_ledger` has NO `sale_class` column** вАФ so the spec's `sale_class='customs_artifact'` exclusion was DROPPED. No such doc_type exists anyway; `inv_sales_ledger.doc_type` values are `shipment / credit / invoice / return_receipt` (NB: NOT `customs_artifact`). The customs-artifact channel-hygiene line in the spec/Part B denominator is **moot вАФ disregard it.** (`sale_class` lives on `ref_customers`, not the ledger; the burn-engine "customs_artifact exclusion" precedent does not transfer to ledger-grain sales queries.)
- **PART C вАФ OVERSELL / ATP-breach: `e80648d` (+ mig 384).** Built per spec Q1-Q4 AS A COMPLETE UNIT вАФ including Q4's snapshot table (spec had flagged Q4 as a separate Kouros-gated follow-on; it was built now, deployed DISABLED, so no scope creep вАФ the cron is inert until the operator enables it).
  - **mig 384 `ops_oversell_snapshot`** вАФ UNIQUE(date, sku) + `schema_meta` (source/allowed classification). MIG HEAD now 384.
  - **`app/oversell.php::oversell_current()`** вАФ READS `fg_stock_compute()` `flag_survendu` (NO parallel calc вАФ the divergence guard honored exactly); attributes shortfall to channel **proportional to open-commitment share**, using fg-stock Step 7's exact open-order gates (`status NOT IN('shipped','cancelled') AND line_status='to_fulfil'`).
  - **`scripts/snapshot-oversell.php`** вАФ idempotent, flock'd.
  - **`db/cron/maltytask-oversell-snapshot.cron`** вАФ DEPLOYED DISABLED.
  - **Opus-verified:** 5 breaches today (111 units short, 98.9% on-trade); oversold set == `flag_survendu` set; channel attribution sums exact; snapshot idempotent.

**CUSTOMER backfill (2026-06-16):** 20 active customers вЖТ `trade_channel='on_trade'`. **рЯФі DELIBERATE NULL: Brasserie du Chien Bleu (id 385) left `trade_channel=NULL` вАФ it is a CONTRACT-BREWING PARTNER, not a sales channel.** ROADMAP FLAG (PM): contract-brewing returns may warrant EXCLUSION from return-rate AND oversell entirely вАФ different dynamics (contract logistics, not event over-booking). NB: P2b burn-rebate guard + the return-RATE numerator both stay latent until rebates start getting dispositioned.

## рЯЖХ PART A/B/C BUILD SPEC вАФ burn-rebate fix ¬Ј returns RATE ¬Ј OVERSELL/ATP tracker (PM architecture read 2026-06-16, Kouros-approved 3-part build; live-probed) вАФ SPEC RETAINED; see AS-BUILT above for what shipped + the Part B sale_class deviation

**LEDGER FACTS (live-verified 2026-06-16, the SoT for all 3 parts):**
- `inv_sales_ledger.doc_type` вИИ {`shipment` (n=31543, qty_signed mostly NEG = depletion), `invoice` (n=6329, mostly NEG), `credit` (n=6619, mostly POS = reversal), `return_receipt` (n=18, mostly POS)}. **shipment & invoice are DISJOINT document populations (0 bc_document_no overlap at sku grain) вАФ burn summing both does NOT double-count.**
- **SALES (depletion) doc_types = `shipment` + `invoice`** (negative qty_signed). **CREDIT/RETURN doc_types = `credit` + `return_receipt`** (positive). `qty_signed` IS the canonical unit basis (signed, SKU units).
- **BC gross-sold units (Part B denominator) = `GREATEST(0, -SUM(qty_signed)) WHERE doc_type IN ('shipment','invoice')`** for the same SKU population. (The burn engine's blanket all-doc_type sum is NET, not gross вАФ for a RATE denominator you want GROSS sales, NOT net-of-returns.)
- **Returns numerator population (canonical, from returns-synthese.php pending_count, lines 100-114):** `doc_type IN ('credit','return_receipt') AND qty_signed>0 AND sku_id_fk IS NOT NULL AND ref_skus.recipe_id IS NOT NULL` (beer-only вАФ same `recipe_id NOT NULL` beer filter the arc already uses). Matches the dispositioned-units population exactly.

**LEDGERвЖФRETURN_LINE LINKAGE (canonical, no cleaner key exists):** `ord_returns.origin_bc_document_no = inv_sales_ledger.bc_document_no` AND `ord_return_lines.sku_id_fk = inv_sales_ledger.sku_id_fk`. There is NO direct ledger-row FK on ord_return_lines (it carries `origin_ledger_sku_code` VARCHAR for display only, NOT an id FK). `ord_returns` DOES carry `origin_order_id_fk`/`origin_sales_order_id_fk` but those point at ord_orders/inv_sales_orders, NOT the ledger. **So bc_document_no + sku_id_fk IS the right and only join key** вАФ it is exactly what returns-synthese.php pending_count already uses (precedent set). Confirm dispatch agent reuses that idiom, doesn't invent a new join.

**CUSTOMER-TYPE CLASSIFICATION (the B3/C2 "don't guess" answer вАФ DECISIVE):**
- `ref_customers.trade_channel` ENUM('on_trade','off_trade') вАФ **THIS is the canonical event/on-premise vs retail field. on_trade = bars/restos/clubs/theatres/events (HoReCa); off_trade = retail/supermarkets (Manor/Coop/Aligro).** Verified by customer-name sampling.
- **BUT only ~23% populated overall (622 on_trade + 64 off_trade + 2375 NULL of 3061).** On the OPEN-ORDER book it's better: 53 on_trade + 6 off_trade + 17 NULL + 1 giveaway of 77.
- `ref_customers.sale_class` ENUM has an `'event'` value BUT it is **NOT meaningfully populated вАФ 3055 of 3061 customers are 'b2b'**, 1 each of the rest. **sale_class does NOT distinguish event vs retail. DO NOT use it for the customer-type cut.** (It IS valid for the existing `customs_artifact` exclusion only.)
- **RULING: the customer-type cut = `ref_customers.trade_channel` (on_trade vs off_trade), with a 3rd explicit `NULL/inconnu` bucket вАФ NEVER fold NULL into either side, NEVER derive channel from sale_class or guess from name.** eshop is mixed INTO on_trade (e.g. "La N√©buleuse - ESHOP (priv√©)") so trade_channel вЙ† a clean eshop discriminator; eshop/taproom are their own depletion legs (inv_sales_orders / inv_sales_bc), not B2B orders. **KOUROS-DECISION NEEDED: is the on_tradeвЙИevent proxy good enough, or should we (i) backfill trade_channel as part of the recurring BCвЖТref_customers sync, or (ii) add a finer segment column? SURFACE вАФ do not let Sonnet guess.** Until then, present the cut as "on-premise (on-trade) / retail (off-trade) / non class√©" with the NULL count visible so the operator sees coverage.

**PART A вАФ burn over-net rebate fix (`app/seasonal-burn.php`):**
- **3 netting sites, not 2:** `sb_family_weekly_series` (~L108-120), `sb_all_sku_levels` window query (~L434-450), AND its **lifetime-stats query (~L455-465)** also nets all doc_types (first_sale/last_sale/lived_full_summer). The lifetime query doesn't sum qty so a rebate row only affects first/last-sale dates marginally вАФ but apply the SAME exclusion to all 3 for consistency.
- **FIX SHAPE (confirmed):** add to each `WHERE` a `NOT EXISTS` correlated subquery excluding ledger rows that are credit/return AND dispositioned 'rebate': `AND NOT EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM ord_returns r JOIN ord_return_lines rl ON rl.return_id_fk=r.id WHERE r.origin_bc_document_no = l.bc_document_no AND rl.sku_id_fk = l.sku_id_fk AND rl.disposition='rebate')`. (bc_document_no+sku join вАФ same key as everywhere.) Only credit/return rows can match a return_line so no need to also gate doc_type inside the subquery, but adding `AND l.doc_type IN ('credit','return_receipt')` to the NOT-EXISTS guard makes intent explicit and keeps the planner honest.
- **RISK TO `6228e8a` / cron: ZERO.** The seasonal-index cron (`/etc/cron.d/maltytask-seasonal-index`, currently DISABLED) only writes `kpi_sku_seasonal_index` (the seasonal SHAPE per recipe√Чiso_week). It reads the same series; excluding rebate lines only sharpens the depletion signal. No schema change, no cron change. The forward sim consumes the level вАФ a slightly higher (less-netted-down) burn = slightly more conservative runway = the intended correction.
- **MAGNITUDE / URGENCY (live): currently ZERO rebate lines dispositioned, and only 1 return line total (the Albaladejo restock=2). The leak is LATENT вАФ it bites once the operator starts dispositioning the 3405-line beer-credit backlog as 'rebate'.** So Part A is correct to fix but is not yet distorting anything. Low urgency; ship with B/C.
- **EQUIP: sql + coder + webapp-testing** (read-only ?view=stock smoke; verify burn numbers unchanged today since 0 rebates, and that a synthetic rebate row drops out of the series).

**PART B вАФ returns RATE (board-spec: returned √Ј BC gross-sold, same SKU pop, trailing-12mo, per-beer + per-customer-type, disposition MIX still leads, CHF in finance view only):**
- **DECISION: EXTEND `returns_synthese()` with a `rate` block, do NOT create a separate fn.** Single-source the returns aggregates (the file's stated purpose, lines 4-6). But the rate block runs on a DIFFERENT window (12mo) than the mix (90d) вАФ so the fn signature grows a 2nd param OR computes both windows internally. **Cleanest: keep `$periodDays` for mix/by_client/by_beer (90d default) AND add the rate block on a hardcoded trailing-365d window internally** (mirrors how pending_count already pins its own 180d window regardless of $periodDays вАФ same precedent, lines 97-99). So: mix=90d, rate=12mo, both in one fn, each documenting its window. **Do NOT unify the windows** вАФ they answer different questions (operational recency vs annualized rate) and the board asked for 12mo rate explicitly.
- **Numerator (12mo):** dispositioned returned units `restock+scrap+quarantine` (rebate EXCLUDED вАФ it's non-physical) over trailing 365d, per beer (`ref_recipes.name` via `ref_skus.recipe_id`) and per customer-type (`trade_channel`). **CAVEAT: only 1 line dispositioned today вЖТ the rate is ~0 until the backlog is triaged. The rate is only meaningful once dispositioning catches up.** Surface that honestly (e.g. "bas√© sur N retours trait√©s" + the pending backlog count) so the operator doesn't read a fake-low rate.
- **Denominator (12mo, MUST match numerator population):** `GREATEST(0,-SUM(qty_signed)) WHERE doc_type IN ('shipment','invoice') AND sku_id_fk IS NOT NULL AND ref_skus.recipe_id IS NOT NULL`, same trailing-365d, grouped per beer and per trade_channel. GROSS sales (not net). Exclude `sale_class='customs_artifact'` to match the burn-engine channel hygiene.
- **per-customer-type:** group both num and denom by `ref_customers.trade_channel` resolved via `inv_sales_ledger.customer_id_fk` (returns side: via the bc_document_noвЖТledgerвЖТcustomer hop already in by_client). 3 buckets: on_trade / off_trade / NULL(non class√©). Show coverage.
- **CHF / contra-revenue: NOT in returns_synthese() вАФ finance view only.** Do not blend CHF into the volume/rate panel. (BC owns revenue; the avoir already reverses it. Any CHF view reads BC, not this fn.)
- **KOUROS-DECISION: the 90d-mix vs 12mo-rate dual window on KPI #283 / the Retours panel** вАФ confirm he wants BOTH shown (mix headline 90d + rate 12mo sub-block) vs unifying. PM rec = keep both (matches his memo: "disposition MIX still leading" + "rate trailing-12mo").
- **EQUIP: sql + coder + ui + webapp-testing.**

**PART C вАФ OVERSELL / ATP-breach tracking (the big one):**
- **Q1 вАФ `flag_survendu` ALREADY == an ATP breach.** Exact def `app/fg-stock.php` L955: `'flag_survendu' => $liveFutur < 0` where `live_futur = physique вИТ open_total_qty` (L905/947). `physique` = anchor + prod(historical, since-anchor) вИТ expedie вИТ eshop вИТ taproom + repack + restock (on-hand FG). `open_total_qty` = `SUM(ord_order_lines.qty) JOIN ord_orders WHERE status NOT IN('shipped','cancelled') AND line_status='to_fulfil'` (Step 7, L702-712). **So flag_survendu = "committed open orders exceed on-hand FG" = ATP breach WITHOUT a scheduled-production term.** The board's ATP = on-hand + scheduled-production вИТ committed; the current flag is the STRICTER on-handвИТcommitted (no future-prod credit). There is NO scheduled/future-production input in fg_stock_compute today (prod is historical-since-anchor only, already in physique). **So we do NOT build a parallel oversell calc вАФ flag_survendu IS it.** Magnitude = `-live_futur` (units short) when negative; attribution comes from the open_book per-SKU (Step 7 `$openBookBySku`, has per-order date/qty/status вАФ extend to carry customer trade_channel).
- **Q2 вАФ attribute oversell to EVENTS:** open orders ARE classifiable вАФ `ord_orders.customer_id_fk вЖТ ref_customers.trade_channel`. Same answer as B3: `trade_channel` on_tradeвЙИevent/on-premise, off_trade=retail, NULL=non class√©. On the open book it's 53/6/17/1 of 77 вАФ usable but with a NULL bucket. **Same KOUROS-DECISION as B3 (is on_tradeвЙИevent good enough / backfill / finer column). Do NOT guess.** `ord_orders.internal_channel` (taproom/eshop/cage/shop) is only for `order_type='internal'` вАФ all 77 open orders are `order_type='customer'` so internal_channel is NULL throughout; not the discriminator.
- **Q3 вАФ WHERE oversell lives (cleanest, reusable):** **(a) a new KPI tracker reading the EXISTING `fg_stock_compute()` output (like #283) вАФ YES, primary.** The engine already emits per-SKU `flag_survendu`, `live_futur`, `open_total_qty`, `couverture.open_book`. A new handler `kpi_logi_oversell` (or similar) calls `fg_stock_compute()`, counts `flag_survendu` SKUs, sums `-live_futur` (units short), and buckets the open_book by trade_channel. NO new compute path. **(b) a panel on the existing Couverture drilldown вАФ secondary, cheap (the data is already in the couverture payload).** **Build (a) the KPI tracker as the headline; optionally surface the per-SKU short list on the Couverture face.** Do NOT add a 2nd derivation вАФ read fg_stock_compute, period.
- **Q4 вАФ HISTORICAL capture: NONE EXISTS. The engine is a pure current/forward snapshot.** `kpi_sku_seasonal_index` stores only the seasonal multiplier (recipe√Чiso_week√Чindex), NOT any survendu/ATP outcome over time. There is NO table recording past oversell incidents. **To track "how often we oversold in high season" you MUST start snapshotting вАФ that is a NEW, SEPARATE concern (a daily/weekly `ops_oversell_snapshot`-type table: date, sku_id_fk, live_futur, units_short, on_trade_short, off_trade_short).** A flock'd daily PHP cron calling fg_stock_compute() and persisting the negative-ATP rows (clone the credential-expiry / seasonal-index cron pattern, deployed DISABLED). **THIS IS A KOUROS SCOPE DECISION: the live tracker (Q3a) ships now off existing output; the time-series (snapshotting for "frequency in high season") is a distinct follow-on build вАФ confirm he wants it in this arc or as a separate one.** PM rec: ship the live tracker now; propose the snapshot table as a fast-follow once he confirms he wants the historical frequency metric.
- **DIVERGENCE GUARD: there is exactly ONE FG/ATP derivation (`fg_stock_compute`). Any oversell tracker/panel/snapshot MUST read it вАФ never recompute open-orders-vs-stock independently (that's the parallel-store anti-pattern).** The Step-7 open-order filter (`status NOT IN('shipped','cancelled') AND line_status='to_fulfil'`) is the canonical "committed" definition вАФ reuse it, don't redefine.
- **EQUIP: sql + coder + ui + webapp-testing** (+ a separate sql+coder dispatch for the snapshot table/cron IF Kouros greenlights Q4).

## рЯУЛ DEFERRED BACKLOG вАФ operator-confirmed-WANTED, not abandoned (confirmed 2026-06-16; pick up later)

**[BL-FULF-1] eshop bundle decomposition вАФ "2√Ч" quantity-multiplier edge + the 100%-off promo line.** The variant-bridge (`ref_sku_shopify_variants`) models **1 Shopify variant вЖТ 1 SKU**; it does NOT model (a) a quantity multiplier (e.g. "2√Ч Pack de No√Ђl" = one line, qty-mult 2) nor (b) a 100%-off promo/gift line that carries NO variant. Both surface in the **visible unresolved tail** (refuse-don't-NULL holds вАФ nothing silently mis-decomposes), so this is a COMPLETENESS gap, not a correctness hazard. **LOW volume.** Architecture verdict: extends the existing variant-bridge + the bundleвЖТ(recipe,container) decomposition already shipped in this arc вАФ no new table, no parallel store; a qty-mult column on the bridge resolution + a promo/zero-price line classifier. Belongs squarely in the Shopify-fulfilment decomposition lane. Gate: none hard вАФ pick up when the unresolved tail accumulates enough of these to matter. EQUIP sql+coder(+ui if the tail surface changes).

**[BL-FULF-2] C3 вАФ operator self-service variant-mapping UI.** Today an unknown Shopify variant lands in the **visible tail** and gets seeded into `ref_sku_shopify_variants` **manually** (direct SQL). A small admin UI (list unmapped variants вЖТ pick a `ref_skus` row вЖТ write the bridge row) closes the loop without an SQL round-trip. **Convenience, not blocking** вАФ the manual seed path works and the tail keeps it honest. Architecture verdict: pure CRUD over `ref_sku_shopify_variants` with a `ref_skus` whitelist (refuse-don't-NULL вАФ no free-text SKU); add a `ref_pages` row + preset grant + RULE-3 tour card on ship. Gate: none; ship when variant volume makes manual seeding annoying. EQUIP sql+coder+ui+webapp-testing.

**рЯФС DURABLE KEY FINDING (re-stated as confirmed):** same-day customer+SKU booking reversals are an **ONGOING BC workflow** (BC posts shipment вЖТ credits it вЖТ re-invoices), **~72% of raw beer "returns"**, sourced from the recurring "√Йcritures comptables article.xlsx" export. `doc_type_raw` cannot distinguish them. **RE-1 follow-on:** add `is_reversal`/`reversed_doc_no` flag at BC-API ingest (deterministic pairing), then flip the view body `NOT EXISTS`-on-same-day вЖТ `is_reversal=0`, ZERO consumer change. ## рЯФі ¬ІRETURNS REVERSAL POLLUTION FIX вАФ ORIGINAL PM SPEC 2026-06-16 (retained for the rationale; build LANDED above)

**FINDING (verified live, 365d, beer SKUs `rs.recipe_id IS NOT NULL`).** The returns RATE block (`returns-synthese.php` `e76e21a`), the over-ship watchlist, the synth√®se `pending_count`, AND the P1 disposition queue in `expeditions.php` count GROSS `credit`/`return_receipt` ledger lines as physical returns. **72.5% are SAME-DAY BOOKING REVERSALS** вАФ a credit posted same day as a shipment/invoice to the same customer for the same SKU (BC posts shipment(вИТN) вЖТ credits it(+N) вЖТ re-invoices).
- GROSS returns 365d = **14 712 units / 800 lines**; SAME-DAY reversals = **10 662 units / 468 lines** (72.5%).
- FWT Management: 926 gross "returns" = **926 same-day reversals**, ~9 real.
- CORRECTED overall rate = **1.82%** (real 4 050 / sold 222 792) vs polluted 6.6%.
- **Reversals are an ONGOING BC workflow** вАФ same-day-reversal lines spread continuously across EVERY posting month 2025-06вЖТ2026-06 (10вАУ80/mo). The `imported_at` clustering on 2026-06-10 is just the bulk historical-load date; posting_date distribution is what matters and it's continuous. вЗТ a read-time filter is durable AND every future BC pull stays clean *as long as consumers go through the canonical accessor*.

**рЯФі `bc_source_no` does NOT work as the reversal key** (corrects the finding's premise). On these rows `bc_source_no` holds a CUSTOMER/source number (3660, 2161, 1293вА¶), NOT the reversed sales-doc number; 0 credits join to a shipment `bc_document_no` via it. The reliable signal is the same-day cust+sku+opposing-sign match. Do NOT build the filter on `bc_source_no` вАФ it would match nothing and exclude zero reversals.

**PM RULINGS (the 5 questions):**
1. **Canonical home = SQL VIEW `v_physical_returns`**, NOT a PHP-helper-returning-a-predicate-string. The predicate is needed in raw SQL across 6+ sites with different aliases (`l.`/`cr.`/`l2.`); a view is the callable canonical accessor for SQL consumers ([call-the-accessor-not-copy] rule). `maltytask_app` HAS `CREATE VIEW`/`SHOW VIEW` (granted 2026-05-26). The view bakes in BOTH the reversal-exclusion AND the existing rebate `disposition='rebate'` NOT-EXISTS, subsuming the current copy-paste of the rebate predicate across ~5 synthese sites + 2 expeditions sites = RULE-1 scrap win. +`schema_meta` row (derived_view, read-only). Optionally a sibling `v_sold_beer_units` for the denominator (symmetry; low cost). Reversal predicate (verified 4050 kept / 10662 excluded):
   ```sql
   AND NOT EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM inv_sales_ledger sh
     WHERE sh.doc_type IN ('shipment','invoice')
       AND sh.posting_date=l.posting_date AND sh.customer_id_fk=l.customer_id_fk
       AND sh.sku_id_fk=l.sku_id_fk AND sh.qty_signed<0)
   ```
2. **Read-time VIEW now (durable) + ingest-flag in RE-1 (follow-on).** Now: the view IS the durable fix вАФ fast (composite idx `(posting_date,customer_id_fk,sku_id_fk,doc_type)`, EXPLAIN-verify), safe, zero-backfill, self-sustaining. RE-1 (BC API auto-pull): add `inv_sales_ledger.is_reversal TINYINT` + `reversed_doc_no VARCHAR`, stamp at load (ingest has both rows of a doc in hand вЖТ deterministic pairing, better than the same-day heuristic). At that point the view body flips `NOT EXISTS`вЖТ`WHERE is_reversal=0` and NO consumer changes вАФ that's the payoff of the view. Record as RE-1 follow-on; don't block today's fix.
3. **BURN/`flag_survendu` SAFE вАФ leave alone, do NOT route through the view.** `seasonal-burn.php` L108вАУ126 `GREATEST(0,-SUM(qty_signed))` nets a same-day вИТN/+N pair to 0 (self-correcting). Burn wants NET physical depletion (legitimately includes real returns adding stock back); the view is a GROSS physical-return lens вАФ different question, must not be unified (same rationale as the code's existing divergence-from-`v_sales_ledger_order_lines` comment). `fg_stock_compute` reads NO return doc_types вЖТ safe alone. **BUT the P1 disposition POST resolver (`expeditions.php` ~L1532) is the REAL hazard**: a reversal sits in the queue today; if an operator dispositions it `restock`, Leg 4 adds phantom kegs to physique that were never returned вЖТ real FG corruption. вЗТ the canonical filter MUST reach L1532 (the POST that feeds Leg 4), not only the L2599 render. This upgrades the queue fix from cosmetic to load-bearing.
4. **DUP sale-doc вАФ NOT applicable to the beer rate; drop from this build.** The "436 groups / 8 060 units" is almost entirely NULL-`sku_id_fk` / non-beer rows, already excluded by `rs.recipe_id IS NOT NULL`. Beer-only excess = **20 groups / ~43 units**, and those are NOT clones (distinct `bc_line_seq` + distinct `sales_amount_chf`, e.g. a chf=0 pick line + a chf=97.80 priced line under one EXPED doc) = legitimate BC multi-line structure. A read `DISTINCT` would FALSE-REJECT real lines (the `inv_deliveries` coarse-UNIQUE lesson). Do NOT dedup. 43u on a 222 792 base = rounding error.
5. **No pre-existing returns view to extend.** `returns_synthese()` is the only aggregation home; the rebate NOT-EXISTS is copy-pasted across ~5 synthese sites + 2 expeditions queue sites вАФ the view subsumes that duplication.

**BUILD SPEC.** Migration (next free; re-`migrate.php --status`): (1) `CREATE VIEW v_physical_returns` (beer credit/return_receipt, qty_signed>0, recipe_id NOT NULL, sku_id_fk NOT NULL, minus same-day-reversal NOT-EXISTS, minus rebate-disposition NOT-EXISTS; expose id/posting_date/bc_document_no/customer_id_fk/sku_id_fk/qty_signed/recipe_id); (2) composite idx above (INPLACE; no IF NOT EXISTS on the ALTER); (3) schema_meta row(s). Code: `returns-synthese.php` repoint rate numerator + per-beer-num + per-channel-num + overship returned_units + the `pending_count` ledger-side query (L103) at the view (remove now-redundant inline rebate NOT-EXISTS; denominators stay base-table shipment/invoice). `expeditions.php` route ALL three ledger-return sites through the view вАФ P1 queue render (~L2599), **P1 disposition POST resolver (~L1532, critical)**, processed list (~L2649). `seasonal-burn.php`/`fg_stock_compute` NO CHANGE (+1-line comment noting reversals intentionally retained in net-depletion, excluded only from the gross-return lens).

**VERIFY (Opus independently вАФ COGS/FG-adjacent, don't trust agent gate-PASS):** view unit-sum == 4 050 real / overall rate 1.82% (4050/222792); 10 662 fewer than gross; FWT through view ~9 (not 926); P1 queue count ~413вЖТ~110вАУ130; burn `sb_forward_sim` byte-identical before/after on a sample recipe; POST resolver REFUSES a synthetic reversal line (un-restockable); idempotent re-run; `php -l` clean; md5 localвЖФVPS each deployed file; `?view=retours` 200 + synth√®se panel renders corrected rate.
